`context.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { auth, type AuthSession, type AuthUser } from "@clinic/auth";
   2 | import type { UserRole } from "@clinic/auth/permissions";
   3 | import { db } from "@clinic/db";
   4 | 
   5 | export type AuthContext = {
   6 | 	headers: Headers;
   7 | 	db: typeof db;
   8 | 	auth: typeof auth;
   9 | 	session: AuthSession | null;
  10 | 	user: AuthUser | null;
  11 | 	clinicId: string | null;
  12 | 	isAuthorized: (requiredRole: UserRole) => boolean;
  13 | };
  14 | 
  15 | export async function createContext(opts: { req: Request }): Promise<AuthContext> {
  16 | 	const headers = opts.req.headers;
  17 |   const session = await auth.api.getSession({
  18 |     headers: opts.req.headers,
  19 |   });
  20 | 	const user = session?.user ?? null;
  21 | 	const clinicId = user?.clinicId ?? null;
  22 | 
  23 | 	const isAuthorized = (requiredRole: UserRole) => user?.role === "admin" || user?.role === requiredRole;
  24 | 
  25 | 
  26 | 
  27 |   return {
  28 | 	headers,
  29 | 		db,
  30 | 		auth,
  31 | 		session,
  32 | 		user,
  33 | 		clinicId,
  34 |     isAuthorized,
  35 |   };
  36 | }
  37 | 
  38 | export type Context = Awaited<ReturnType<typeof createContext>>;

```

```ts
 234 | type ResourceName = keyof typeof resourceConfigs;
 235 | type ResourceConfigType<T extends ResourceName> = (typeof resourceConfigs)[T];
 236 | 
 237 | // ============================================================================
 238 | // Helper Functions - Type-safe implementations
 239 | // ============================================================================
 240 | 
 241 | /**
 242 |  * Safely gets a column from a table with type checking
 243 |  */
 244 | function getTableColumn(table: PgTable, columnName: string): GenericColumn | undefined {
 245 | 	const columns = table as unknown as Record<string, PgColumn>;
 246 | 	return columns[columnName] as GenericColumn | undefined;
 247 | }
 248 | 
 249 | /**
 250 |  * Builds WHERE conditions from filter parameters
 251 |  */
 252 | function buildWhereConditions(config: ResourceConfigType<ResourceName>, filter: FilterParams): SQL[] {
 253 | 	const conditions: SQL[] = [];
 254 | 
 255 | 	if (!filter || Object.keys(filter).length === 0) {
 256 | 		return conditions;
 257 | 	}
 258 | 
 259 | 	// Handle search (q parameter) across searchable fields
 260 | 	if (filter.q && config.searchFields?.length) {
 261 | 		const searchConditions = config.searchFields
 262 | 			.map(field => {
 263 | 				const column = getTableColumn(config.table, field as string);
 264 | 				return column ? ilike(column, `%${filter.q}%`) : null;
 265 | 			})
 266 | 			.filter((condition): condition is SQL => condition !== null);
 267 | 
 268 | 		if (searchConditions.length > 0) {
 269 | 			conditions.push(or(...searchConditions));
 270 | 		}
 271 | 	}
 272 | 
 273 | 	// Handle exact match filters on specified filter fields
 274 | 	if (config.filterFields) {
 275 | 		for (const field of config.filterFields) {
 276 | 			const fieldName = field as string;
 277 | 			const value = filter[fieldName];
 278 | 
 279 | 			if (value !== undefined && value !== null && value !== "") {
 280 | 				const column = getTableColumn(config.table, fieldName);
 281 | 				if (column) {
 282 | 					conditions.push(eq(column, value as ColumnValue));
 283 | 				}
 284 | 			}
 285 | 		}
 286 | 	}
 287 | 
 288 | 	// Handle common filter fields dynamically
 289 | 	const commonFilters = ["status", "type", "doctorId", "patientId", "clinicId", "gender"];
 290 | 	for (const field of commonFilters) {
 291 | 		const value = filter[field];
 292 | 		if (value !== undefined && value !== null && value !== "") {
 293 | 			const column = getTableColumn(config.table, field);
 294 | 			if (column) {
 295 | 				conditions.push(eq(column, value as ColumnValue));
 296 | 			}
 297 | 		}
 298 | 	}
 299 | 
 300 | 	// Handle boolean isActive filter
 301 | 	if (filter.isActive !== undefined) {
 302 | 		const column = getTableColumn(config.table, "isActive");
 303 | 		if (column) {
 304 | 			const boolValue = filter.isActive === "true" || filter.isActive === true;
 305 | 			conditions.push(eq(column, boolValue));
 306 | 		}
 307 | 	}
 308 | 
 309 | 	// Handle date range filter
 310 | 	if (filter.dateRange?.start && filter.dateRange?.end) {
 311 | 		const createdAtColumn = getTableColumn(config.table, "createdAt");
 312 | 		if (createdAtColumn) {
 313 | 			conditions.push(
 314 | 				sql`${createdAtColumn} >= ${filter.dateRange.start} AND ${createdAtColumn} <= ${filter.dateRange.end}`
 315 | 			);
 316 | 		}
 317 | 	}
 318 | 
 319 | 	return conditions;
 320 | }
 321 | 
 322 | /**
 323 |  * Builds ORDER BY clause from sort parameters
 324 |  */
 325 | function buildOrderBy(config: ResourceConfigType<ResourceName>, sort: SortParams): SQL {
 326 | 	const sortField = sort?.field;
 327 | 	const sortOrder = sort?.order || "DESC";
 328 | 
 329 | 	// Try to use the requested sort field
 330 | 	if (sortField && config.sortableFields && (config.sortableFields as Record<string, GenericColumn>)[sortField]) {
 331 | 		const field = (config.sortableFields as Record<string, GenericColumn>)[sortField];
 332 | 		if (field) {
 333 | 			return sortOrder === "ASC" ? asc(field) : desc(field);
 334 | 		}
 335 | 	}
 336 | 
 337 | 	// Fall back to default sort
 338 | 	if (config.defaultSort && (config.sortableFields as Record<string, GenericColumn>)?.[config.defaultSort.field]) {
 339 | 		const field = config.sortableFields[config.defaultSort.field];
 340 | 		if (field) {
 341 | 			return config.defaultSort.order === "ASC" ? asc(field) : desc(field);
 342 | 		}
 343 | 	}
 344 | 
 345 | 	// Ultimate fallback: use createdAt column if it exists
 346 | 	const createdAtColumn = getTableColumn(config.table, "createdAt");
 347 | 	if (createdAtColumn) {
 348 | 		return desc(createdAtColumn);
 349 | 	}
 350 | 
 351 | 	// Last resort: use the first column in the table
 352 | 	const columns = config.table as unknown as Record<string, PgColumn>;
 353 | 	const firstColumn = Object.values(columns)[0];
 354 | 	return firstColumn ? desc(firstColumn) : sql`1`;
 355 | }

 357 | // ============================================================================
 358 | // Data Provider Implementation - Fully typed
 359 | // ============================================================================
 360 | 
 361 | export const drizzleDataProvider: DataProvider = {
 362 | 	async getList<RecordType extends { id: string | number }>(
 363 | 		resource: string,
 364 | 		params: FilterParams
 365 | 	): Promise<GetListResult<RecordType>> {
 366 | 		const config = resourceConfigs[resource as ResourceName];
 367 | 		if (!config) {
 368 | 			throw new Error(`Unknown resource: ${resource}`);
 369 | 		}
 370 | 
 371 | 		const { pagination, sort, ...filter } = params;
 372 | 		const { page = 1, perPage = 10 } = (pagination as PaginationParams) || {};
 373 | 		const offset = (page - 1) * perPage;
 374 | 
 375 | 		// Build and execute main query
 376 | 		let query = db.select().from(config.table).$dynamic();
 377 | 		const conditions = buildWhereConditions(config, filter);
 378 | 
 379 | 		if (conditions && conditions.length > 0) {
 380 | 			query = query.where(and(...conditions));
 381 | 		}
 382 | 
 383 | 		const orderBy = buildOrderBy(config, sort as SortParams);
 384 | 		query = query.orderBy(orderBy).limit(perPage).offset(offset);
 385 | 
 386 | 		let data = await query;
 387 | 
 388 | 		// Get total count
 389 | 		let countQuery = db.select({ count: count() }).from(config.table).$dynamic();
 390 | 		if (conditions && conditions.length > 0) {
 391 | 			countQuery = countQuery.where(and(...conditions));
 392 | 		}
 393 | 		const totalResult = await countQuery;
 394 | 		const total = Number(totalResult[0]?.count ?? 0);
 395 | 
 396 | 		// Apply transformations
 397 | 		const transform = config.transformGet;
 398 | 		if (transform) {
 399 | 			// biome-ignore lint/suspicious/noExplicitAny: Record types from database are complex unions
 400 | 			data = data.map(record => transform(record as any));
 401 | 		}
 402 | 
 403 | 		return { data: data as unknown as RecordType[], total };
 404 | 	},
 405 | 
 406 | 	async getOne<RecordType extends { id: string | number }>(
 407 | 		resource: string,
 408 | 		params: { id: string | number }
 409 | 	): Promise<GetOneResult<RecordType>> {
 410 | 		const config = resourceConfigs[resource as ResourceName];
 411 | 		if (!config) {
 412 | 			throw new Error(`Unknown resource: ${resource}`);
 413 | 		}
 414 | 
 415 | 		const { id } = params;
 416 | 		const primaryKey = config.primaryKey as string;
 417 | 		const column = getTableColumn(config.table, primaryKey);
 418 | 
 419 | 		if (!column) {
 420 | 			throw new Error(`Primary key column '${primaryKey}' not found`);
 421 | 		}
 422 | 
 423 | 		const result = await db.select().from(config.table).where(eq(column, id));
 424 | 
 425 | 		if (!result[0]) {
 426 | 			throw new Error(`Record not found: ${id}`);
 427 | 		}
 428 | 
 429 | 		// biome-ignore lint/suspicious/noExplicitAny: Generic transform requires loose cast
 430 | 		const record = config.transformGet ? config.transformGet(result[0] as any) : result[0];
 431 | 		return { data: record as unknown as RecordType };
 432 | 	},
 433 | 
 434 | 	async getMany<RecordType extends { id: string | number }>(
 435 | 		resource: string,
 436 | 		params: { ids: (string | number)[] }
 437 | 	): Promise<GetManyResult<RecordType>> {
 438 | 		const config = resourceConfigs[resource as ResourceName];
 439 | 		if (!config) {
 440 | 			throw new Error(`Unknown resource: ${resource}`);
 441 | 		}
 442 | 
 443 | 		const { ids } = params;
 444 | 		const primaryKey = config.primaryKey as string;
 445 | 		const column = getTableColumn(config.table, primaryKey);
 446 | 
 447 | 		if (!column) {
 448 | 			throw new Error(`Primary key column '${primaryKey}' not found`);
 449 | 		}
 450 | 
 451 | 		const results = await db
 452 | 			.select()
 453 | 			.from(config.table)
 454 | 			.where(inArray(column, ids as string[]));
 455 | 
 456 | 		const data = config.transformGet ? results.map(r => config.transformGet(r)) : results;
 457 | 		return { data: data as unknown as RecordType[] };
 458 | 	},
 459 | 
 460 | 	async getManyReference<RecordType extends { id: string | number }>(
 461 | 		resource: string,
 462 | 		params: any
 463 | 	): Promise<GetManyResult<RecordType> & { total: number }> {
 464 | 		const config = resourceConfigs[resource as ResourceName];
 465 | 		if (!config) {
 466 | 			throw new Error(`Unknown resource: ${resource}`);
 467 | 		}
 468 | 
 469 | 		const { target, id, pagination, sort } = params;
 470 | 		const { page = 1, perPage = 10 } = (pagination as PaginationParams) || {};
 471 | 		const offset = (page - 1) * perPage;
 472 | 
 473 | 		const targetColumn = getTableColumn(config.table, target);
 474 | 
 475 | 		if (!targetColumn) {
 476 | 			throw new Error(`Target column '${target}' not found`);
 477 | 		}
 478 | 
 479 | 		let query = db.select().from(config.table).where(eq(targetColumn, id)).$dynamic();
 480 | 
 481 | 		const orderBy = buildOrderBy(config, sort as SortParams);
 482 | 		query = query.orderBy(orderBy).limit(perPage).offset(offset);
 483 | 
 484 | 		let data = await query;
 485 | 
 486 | 		// Get total count
 487 | 		const countResult = await db.select({ count: count() }).from(config.table).where(eq(targetColumn, id));
 488 | 		const total = Number(countResult[0]?.count ?? 0);
 489 | 
 490 | 		const transform = config.transformGet;
 491 | 		if (transform) {
 492 | 			// biome-ignore lint/suspicious/noExplicitAny: Data mapping
 493 | 			data = data.map(record => transform(record as any));
 494 | 		}
 495 | 
 496 | 		return { data: data as unknown as RecordType[], total };
 497 | 	},
 498 | 
 499 | 	async create<RecordType extends { id: string | number }>(
 500 | 		resource: string,
 501 | 		params: { data:  }
 502 | 	): Promise<CreateResult<RecordType>> {
 503 | 		const config = resourceConfigs[resource as ResourceName];
 504 | 		if (!config) {
 505 | 			throw new Error(`Unknown resource: ${resource}`);
 506 | 		}
 507 | 
 508 | 		let { data } = params;
 509 | 
 510 | 		if (config.transformCreate) {
 511 | 			data = config.transformCreate(data);
 512 | 		}
 513 | 
 514 | 		const result = await db.insert(config.table).values(data).returning();
 515 | 
 516 | 		if (!result[0]) {
 517 | 			throw new Error(`Failed to create record in ${resource}`);
 518 | 		}
 519 | 
 520 | 		// biome-ignore lint/suspicious/noExplicitAny: Cast for generic result
 521 | 		const record = config.transformGet ? config.transformGet(result[0] as any) : result[0];
 522 | 		return { data: record as unknown as RecordType };
 523 | 	},
 524 | 
 525 | 	async update<RecordType extends { id: string | number }>(
 526 | 		resource: string,
 527 | 		params: { id: string | number; data: Record<string, unknown> }
 528 | 	): Promise<UpdateResult<RecordType>> {
 529 | 		const config = resourceConfigs[resource as ResourceName];
 530 | 		if (!config) {
 531 | 			throw new Error(`Unknown resource: ${resource}`);
 532 | 		}
 533 | 
 534 | 		let { id, data } = params;
 535 | 
 536 | 		if (config.transformUpdate) {
 537 | 			data = config.transformUpdate(data);
 538 | 		}
 539 | 
 540 | 		const primaryKey = config.primaryKey as string;
 541 | 		const column = getTableColumn(config.table, primaryKey);
 542 | 
 543 | 		if (!column) {
 544 | 			throw new Error(`Primary key column '${primaryKey}' not found`);
 545 | 		}
 546 | 
 547 | 		const result = await db.update(config.table).set(data).where(eq(column, id)).returning();
 548 | 
 549 | 		if (!result[0]) {
 550 | 			throw new Error(`Record not found: ${id}`);
 551 | 		}
 552 | 
 553 | 		// biome-ignore lint/suspicious/noExplicitAny: Generic cast
 554 | 		const record = config.transformGet ? config.transformGet(result[0] as any) : result[0];
 555 | 		return { data: record as unknown as RecordType };
 556 | 	},
 557 | 
 558 | 	async updateMany(
 559 | 		resource: string,
 560 | 		params: { ids: (string | number)[]; data: Record<string, unknown> }
 561 | 	): Promise<{ data: (string | number)[] }> {
 562 | 		const config = resourceConfigs[resource as ResourceName];
 563 | 		if (!config) {
 564 | 			throw new Error(`Unknown resource: ${resource}`);
 565 | 		}
 566 | 
 567 | 		const { ids, data } = params;
 568 | 		const primaryKey = config.primaryKey as string;
 569 | 		const column = getTableColumn(config.table, primaryKey);
 570 | 
 571 | 		if (!column) {
 572 | 			throw new Error(`Primary key column '${primaryKey}' not found`);
 573 | 		}
 574 | 
 575 | 		const results: string[] = [];
 576 | 
 577 | 		for (const id of ids as string[]) {
 578 | 			const updateData = config.transformUpdate ? config.transformUpdate(data) : data;
 579 | 			const result = await db
 580 | 				.update(config.table)
 581 | 				.set(updateData)
 582 | 				.where(eq(column, id))
 583 | 				.returning();
 584 | 
 585 | 			if (result[0]) {
 586 | 				results.push((result[0] as { id: string }).id);
 587 | 			}
 588 | 		}
 589 | 
 590 | 		return { data: results };
 591 | 	},
 592 | 
 593 | 	async delete<RecordType extends { id: string | number }>(
 594 | 		resource: string,
 595 | 		params: { id: string | number }
 596 | 	): Promise<DeleteResult<RecordType>> {
 597 | 		const config = resourceConfigs[resource as ResourceName];
 598 | 		if (!config) {
 599 | 			throw new Error(`Unknown resource: ${resource}`);
 600 | 		}
 601 | 
 602 | 		const { id } = params;
 603 | 		const primaryKey = config.primaryKey as string;
 604 | 		const column = getTableColumn(config.table, primaryKey);
 605 | 
 606 | 		if (!column) {
 607 | 			throw new Error(`Primary key column '${primaryKey}' not found`);
 608 | 		}
 609 | 
 610 | 		const result = await db.delete(config.table).where(eq(column, id)).returning();
 611 | 
 612 | 		if (!result[0]) {
 613 | 			throw new Error(`Record not found: ${id}`);
 614 | 		}
 615 | 
 616 | 		// biome-ignore lint/suspicious/noExplicitAny: Generic delete cast
 617 | 		const record = config.transformGet ? config.transformGet(result[0] as any) : result[0];
 618 | 		return { data: record as unknown as RecordType };
 619 | 	},
 620 | 
 621 | 	async deleteMany(resource: string, params: { ids: (string | number)[] }): Promise<{ data: (string | number)[] }> {
 622 | 		const config = resourceConfigs[resource as ResourceName];
 623 | 		if (!config) {
 624 | 			throw new Error(`Unknown resource: ${resource}`);
 625 | 		}
 626 | 
 627 | 		const { ids } = params;
 628 | 		const primaryKey = config.primaryKey as string;
 629 | 		const column = getTableColumn(config.table, primaryKey);
 630 | 
 631 | 		if (!column) {
 632 | 			throw new Error(`Primary key column '${primaryKey}' not found`);
 633 | 		}
 634 | 
 635 | 		const result = await db
 636 | 			.delete(config.table)
 637 | 			.where(inArray(column, ids as string[]))
 638 | 			.returning();
 639 | 
 640 | 		return { data: (result as { id: string }[]).map(record => record.id) };
 641 | 	}
 642 | };

```

`index.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { ORPCError, os } from "@orpc/server";
   2 | 
   3 | import type { UserRole } from "@clinic/auth/permissions";
   4 | import z from "zod";
   5 | import type { Context } from "./context";
   6 | 
   7 | export const o = os.$context<Context>().errors({
   8 | 	UNAUTHORIZED: {
   9 | 		message: "Unauthorized access",
  10 | 		statusCode: 401
  11 | 	},
  12 | 	FORBIDDEN: {
  13 | 		message: "Forbidden access",
  14 | 		statusCode: 403
  15 | 	},
  16 | 	RATE_LIMITED: {
  17 | 		data: z.object({ retryAfter: z.number() }),
  18 | 		message: "You are being rate limited",
  19 | 		statusCode: 429
  20 | 	}
  21 | });
  22 | 
  23 | export const publicProcedure = o;
  24 | 
  25 | const requireAuth = o.middleware(async ({ context, next }) => {
  26 |   if (!context.session?.user) {
  27 |     throw new ORPCError("UNAUTHORIZED");
  28 |   }
  29 |   return next({
  30 |     context: {
  31 |       ...context,
  32 |       session: context.session,
  33 |       user: context.session.user,
  34 |       clinicId: context.session.user.clinicId ?? null,
  35 |       isAuthorized: (requiredRole: UserRole) => context.session?.user?.role === "admin" || context.session?.user?.role === (requiredRole as string)
  36 |     },
  37 |   });
  38 | });
  39 | 
  40 | export const protectedProcedure = publicProcedure.use(requireAuth);
  41 | 
  42 | const requireAdmin = o.middleware(async ({ context, next }) => {
  43 | 	if (!context.session?.user) {
  44 | 		throw new ORPCError("UNAUTHORIZED");
  45 | 	}
  46 | 	if (context.session.user.role !== "admin") {
  47 | 		throw new ORPCError("FORBIDDEN");
  48 | 	}
  49 | 	return next({
  50 | 		context
  51 | 	});
  52 | });
  53 | 
  54 | export const adminProcedure = publicProcedure.use(requireAdmin);
  55 | export const requireClinicId = (clinicId?: string | null) => {
  56 | 	if (!clinicId) {
  57 | 		throw new ORPCError("FORBIDDEN", { message: "Clinic ID is required" });
  58 | 	}
  59 | 	return clinicId;
  60 | };
  61 | 
  62 | export const clinicProcedure = protectedProcedure.use(async ({ context, next }) => {
  63 | 	const clinicId = requireClinicId(context.user?.clinicId);
  64 | 	return next({
  65 | 		context: {
  66 | 			...context,
  67 | 			clinicId
  68 | 		}
  69 | 	});
  70 | });
  71 | 
  72 | export function requireRole(role: "admin" | "doctor" | "patient" | "staff") {
  73 | 	return o.middleware(({ context, next }) => {
  74 | 		if (context.user?.role !== role) {
  75 | 			throw new ORPCError("FORBIDDEN", {
  76 | 				message: `Requires ${role} role. Current role: ${context.user?.role}`
  77 | 			});
  78 | 		}
  79 | 		return next({});
  80 | 	});
  81 | }

```

`lib/auth-functions.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { createServerFn } from "@tanstack/react-start";
   2 | import { getRequest, setResponseHeader } from "@tanstack/react-start/server";
   3 | 
   4 | import { auth } from "@clinic/auth";
   5 | 
   6 | type GetUserServerQuery = {
   7 | 	disableCookieCache?: boolean | undefined;
   8 | 	disableRefresh?: boolean | undefined;
   9 | };
  10 | 
  11 | /**
  12 |  * Shared logic for session retrieval.
  13 |  * Kept as a standard function to avoid TanStack Start compiler collisions.
  14 |  * This should only be called within a server context (e.g., createServerFn).
  15 |  */
  16 | async function fetchSessionInternal(query?: GetUserServerQuery) {
  17 | 	const request = getRequest();
  18 | 
  19 | 	const session = await auth.api.getSession({
  20 | 		headers: request.headers,
  21 | 		query,
  22 | 		returnHeaders: true
  23 | 	});
  24 | 
  25 | 	const cookies = session.headers?.getSetCookie();
  26 | 	if (cookies?.length) {
  27 | 		setResponseHeader("Set-Cookie", cookies);
  28 | 	}
  29 | 
  30 | 	return session;
  31 | }
  32 | 
  33 | /** Publicly exported server function to be called from the client */
  34 | export const getSession = createServerFn({ method: "GET" }).handler(async ({ data }: { data?: GetUserServerQuery }) => {
  35 | 	const session = await fetchSessionInternal(data);
  36 | 	// We only return the response part because Headers objects are not serializable
  37 | 	// and cause TanStack Start compiler/type errors.
  38 | 	return session.response;
  39 | });

```

`lib/roles.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { getSession } from "../lib/auth-functions";
   2 | import type { UserRole } from "@clinic/auth/permissions";
   3 | 
   4 | 
   5 | export const checkRole = async (role: UserRole): Promise<boolean> => {
   6 | 	const session = await getSession();
   7 | 
   8 | 	// Assuming Better-Auth stores user metadata in session.user.publicMetadata
   9 | 	const userRole = session?.user?.role?.toLowerCase();
  10 | 
  11 | 	return userRole === role.toLowerCase();
  12 | };
  13 | 
  14 | export const getRole = async (): Promise<string> => {
  15 | 	const session = await getSession();
  16 | 
  17 | 	// Default to "patient" if role is missing
  18 | 	const role = session?.user?.role?.toLowerCase() || "patient";
  19 | 
  20 | 	return role;
  21 | };

```

```ts
  24 | 
  25 | export const getAdminDashboardStats = adminProcedure
  26 | 	.output(AdminDashboardStatsSchema)
  27 | 	.handler(async ({ context }): Promise<z.infer<typeof AdminDashboardStatsSchema>> => {
  28 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  29 | 		// Run queries in parallel for better performance
  30 | 		const [clinicStats, appointmentCounts, monthlyData] = await Promise.all([
  31 | 			clinicRepo.getClinicDashboard(clinicId),
  32 | 			appointmentRepo.getAppointmentCountsByStatus(clinicId),
  33 | 			appointmentRepo.getMonthlyAppointmentData(clinicId, new Date().getFullYear())
  34 | 		]);
  35 | 
  36 | 		// Transform appointment counts with proper typing
  37 | 		const appointmentCountsArray = appointmentCounts as unknown as Array<{
  38 | 			status: AppointmentStatus;
  39 | 			count: number;
  40 | 		}>;
  41 | 
  42 | 		const appointmentCountsMap = appointmentCountsArray.reduce(
  43 | 			(acc: Record<string, number>, { status, count }) => {
  44 | 				if (status && status in acc) {
  45 | 					acc[status] = count;
  46 | 				}
  47 | 				return acc;
  48 | 			},
  49 | 			{
  50 | 				SCHEDULED: 0,
  51 | 				COMPLETED: 0,
  52 | 				CANCELLED: 0,
  53 | 				PENDING: 0,
  54 | 				NO_SHOW: 0,
  55 | 				CONFIRMED: 0
  56 | 			}
  57 | 		);
  58 | 
  59 | 		// Format available doctors
  60 | 		const formattedAvailableDoctors = ((clinicStats.topDoctors as Doctor[]) || []).map((doctor: Doctor) => ({
  61 | 			id: doctor.id ?? "",
  62 | 			name: doctor.name,
  63 | 			specialty: doctor.specialty ?? null,
  64 | 			available: doctor.isActive ?? false,
  65 | 			nextAvailableTime: null as string | null
  66 | 		}));
  67 | 
  68 | 		// Format recent records
  69 | 		const formattedLast5Records = (
  70 | 			(clinicStats.recentAppointments as unknown as typeof clinicStats.recentAppointments) || []
  71 | 		).map(record => ({
  72 | 			id: record.id,
  73 | 			patientName: record.patient ? `${record.patient.firstName} ${record.patient.lastName}` : "Unknown Patient",
  74 | 			doctorName: record.doctor?.name ?? "Unknown Doctor",
  75 | 			appointmentDate: record.appointmentDate,
  76 | 			status: (record.status ?? "PENDING") as AppointmentStatus,
  77 | 			type: record.type ?? null
  78 | 		}));
  79 | 
  80 | 		return {
  81 | 			availableDoctors: formattedAvailableDoctors,
  82 | 			last5Records: formattedLast5Records,
  83 | 			appointmentCounts: appointmentCountsMap as z.infer<typeof AdminDashboardStatsSchema>["appointmentCounts"],
  84 | 			monthlyData: monthlyData.map(d => ({
  85 | 				month: d.month.toString(),
  86 | 				appointments: Number(d.count)
  87 | 			})),
  88 | 			totalDoctors: clinicStats.stats.doctors,
  89 | 			totalPatient: clinicStats.stats.patients,
  90 | 			totalAppointments: clinicStats.stats.appointments
  91 | 		};
  92 | 	});

 366 | 	})
 367 | } as const;
 368 | 
 369 | // ============================================================================
 370 | // Main Router Export
 371 | // ============================================================================
 372 | 
 373 | export const adminRouter = {
 374 | 	search: searchProcedures,
 375 | 	reporting: reportingProcedures,
 376 | 	manage: userManagementProcedures,
 377 | 	userAuth: userAuthProcedures
 378 | } as const;

```

`routers/analytics.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // packages/api/src/routers/analytics.server.ts
   2 | 
   3 | import { z } from "zod";
   4 | 
   5 | import { appointmentRepo, patientRepo, pediatricRepo, systemRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   6 | 
   7 | import { clinicProcedure } from "../index";
   8 | 
   9 | // ============================================================================
  10 | // Types & Schemas
  11 | // ============================================================================
  12 | 
  13 | const TrendPeriodSchema = z.enum(["week", "month", "quarter", "year", "6months", "all"]);
  14 | const MetricTypeSchema = z.enum(["appointments", "patients", "revenue", "immunizations", "prescriptions", "growth"]);
  15 | 
  16 | const GetTrendsSchema = z.object({
  17 | 	period: TrendPeriodSchema.default("month"),
  18 | 	metric: MetricTypeSchema.optional(),
  19 | 	startDate: z.date().optional(),
  20 | 	endDate: z.date().optional(),
  21 | 	groupBy: z.enum(["day", "week", "month"]).default("month")
  22 | });
  23 | 
  24 | const GetAIPredictionsSchema = z.object({
  25 | 	patientId: z.string().optional(),
  26 | 	metric: MetricTypeSchema.default("appointments"),
  27 | 	horizon: z.enum(["week", "month", "quarter"]).default("month")
  28 | });
  29 | 
  30 | const GetOutcomeMetricsSchema = z.object({
  31 | 	clinicId: z.string().optional(),
  32 | 	startDate: z.date().optional(),
  33 | 	endDate: z.date().optional(),
  34 | 	patientId: z.string().optional()
  35 | });
  36 | 
  37 | // ============================================================================
  38 | // Analytics Procedures
  39 | // ============================================================================
  40 | 
  41 | // Get trends for various metrics
  42 | export const getTrends = clinicProcedure
  43 | 	.input(GetTrendsSchema)
  44 | 	.output(
  45 | 		z.object({
  46 | 			period: z.object({
  47 | 				start: z.date(),
  48 | 				end: z.date(),
  49 | 				label: z.string()
  50 | 			}),
  51 | 			data: z.array(
  52 | 				z.object({
  53 | 					date: z.date(),
  54 | 					value: z.number(),
  55 | 					label: z.string(),
  56 | 					metadata: z.record(z.string(), z.unknown()).optional()
  57 | 				})
  58 | 			),
  59 | 			summary: z.object({
  60 | 				total: z.number(),
  61 | 				average: z.number(),
  62 | 				growth: z.number(),
  63 | 				previousPeriodTotal: z.number(),
  64 | 				percentageChange: z.number()
  65 | 			})
  66 | 		})
  67 | 	)
  68 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  69 | 		const { period, metric, startDate, endDate } = input;
  70 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  71 | 
  72 | 		// Calculate date range based on period (Simplified implementation)
  73 | 		const end = endDate ?? new Date();
  74 | 		const start = startDate ?? new Date();
  75 | 		if (!startDate) {
  76 | 			switch (period) {
  77 | 				case "week": start.setDate(end.getDate() - 7); break;
  78 | 				case "month": start.setMonth(end.getMonth() - 1); break;
  79 | 				case "quarter": start.setMonth(end.getMonth() - 3); break;
  80 | 				case "6months": start.setMonth(end.getMonth() - 6); break;
  81 | 				case "year": start.setFullYear(end.getFullYear() - 1); break;
  82 | 				default: start.setMonth(end.getMonth() - 1);
  83 | 			}
  84 | 		}
  85 | 		const label = period;
  86 | 		const duration = end.getTime() - start.getTime();
  87 | 		const previousPeriodStart = new Date(start.getTime() - duration);
  88 | 
  89 | 		// Get data based on metric type
  90 | 		let data: Array<{ date: Date; value: number; label: string }> = [];
  91 | 		let previousPeriodTotal = 0;
  92 | 
  93 | 		switch (metric) {
  94 | 			case "appointments": {
  95 | 				const appointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, start, end);
  96 | 				data = appointments.map(a => ({ date: a.appointmentDate, value: 1, label: "Appointment" }));
  97 | 				const prev = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, previousPeriodStart, start);
  98 | 				previousPeriodTotal = prev.length;
  99 | 				break;
 100 | 			}
 101 | 			case "patients": {
 102 | 				const patients = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, start, end);
 103 | 				data = [{ date: start, value: patients.patients.total, label: "Patients" }];
 104 | 				const prev = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, previousPeriodStart, start);
 105 | 				previousPeriodTotal = prev.patients.total;
 106 | 				break;
 107 | 			}
 108 | 			case "revenue": {
 109 | 				const analytics = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, start, end);
 110 | 				data = [{ date: start, value: analytics.revenue.total, label: "Revenue" }];
 111 | 				const prev = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, previousPeriodStart, start);
 112 | 				previousPeriodTotal = prev.revenue.total;
 113 | 				break;
 114 | 			}
 115 | 			case "immunizations": {
 116 | 				const immunizations = await pediatricRepo.getImmunizationsInRange(clinicId, start, end);
 117 | 				data = immunizations.map(i => ({ date: i.date, value: 1, label: i.vaccine }));
 118 | 				const prev = await pediatricRepo.getImmunizationsInRange(clinicId, previousPeriodStart, start);
 119 | 				previousPeriodTotal = prev.length;
 120 | 				break;
 121 | 			}
 122 | 			case "prescriptions": {
 123 | 				const analytics = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, start, end);
 124 | 				data = [{ date: start, value: analytics.prescriptions, label: "Prescriptions" }];
 125 | 				const prev = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, previousPeriodStart, start);
 126 | 				previousPeriodTotal = prev.prescriptions;
 127 | 				break;
 128 | 			}
 129 | 			case "growth": {
 130 | 				const records = await pediatricRepo.getPatientGrowthRecords("", clinicId);
 131 | 				const filtered = records.filter(r => r.date >= start && r.date <= end);
 132 | 				data = filtered.map(r => ({ date: r.date, value: 1, label: "Growth Record" }));
 133 | 				previousPeriodTotal = records.filter(r => r.date >= previousPeriodStart && r.date < start).length;
 134 | 				break;
 135 | 			}
 136 | 			default: {
 137 | 				const appointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, start, end);
 138 | 				data = appointments.map(a => ({ date: a.appointmentDate, value: 1, label: "Appointment" }));
 139 | 				const prev = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, previousPeriodStart, start);
 140 | 				previousPeriodTotal = prev.length;
 141 | 			}
 142 | 		}
 143 | 
 144 | 		const total = data.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.value, 0);
 145 | 		const average = data.length > 0 ? total / data.length : 0;
 146 | 		const growth = previousPeriodTotal > 0 ? ((total - previousPeriodTotal) / previousPeriodTotal) * 100 : 0;
 147 | 
 148 | 		return {
 149 | 			period: { start, end, label },
 150 | 			data: data.map(d => ({
 151 | 				date: d.date,
 152 | 				value: d.value,
 153 | 				label: d.label
 154 | 			})),
 155 | 			summary: {
 156 | 				total,
 157 | 				average,
 158 | 				growth,
 159 | 				previousPeriodTotal,
 160 | 				percentageChange: growth
 161 | 			}
 162 | 		};
 163 | 	});

 405 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 406 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 407 | 		const startDate = input.startDate ?? new Date(Date.now() - 365 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
 408 | 		const endDate = input.endDate ?? new Date();
 409 |

 411 |

 414 | 				totalPatients: analytics.patients.total,
 415 | 				ageDistribution: [],

 417 | 			},

 423 | 			},

 426 | 					condition: "Common Cold",
 427 | 					prevalence: 25,
 428 | 					trend: "stable",
 429 | 					affectedPatients: Math.round(analytics.patients.total * 0.25)
 430 | 				}
 431 | 			],

 433 | 				{ season: "Winter", condition: "Influenza", incidence: 15 }
 434 | 			]

 438 | // Get performance benchmarks
 439 | export const getPerformanceBenchmarks = clinicProcedure
 440 | 	.input(
 441 | 		z.object({
 442 | 			metric: MetricTypeSchema.default("appointments"),
 443 | 			compareTo: z
 444 | 				.enum(["previous_period", "national_average", "state_average", "target"])
 445 | 				.default("previous_period")
 446 | 		})
 447 | 	)
 448 | 	.output(
 449 | 		z.object({
 450 | 			current: z.number(),
 451 | 			benchmark: z.number(),
 452 | 			variance: z.number(),
 453 | 			percentageDiff: z.number(),
 454 | 			status: z.enum(["above", "below", "at"]),
 455 | 			trend: z.enum(["improving", "declining", "stable"]),
 456 | 			recommendations: z.array(z.string())
 457 | 		})
 458 | 	)
 459 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 460 | 		const { metric, compareTo } = input;
 461 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 462 | 
 463 | 		const analytics = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000), new Date());
 464 | 		let currentValue = 0;
 465 | 		if (metric === "appointments") currentValue = analytics.appointments.total;
 466 | 		if (metric === "patients") currentValue = analytics.patients.total;
 467 | 		if (metric === "revenue") currentValue = analytics.revenue.total;
 468 | 
 469 | 		// Get benchmark value
 470 | 		let benchmarkValue = 0;
 471 | 		switch (compareTo) {
 472 | 			case "previous_period": {
 473 | 				benchmarkValue = currentValue * 0.9;
 474 | 				break;
 475 | 			}
 476 | 			case "national_average":
 477 | 				benchmarkValue = currentValue * 1.1;
 478 | 				break;
 479 | 			case "state_average":
 480 | 				benchmarkValue = currentValue * 1.05;
 481 | 				break;
 482 | 			case "target":
 483 | 				benchmarkValue = currentValue * 1.2;
 484 | 				break;
 485 | 		}
 486 | 
 487 | 		const variance = currentValue - benchmarkValue;
 488 | 		const percentageDiff = benchmarkValue > 0 ? (variance / benchmarkValue) * 100 : 0;
 489 | 		const status = percentageDiff > 5 ? "above" : percentageDiff < -5 ? "below" : "at";
 490 | 		const trend = "stable";
 491 | 
 492 | 		const recommendations = getBenchmarkRecommendationsAction(metric, status, trend);
 493 | 
 494 | 		return {
 495 | 			current: currentValue,
 496 | 			benchmark: benchmarkValue,
 497 | 			variance,
 498 | 			percentageDiff,
 499 | 			status,
 500 | 			trend,
 501 | 			recommendations
 502 | 		};
 503 | 	});
 504 | 
 505 | // ============================================================================
 506 | // Analytics Router Export
 507 | // ============================================================================
 508 | 
 509 | export const analyticsRouter = {
 510 | 	getTrends,
 511 | 	getAIPredictions,
 512 | 	getOutcomeMetrics,
 513 | 	getPatientOutcomePredictions,
 514 | 	getPopulationHealth,
 515 | 	getPerformanceBenchmarks
 516 | };
 517 | 
 518 | function getBenchmarkRecommendationsAction(
 519 | 	metric: z.infer<typeof MetricTypeSchema>,
 520 | 	status: "above" | "below" | "at",
 521 | 	trend: "improving" | "declining" | "stable"
 522 | ): string[] {
 523 | 	const recommendations: string[] = [];
 524 | 	const metricLabels: Record<string, string> = {
 525 | 		appointments: "appointment volume",
 526 | 		patients: "patient engagement",
 527 | 		revenue: "revenue performance",
 528 | 		immunizations: "immunization coverage",
 529 | 		prescriptions: "prescription management",
 530 | 		growth: "growth tracking"
 531 | 	};
 532 | 	const label = metricLabels[metric] ?? metric;
 533 | 
 534 | 	if (status === "below") {
 535 | 		recommendations.push(
 536 | 			`Review ${label} workflows and strengthen outreach or follow-up processes to close the gap.`
 537 | 		);
 538 | 	} else if (status === "above") {
 539 | 		recommendations.push(
 540 | 			`Maintain current ${label} practices while looking for opportunities to standardize success.`
 541 | 		);
 542 | 	} else {
 543 | 		recommendations.push(`Continue monitoring ${label} and keep performance consistent.`);
 544 | 	}
 545 | 
 546 | 	if (trend === "declining") {
 547 | 		recommendations.push(
 548 | 			`Investigate any recent operational changes affecting ${label} and address issues quickly.`
 549 | 		);
 550 | 	} else if (trend === "improving") {
 551 | 		recommendations.push(`Continue initiatives that are driving improvement in ${label}.`);
 552 | 	} else {
 553 | 		recommendations.push(`Keep a close watch on ${label} to ensure the trend remains stable.`);
 554 | 	}
 555 | 
 556 | 	switch (metric) {
 557 | 		case "appointments":
 558 | 			recommendations.push("Optimize scheduling and reminder systems to support growth.");
 559 | 			break;
 560 | 		case "patients":
 561 | 			recommendations.push("Enhance patient communication and retention efforts.");
 562 | 			break;
 563 | 		case "revenue":
 564 | 			recommendations.push("Review billing, coding, and collection workflows for efficiency.");
 565 | 			break;
 566 | 		case "immunizations":
 567 | 			recommendations.push("Ensure vaccine availability and follow-up for overdue patients.");
 568 | 			break;
 569 | 		case "prescriptions":
 570 | 			recommendations.push("Audit prescription fulfillment and adherence support processes.");
 571 | 			break;
 572 | 		case "growth":
 573 | 			recommendations.push("Track growth-related metrics closely and align care plans accordingly.");
 574 | 			break;
 575 | 	}
 576 | 
 577 | 	return recommendations;
 578 | }
 579 | 
 580 | // ============================================================================
 581 | // Helper Functions
 582 | // ============================================================================
 583 |

 585 | // Update main routers/index.ts to include analyticsRouter
 586 | // ============================================================================

```

`routers/appointment.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // ============================================================================
   2 | // Input Schemas
   3 | // ============================================================================
   4 | 
   5 | import z from "zod";
   6 | 
   7 | import { AppointmentSchema, type AppointmentStatus } from "@clinic/db/zod/clinic.schema";
   8 | 
   9 | import {
  10 |   bulkUpdateAppointmentsStatusAction,
  11 |   cancelAppointmentAction,
  12 |   createAppointmentAction,
  13 |   getAppointmentsInRangeAction,
  14 |   rescheduleAppointmentAction,
  15 |   searchAppointmentsAction,
  16 |   updateAppointmentAction as updateAppointmentActionFn
  17 | } from "@clinic/db/actions";
  18 | import { appointmentRepo, doctorRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
  19 | import { clinicProcedure, protectedProcedure, requireClinicId } from "..";
  20 | import {
  21 |   BulkUpdateStatusSchema,
  22 |   CancelAppointmentSchema,
  23 |   CreateAppointmentWithReminderSchema,
  24 |   GetAppointmentsSchema,
  25 |   GetAvailableTimeSlotsSchema,
  26 |   GetDoctorAvailabilitySchema,
  27 |   ListAppointmentsSchema,
  28 |   RescheduleAppointmentSchema,
  29 |   UpdateAppointmentStatusSchema
  30 | } from "../types";
  31 | // ============================================================================
  32 | // Appointment Procedures
  33 | // ============================================================================
  34 | export const appointmentProcedures = {
  35 | 	updateStatus: protectedProcedure.input(UpdateAppointmentStatusSchema).handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  36 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  37 | 		return await appointmentRepo.updateAppointment(input.id, {
  38 | 			status: input.status as AppointmentStatus,
  39 | 			clinicId
  40 | 		});
  41 | 	}),
  42 | 
  43 | 	bulkUpdateStatus: protectedProcedure.input(BulkUpdateStatusSchema).handler(async ({ input }) => {
  44 | 		return await appointmentRepo.updateManyAppointments(input.appointmentIds, {
  45 | 			status: input.status as AppointmentStatus
  46 | 		});
  47 | 	}),
  48 | 
  49 | 	cancel: protectedProcedure.input(CancelAppointmentSchema).handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  50 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  51 | 		return await appointmentRepo.updateAppointment(input.id, {
  52 | 			status: "CANCELLED",
  53 | 			clinicId
  54 | 			// notes: input.reason // if supported by mutation
  55 | 		});
  56 | 	}),
  57 | 
  58 | 	reschedule: protectedProcedure.input(RescheduleAppointmentSchema).handler(async ({ input }) => {
  59 | 		const appointmentDate = new Date(`${input.newDate}T${input.newTime}`);
  60 | 		return await appointmentRepo.updateAppointment(input.id, {
  61 | 			appointmentDate
  62 | 			// reason: input.reason // if supported by mutation
  63 | 		});
  64 | 	})
  65 | };
  66 | 
  67 | // Create appointment
  68 | export const createAppointment = clinicProcedure
  69 | 	.input(AppointmentSchema)
  70 | 	.output(z.any())
  71 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  72 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  73 | 		return await createAppointmentAction({ ...input, clinicId });
  74 | 	});
  75 | 
  76 | // Update appointment
  77 | export const updateAppointment = clinicProcedure
  78 | 	.input(AppointmentSchema.partial())
  79 | 	.output(z.any())
  80 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  81 | 		if (!input.id) {
  82 | 			throw new Error("Appointment ID is required for update");
  83 | 		}
  84 | 
  85 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  86 | 
  87 | 		// 1. Remove undefined values to satisfy the Drizzle/TypeScript strict types
  88 | 		// This removes any keys that were not provided in the partial input
  89 | 		const updateData = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(input).filter(([_, value]) => value !== undefined));
  90 | 
  91 | 		return await updateAppointmentActionFn({ ...updateData, id: input.id, clinicId });
  92 | 	});
  93 | // Update appointment status
  94 | export const updateAppointmentStatus = protectedProcedure
  95 | 	.input(UpdateAppointmentStatusSchema)
  96 | 	.output(z.any())
  97 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  98 | 		// const _clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  99 | 		return await appointmentRepo.updateAppointmentStatus(input.id, input.status);
 100 | 	});
 101 | 
 102 | // Bulk update appointment status
 103 | export const bulkUpdateAppointmentStatus = protectedProcedure
 104 | 	.input(BulkUpdateStatusSchema)
 105 | 	.output(z.array(z.any()))
 106 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 107 | 		const result = await bulkUpdateAppointmentsStatusAction({
 108 | 			appointmentIds: input.appointmentIds,
 109 | 			status: input.status,
 110 | 			reason: input.reason
 111 | 		});
 112 | 		if (result.error || !result.data) {
 113 | 			throw new Error(result.error || "Failed to update appointments");
 114 | 		}
 115 | 		return result.data.updatedAppointments;
 116 | 	});
 117 | 
 118 | // Cancel appointment
 119 | export const cancelAppointment = protectedProcedure
 120 | 	.input(CancelAppointmentSchema)
 121 | 	.output(z.any())
 122 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 123 | 		return await cancelAppointmentAction(input);
 124 | 	});
 125 | 
 126 | // Reschedule appointment
 127 | export const rescheduleAppointment = protectedProcedure
 128 | 	.input(RescheduleAppointmentSchema)
 129 | 	.output(z.any())
 130 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 131 | 		return await rescheduleAppointmentAction({
 132 | 			id: input.id,
 133 | 			newDate: input.newDate,
 134 | 			newTime: input.newTime,
 135 | 			reason: input.reason
 136 | 		});
 137 | 	});
 138 | 
 139 | // Get paginated appointments
 140 | export const getAppointments = protectedProcedure.input(GetAppointmentsSchema).handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 141 | 	const clinicId = requireClinicId(context.clinicId);
 142 | 	const { page, limit, status, doctorId, patientId } = input;
 143 | 	return await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsFallbackPaginated(clinicId, page, limit, status, doctorId, patientId);
 144 | });
 145 | 
 146 | // Get appointment by ID
 147 | export const getAppointmentById = protectedProcedure
 148 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 149 | 	.output(z.any())
 150 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 151 | 		const clinicId = requireClinicId(context.clinicId);
 152 | 		return await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentById(input.id, clinicId);
 153 | 	});
 154 | 
 155 | // List appointments with advanced filters
 156 | export const listAppointments = protectedProcedure
 157 | 	.input(ListAppointmentsSchema)
 158 | 	.output(
 159 | 		z.object({
 160 | 			appointments: z.array(z.any()),
 161 | 			total: z.number(),
 162 | 			page: z.number(),
 163 | 			limit: z.number(),
 164 | 			totalPages: z.number()
 165 | 		})
 166 | 	)
 167 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 168 | 		const clinicId = requireClinicId(context.clinicId);
 169 | 		const { page, limit, ...filters } = input;
 170 | 		const result = await searchAppointmentsAction(clinicId, filters, { page, limit });
 171 | 		if (result.error || !result.data) {
 172 | 			throw new Error(result.error || "Failed to list appointments");
 173 | 		}
 174 | 		return result.data;
 175 | 	});
 176 | 
 177 | // Get doctor availability
 178 | export const getDoctorAvailability = protectedProcedure
 179 | 	.input(GetDoctorAvailabilitySchema)
 180 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 181 | 		return await doctorRepo.getDoctorAvailability(input.doctorId, input.date);
 182 | 	});
 183 | 
 184 | // Get available time slots
 185 | export const getAvailableTimeSlots = protectedProcedure
 186 | 	.input(GetAvailableTimeSlotsSchema)
 187 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 188 | 		return await doctorRepo.getAvailableTimeSlots(input.doctorId, input.date, input.durationMinutes);
 189 | 	});
 190 | 
 191 | // Create appointment with reminder
 192 | export const createAppointmentWithReminder = protectedProcedure
 193 | 	.input(CreateAppointmentWithReminderSchema)
 194 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 195 | 		return await appointmentRepo.createAppointmentWithReminder(input.data, input.reminderData);
 196 | 	});
 197 | 
 198 | // ============================================================================
 199 | // Main Router Export
 200 | // ============================================================================
 201 | 
 202 | export const appointmentRouter = {
 203 | 	// Core CRUD operations
 204 | 	create: createAppointment,
 205 | 	update: updateAppointment,
 206 | 	getById: getAppointmentById,
 207 | 
 208 | 	// Status management
 209 | 	updateStatus: updateAppointmentStatus,
 210 | 	bulkUpdateStatus: bulkUpdateAppointmentStatus,
 211 | 	cancel: cancelAppointment,
 212 | 	reschedule: rescheduleAppointment,
 213 | 
 214 | 	// Query operations
 215 | 	list: listAppointments,
 216 | 	get: getAppointments,
 217 | 	getInRange: getAppointmentsInRangeAction,
 218 | 
 219 | 	// Doctor availability
 220 | 	getDoctorAvailability,
 221 | 	getAvailableTimeSlots,
 222 | 
 223 | 	// Advanced operations
 224 | 	createWithReminder: createAppointmentWithReminder
 225 | } as const;

```

`routers/auth.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // src/orpc/routers/auth.ts
   2 | 
   3 | import { ORPCError } from "@orpc/server";
   4 | import z from "zod";
   5 | 
   6 | import { UserCreateSchema } from "@clinic/db/zod";
   7 | import { auth } from "@clinic/auth";
   8 | 
   9 | import { updateUserAction } from "@clinic/db/actions";
  10 | import { o as base, protectedProcedure, publicProcedure } from "../index";
  11 | 
  12 | export const UserAuthSchema = UserCreateSchema.omit({
  13 | 	role: true,
  14 | 	name: true,
  15 | 	email: true
  16 | }).extend({
  17 | 	role: z.enum(["admin", "doctor", "patient", "staff"]),
  18 | 	password: z.string().min(6),
  19 | 	name: z.string(),
  20 | 	email: z.email()
  21 | });
  22 | 
  23 | const signUpSchema = UserCreateSchema.pick({ email: true }).extend({
  24 | 	role: z.enum(["patient", "doctor"]),
  25 | 	password: z.string().min(6),
  26 | 	name: z.string()
  27 | });
  28 | 
  29 | export const authRouter = base.router({
  30 | 	signup: publicProcedure
  31 | 		.route({
  32 | 			method: "POST",
  33 | 			path: "/auth/signup",
  34 | 			summary: "User signup",
  35 | 			tags: ["Auth"]
  36 | 		})
  37 | 		.input(signUpSchema)
  38 | 		.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  39 | 			const { email, password, role, name } = input;
  40 | 
  41 | 			// Passing headers helps Better Auth manage the initial session/cookies
  42 | 			const result = await auth.api.signUpEmail({
  43 | 				body: { email, password, name },
  44 | 				headers: context.headers
  45 | 			});
  46 | 
  47 | 			// Better Auth returns standard objects, check for user existence
  48 | 			if (!result?.user) {
  49 | 				throw new ORPCError("BAD_REQUEST", {
  50 | 					message: "Registration failed. User may already exist."
  51 | 				});
  52 | 			}
  53 | 
  54 | 			// Update role using mutations
  55 | 			await updateUserAction(result.user.id, { role });
  56 | 
  57 | 			return {
  58 | 				id: result.user.id,
  59 | 				email: result.user.email,
  60 | 				name: result.user.name,
  61 | 				role
  62 | 			};
  63 | 		}),
  64 | 
  65 | 	signIn: publicProcedure
  66 | 		.route({
  67 | 			method: "POST",
  68 | 			path: "/auth/signin",
  69 | 			summary: "User signin",
  70 | 			tags: ["Auth"]
  71 | 		})
  72 | 		.input(
  73 | 			z.object({
  74 | 				email: z.email(),
  75 | 				password: z.string()
  76 | 			})
  77 | 		)
  78 | 		.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  79 | 			const result = await auth.api.signInEmail({
  80 | 				body: input,
  81 | 				headers: context.headers
  82 | 			});
  83 | 
  84 | 			if (!result?.user) {
  85 | 				throw new ORPCError("UNAUTHORIZED", {
  86 | 					message: "Invalid email or password"
  87 | 				});
  88 | 			}
  89 | 
  90 | 			return {
  91 | 				id: result.user.id,
  92 | 				email: result.user.email,
  93 | 				name: result.user.name,
  94 | 				role: result.user?.role // Explicit cast if role is custom
  95 | 			};
  96 | 		}),
  97 | 
  98 | 	signOut: protectedProcedure
  99 | 		.route({
 100 | 			method: "POST",
 101 | 			path: "/auth/signout",
 102 | 			summary: "User signout",
 103 | 			tags: ["Auth"]
 104 | 		})
 105 | 		.handler(async ({ context }) => {
 106 | 			// Must pass headers to identify which session to kill
 107 | 			await auth.api.signOut({
 108 | 				headers: context.headers
 109 | 			});
 110 | 
 111 | 			return { success: true };
 112 | 		}),
 113 | 
 114 | 	getSession: protectedProcedure
 115 | 		.route({
 116 | 			method: "GET",
 117 | 			path: "/auth/session",
 118 | 			summary: "Get current user session",
 119 | 			tags: ["Auth"]
 120 | 		})
 121 | 		.handler(async ({ context }) => {
 122 | 			const result = await auth.api.getSession({
 123 | 				headers: context.headers
 124 | 			});
 125 | 
 126 | 			if (!result?.user) {
 127 | 				throw new ORPCError("UNAUTHORIZED", {
 128 | 					message: "No active session found"
 129 | 				});
 130 | 			}
 131 | 
 132 | 			return {
 133 | 				id: result.user.id,
 134 | 				email: result.user.email,
 135 | 				name: result.user.name,
 136 | 				role: result.user?.role,
 137 | 				image: result.user?.image ?? null // Include image if available
 138 | 			};
 139 | 		})
 140 | });

```

`routers/calender.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { z } from "zod";
   2 | 
   3 | import type { AppointmentStatus } from "@clinic/db";
   4 | import { appointmentRepo, calendarRepo, doctorRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   5 | import { clinicProcedure } from "../index";
   6 | import { CreateAppointmentWithReminderSchema } from "../types";
   7 | import { getEventColorAction } from '@clinic/db/actions/calendar.actions';
   8 | 
   9 | // ============================================================================
  10 | // Types & Schemas
  11 | // ============================================================================
  12 | 
  13 | const CalendarEventSchema = z.object({
  14 | 	id: z.string(),
  15 | 	title: z.string(),
  16 | 	start: z.date(),
  17 | 	end: z.date(),
  18 | 	allDay: z.boolean().default(false),
  19 | 	backgroundColor: z.string().optional(),
  20 | 	borderColor: z.string().optional(),
  21 | 	textColor: z.string().optional(),
  22 | 	extendedProps: z.object({
  23 | 		patientId: z.string(),
  24 | 		patientName: z.string(),
  25 | 		doctorId: z.string(),
  26 | 		doctorName: z.string(),
  27 | 		type: z.string(),
  28 | 		status: z.string(),
  29 | 		notes: z.string().nullable(),
  30 | 		appointmentId: z.string()
  31 | 	})
  32 | });
  33 | 
  34 | const GetCalendarEventsSchema = z.object({
  35 | 	start: z.date(),
  36 | 	end: z.date(),
  37 | 	doctorId: z.string().optional(),
  38 | 	status: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
  39 | 	type: z.array(z.string()).optional()
  40 | });
  41 | 
  42 | const UpdateCalendarEventSchema = z.object({
  43 | 	id: z.string(),
  44 | 	title: z.string().optional(),
  45 | 	start: z.date().optional(),
  46 | 	end: z.date().optional(),
  47 | 	status: z.enum(["SCHEDULED", "CONFIRMED", "COMPLETED", "CANCELLED", "NO_SHOW"]).optional(),
  48 | 	notes: z.string().optional()
  49 | });
  50 | 
  51 | const BulkUpdateSchema = z.object({
  52 | 	eventIds: z.array(z.string()),
  53 | 	status: z.enum(["SCHEDULED", "CONFIRMED", "CANCELLED"]),
  54 | 	reason: z.string().optional()
  55 | });
  56 | 
  57 | const GetAvailabilitySchema = z.object({
  58 | 	doctorId: z.string(),
  59 | 	date: z.date(),
  60 | 	duration: z.number().default(30)
  61 | });
  62 | 
  63 | const GetAvailableSlotsSchema = z.object({
  64 | 	doctorId: z.string(),
  65 | 	date: z.date(),
  66 | 	duration: z.number().default(30),
  67 | 	startTime: z.string().optional(),
  68 | 	endTime: z.string().optional()
  69 | });
  70 | 
  71 | // ============================================================================
  72 | // Calendar Procedures
  73 | // ============================================================================
  74 | 
  75 | // Get calendar events for date range
  76 | export const getCalendarEvents = clinicProcedure
  77 | 	.input(GetCalendarEventsSchema)
  78 | 	.output(z.array(CalendarEventSchema))
  79 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  80 | 		const { start, end, doctorId } = input;
  81 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  82 | 
  83 | 		const appointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, start, end, doctorId);
  84 | 
  85 | 		// Transform to calendar events
  86 | 		return appointments.map(apt => {
  87 | 			const duration = apt.durationMinutes || 30;
  88 | 			const endTime = new Date(apt.appointmentDate);
  89 | 			endTime.setMinutes(endTime.getMinutes() + duration);
  90 | 
  91 | 			const typeColor = getEventColorAction(apt.type || "sick-visit");
  92 | 
  93 | 			return {
  94 | 				id: apt.id,
  95 | 				title: `${apt.patient?.firstName || "Unknown"} ${apt.patient?.lastName || ""} - ${formatEventType(apt.type)}`,
  96 | 				start: apt.appointmentDate,
  97 | 				end: endTime,
  98 | 				allDay: false,
  99 | 				backgroundColor: typeColor,
 100 | 				borderColor: typeColor,
 101 | 				textColor: "#ffffff",
 102 | 				extendedProps: {
 103 | 					patientId: apt.patientId,
 104 | 					patientName: `${apt.patient?.firstName || "Unknown"} ${apt.patient?.lastName || ""}`,
 105 | 					doctorId: apt.doctorId || "",
 106 | 					doctorName: apt.doctor?.name || "Unassigned",
 107 | 					type: mapAppointmentTypeToEventType(apt.type),
 108 | 					status: apt.status || "SCHEDULED",
 109 | 					notes: apt.note,
 110 | 					appointmentId: apt.id
 111 | 				}
 112 | 			};
 113 | 		});
 114 | 	});
 115 | 
 116 | // Create calendar event (appointment) - Using mutations
 117 | export const createCalendarEvent = clinicProcedure
 118 | 	.input(CreateAppointmentWithReminderSchema)
 119 | 	.output(CalendarEventSchema)
 120 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 121 | 		const { data, reminderData } = input;
 122 | 		const { appointmentDate: start, patientId, doctorId, type, note: notes, durationMinutes: duration } = data;
 123 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 124 | 		const appointmentDuration = duration || 30;
 125 | 		const end = new Date(new Date(start).getTime() + appointmentDuration * 60000);
 126 | 
 127 | 		// Check if slot is available using queries
 128 | 		const availableSlots = await doctorRepo.getAvailableTimeSlots(doctorId, new Date(start), appointmentDuration);
 129 | 
 130 | 		const isSlotAvailable = availableSlots.some(
 131 | 			slot => new Date(slot.startTime).getTime() === new Date(start).getTime()
 132 | 		);
 133 | 
 134 | 		if (!isSlotAvailable) {
 135 | 			throw new Error("Selected time slot is not available");
 136 | 		}
 137 | 
 138 | 		// Get patient and doctor info using queries
 139 | 		const patientData = await context.db.query.patient.findFirst({
 140 | 			where: { id: patientId },
 141 | 			columns: { firstName: true, lastName: true }
 142 | 		});
 143 | 
 144 | 		const doctorData = await context.db.query.doctor.findFirst({
 145 | 			where: { id: doctorId },
 146 | 			columns: { name: true }
 147 | 		});
 148 | 
 149 | 		const patientName = patientData ? `${patientData.firstName} ${patientData.lastName}` : "Unknown";
 150 | 
 151 | 		// Create appointment using mutation
 152 | 		const newAppointment = await appointmentRepo.createAppointment({
 153 | 			id: crypto.randomUUID(),
 154 | 			clinicId,
 155 | 			patientId,
 156 | 			doctorId,
 157 | 			appointmentDate: new Date(start),
 158 | 			durationMinutes: appointmentDuration,
 159 | 			type: type || "sick-visit",
 160 | 			status: "PENDING",
 161 | 			note: notes,
 162 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
 163 | 			updatedAt: new Date(),
 164 | 			time: new Date(start).toLocaleTimeString()
 165 | 		});
 166 | 
 167 | 		if (!newAppointment) {
 168 | 			throw new Error("Failed to create appointment");
 169 | 		}
 170 | 
 171 | 		// Create reminders if requested using calendar helper
 172 | 		if (reminderData) {
 173 | 			await appointmentRepo.createAppointmentWithReminder(data, reminderData);
 174 | 		}
 175 | 
 176 | 		const eventType = type || "sick-visit";
 177 | 
 178 | 		// Return calendar event
 179 | 		return {
 180 | 			id: newAppointment.id,
 181 | 			title: `${patientName} - ${formatEventType(eventType)}`,
 182 | 			start: new Date(start),
 183 | 			end,
 184 | 			allDay: false,
 185 | 			backgroundColor: getEventColor(eventType),
 186 | 			borderColor: getEventColor(eventType),
 187 | 			textColor: "#ffffff",
 188 | 			extendedProps: {
 189 | 				patientId,
 190 | 				patientName,
 191 | 				doctorId,
 192 | 				doctorName: doctorData?.name || "Unassigned",
 193 | 				type: eventType,
 194 | 				status: "SCHEDULED",
 195 | 				notes: notes || null,
 196 | 				appointmentId: newAppointment.id
 197 | 			}
 198 | 		};
 199 | 	});
 200 | 
 201 | // Update calendar event - Using mutations
 202 | export const updateCalendarEvent = clinicProcedure
 203 | 	.input(UpdateCalendarEventSchema)
 204 | 	.output(CalendarEventSchema)
 205 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 206 | 		const { id, start, end, status, notes } = input;
 207 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 208 | 
 209 | 		// Get existing appointment using queries
 210 | 		const existingAppointment = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentById(id, clinicId);
 211 | 
 212 | 		if (!existingAppointment) {
 213 | 			throw new Error("Appointment not found");
 214 | 		}
 215 | 
 216 | 		// If rescheduling, check availability
 217 | 		if (start && start.getTime() !== existingAppointment.appointmentDate.getTime()) {
 218 | 			const appointmentDuration = existingAppointment.durationMinutes || 30;
 219 | 			const availableSlots = await doctorRepo.getAvailableTimeSlots(
 220 | 				existingAppointment.doctorId,
 221 | 				new Date(start),
 222 | 				appointmentDuration
 223 | 			);
 224 | 
 225 | 			const isAvailable = availableSlots.some(
 226 | 				slot => new Date(slot.startTime).getTime() === new Date(start).getTime()
 227 | 			);
 228 | 
 229 | 			if (!isAvailable) {
 230 | 				throw new Error("Selected time slot is not available");
 231 | 			}
 232 | 		}
 233 | 
 234 | 		// Update appointment using mutation
 235 | 		const updatedAppointment = await appointmentRepo.updateAppointment(id, {
 236 | 			clinicId,
 237 | 			appointmentDate: start || existingAppointment.appointmentDate,
 238 | 			durationMinutes:
 239 | 				start && end
 240 | 					? Math.round((end.getTime() - start.getTime()) / (1000 * 60))
 241 | 					: existingAppointment.durationMinutes,
 242 | 			status: (status as AppointmentStatus) || existingAppointment.status,
 243 | 			note: notes !== undefined ? notes : existingAppointment.note,
 244 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
 245 | 		});
 246 | 
 247 | 		if (!updatedAppointment) {
 248 | 			throw new Error("Failed to update appointment");
 249 | 		}
 250 | 
 251 | 		const eventStart = start || existingAppointment.appointmentDate;
 252 | 		const eventEnd = end || new Date(eventStart.getTime() + (existingAppointment.durationMinutes || 30) * 60000);
 253 | 		const eventType = mapAppointmentTypeToEventType(existingAppointment.type);
 254 | 		const patientName = existingAppointment.patient
 255 | 			? `${existingAppointment.patient.firstName} ${existingAppointment.patient.lastName}`
 256 | 			: "Unknown";
 257 | 
 258 | 		return {
 259 | 			id: updatedAppointment.id,
 260 | 			title: `${patientName} - ${formatEventType(eventType)}`,
 261 | 			start: eventStart,
 262 | 			end: eventEnd,
 263 | 			allDay: false,
 264 | 			backgroundColor: getEventColor(eventType),
 265 | 			borderColor: getEventColor(eventType),
 266 | 			textColor: "#ffffff",
 267 | 			extendedProps: {
 268 | 				patientId: existingAppointment.patientId,
 269 | 				patientName,
 270 | 				doctorId: existingAppointment.doctorId,
 271 | 				doctorName: existingAppointment.doctor?.name || "Unassigned",
 272 | 				type: eventType,
 273 | 				status: updatedAppointment.status || "SCHEDULED",
 274 | 				notes: updatedAppointment.note,
 275 | 				appointmentId: updatedAppointment.id
 276 | 			}
 277 | 		};
 278 | 	});
 279 | 
 280 | // Delete calendar event - Using mutations (soft delete)
 281 | export const deleteCalendarEvent = clinicProcedure
 282 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string(), reason: z.string().optional() }))
 283 | 	.output(z.object({ success: z.boolean(), message: z.string() }))
 284 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 285 | 		const { id, reason } = input;
 286 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 287 | 
 288 | 		// Use cancelAppointment mutation
 289 | 		const cancelledAppointment = await appointmentRepo.cancelAppointment(
 290 | 			id,
 291 | 			reason || "Cancelled via calendar",
 292 | 			clinicId
 293 | 		);
 294 | 
 295 | 		if (!cancelledAppointment) {
 296 | 			throw new Error("Appointment not found or could not be cancelled");
 297 | 		}
 298 | 
 299 | 		return {
 300 | 			success: true,
 301 | 			message: "Event deleted successfully"
 302 | 		};
 303 | 	});
 304 | 
 305 | // Bulk update events - Using mutations
 306 | export const bulkUpdateEvents = clinicProcedure
 307 | 	.input(BulkUpdateSchema)
 308 | 	.output(z.object({ updatedCount: z.number(), failedIds: z.array(z.string()) }))
 309 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 310 | 		const { eventIds, status } = input;
 311 | 		// const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 312 | 		const failedIds: string[] = [];
 313 | 
 314 | 		// Use bulk update mutation
 315 | 		const updated = await appointmentRepo.bulkUpdateAppointmentStatus(eventIds, status as AppointmentStatus);
 316 | 
 317 | 		const updatedCount = updated.length;
 318 | 		const updatedIds = new Set(updated.map(a => a.id));
 319 | 		const failed = eventIds.filter(id => !updatedIds.has(id));
 320 | 		failedIds.push(...failed);
 321 | 
 322 | 		return {
 323 | 			updatedCount,
 324 | 			failedIds
 325 | 		};
 326 | 	});
 327 | 
 328 | // Get doctor availability for a specific date - Using queries
 329 | export const getDoctorAvailability = clinicProcedure
 330 | 	.input(GetAvailabilitySchema)
 331 | 	.output(
 332 | 		z.object({
 333 | 			isAvailable: z.boolean(),
 334 | 			availableSlots: z.array(
 335 | 				z.object({
 336 | 					start: z.date(),
 337 | 					end: z.date()
 338 | 				})
 339 | 			),
 340 | 			bookedSlots: z.array(
 341 | 				z.object({
 342 | 					start: z.date(),
 343 | 					end: z.date()
 344 | 				})
 345 | 			),
 346 | 			workingHours: z.object({
 347 | 				start: z.string(),
 348 | 				end: z.string()
 349 | 			})
 350 | 		})
 351 | 	)
 352 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 353 | 		const { doctorId, date, duration } = input;
 354 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 355 | 
 356 | 		// Get doctor's working hours for the day using queries
 357 | 		const workingHours = await calendarRepo.getDoctorWorkingHours(doctorId, date);
 358 | 
 359 | 		if (!workingHours) {
 360 | 			return {
 361 | 				isAvailable: false,
 362 | 				availableSlots: [],
 363 | 				bookedSlots: [],
 364 | 				workingHours: { start: "09:00", end: "17:00" }
 365 | 			};
 366 | 		}
 367 | 
 368 | 		// Get existing appointments for the doctor on this date using queries
 369 | 		const startOfDay = new Date(date);
 370 | 		startOfDay.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
 371 | 
 372 | 		const endOfDay = new Date(date);
 373 | 		endOfDay.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
 374 | 
 375 | 		const existingAppointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(
 376 | 			clinicId,
 377 | 			startOfDay,
 378 | 			endOfDay,
 379 | 			doctorId
 380 | 		);
 381 | 
 382 | 		// Calculate available time slots using calendar helper
 383 | 		const availableSlots = calculateAvailableSlots(
 384 | 			workingHours.start,
 385 | 			workingHours.end,
 386 | 			duration,
 387 | 			existingAppointments.map(apt => ({
 388 | 				start: apt.appointmentDate,
 389 | 				duration: apt.durationMinutes ?? 30
 390 | 			}))
 391 | 		);
 392 | 
 393 | 		const bookedSlots = existingAppointments.map(apt => ({
 394 | 			start: apt.appointmentDate,
 395 | 			end: new Date(apt.appointmentDate.getTime() + (apt.durationMinutes || 30) * 60000)
 396 | 		}));
 397 | 
 398 | 		return {
 399 | 			isAvailable: availableSlots.length > 0,
 400 | 			availableSlots,
 401 | 			bookedSlots,
 402 | 			workingHours
 403 | 		};
 404 | 	});
 405 | 
 406 | // Get available time slots for a doctor - Using queries
 407 | export const getAvailableTimeSlots = clinicProcedure
 408 | 	.input(GetAvailableSlotsSchema)
 409 | 	.output(
 410 | 		z.array(
 411 | 			z.object({
 412 | 				start: z.date(),
 413 | 				end: z.date(),
 414 | 				formattedStart: z.string(),
 415 | 				formattedEnd: z.string()
 416 | 			})
 417 | 		)
 418 | 	)
 419 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 420 | 		const { doctorId, date, duration, startTime, endTime } = input;
 421 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 422 | 
 423 | 		// Get doctor's working hours
 424 | 		const workingHours = await calendarRepo.getDoctorWorkingHours(doctorId, date);
 425 | 
 426 | 		const workingStart = startTime || workingHours?.start || "09:00";
 427 | 		const workingEnd = endTime || workingHours?.end || "17:00";
 428 | 
 429 | 		// Get existing appointments using queries
 430 | 		const startOfDay = new Date(date);
 431 | 		startOfDay.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
 432 | 
 433 | 		const endOfDay = new Date(date);
 434 | 		endOfDay.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
 435 | 
 436 | 		const existingAppointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(
 437 | 			clinicId,
 438 | 			startOfDay,
 439 | 			endOfDay,
 440 | 			doctorId
 441 | 		);
 442 | 
 443 | 		// Calculate slots using calendar helper
 444 | 		const slots = getAvailableTimeSlotsAction(
 445 | 			workingStart,
 446 | 			workingEnd,
 447 | 			duration,
 448 | 			existingAppointments.map(apt => ({
 449 | 				start: apt.appointmentDate,
 450 | 				duration: apt.durationMinutes ?? 30
 451 | 			}))
 452 | 		);
 453 | 
 454 | 		// Format slots for display
 455 | 		return slots.map(slot => ({
 456 | 			start: slot.start,
 457 | 			end: slot.end,
 458 | 			formattedStart: slot.start.toLocaleTimeString([], {
 459 | 				hour: "2-digit",
 460 | 				minute: "2-digit"
 461 | 			}),
 462 | 			formattedEnd: slot.end.toLocaleTimeString([], {
 463 | 				hour: "2-digit",
 464 | 				minute: "2-digit"
 465 | 			})
 466 | 		}));
 467 | 	});

 469 | // Get event details by ID - Using queries
 470 | export const getEventDetails = clinicProcedure
 471 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 472 | 	.output(CalendarEventSchema.nullable())
 473 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 474 | 		const { id } = input;
 475 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 476 | 
 477 | 		const appointmentData = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentById(id, clinicId);
 478 | 
 479 | 		if (!appointmentData) {
 480 | 			return null;
 481 | 		}
 482 | 
 483 | 		const duration = appointmentData.durationMinutes || 30;
 484 | 		const endTime = new Date(appointmentData.appointmentDate);
 485 | 		endTime.setMinutes(endTime.getMinutes() + duration);
 486 | 
 487 | 		const patientName = appointmentData.patient
 488 | 			? `${appointmentData.patient.firstName} ${appointmentData.patient.lastName}`
 489 | 			: "Unknown";
 490 | 		const eventType = mapAppointmentTypeToEventType(appointmentData.type);
 491 | 
 492 | 		return {
 493 | 			id: appointmentData.id,
 494 | 			title: `${patientName} - ${formatEventType(eventType)}`,
 495 | 			start: appointmentData.appointmentDate,
 496 | 			end: endTime,
 497 | 			allDay: false,
 498 | 			backgroundColor: getEventColor(eventType),
 499 | 			borderColor: getEventColor(eventType),
 500 | 			textColor: "#ffffff",
 501 | 			extendedProps: {
 502 | 				patientId: appointmentData.patientId,
 503 | 				patientName,
 504 | 				doctorId: appointmentData.doctorId || "",
 505 | 				doctorName: appointmentData.doctor?.name || "Unassigned",
 506 | 				type: eventType,
 507 | 				status: appointmentData.status || "SCHEDULED",
 508 | 				notes: appointmentData.note,
 509 | 				appointmentId: appointmentData.id
 510 | 			}
 511 | 		};
 512 | 	});
 513 | 
 514 | // Get calendar statistics - Using queries
 515 | export const getCalendarStats = clinicProcedure
 516 | 	.input(
 517 | 		z.object({
 518 | 			startDate: z.date(),
 519 | 			endDate: z.date(),
 520 | 			doctorId: z.string().optional()
 521 | 		})
 522 | 	)
 523 | 	.output(
 524 | 		z.object({
 525 | 			totalAppointments: z.number(),
 526 | 			completedAppointments: z.number(),
 527 | 			cancelledAppointments: z.number(),
 528 | 			noShowAppointments: z.number(),
 529 | 			averageDuration: z.number(),
 530 | 			busiestDay: z.string(),
 531 | 			appointmentsByType: z.record(z.string(), z.number()),
 532 | 			appointmentsByStatus: z.record(z.string(), z.number()),
 533 | 			dailyAverage: z.number()
 534 | 		})
 535 | 	)
 536 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 537 | 		const { startDate, endDate, doctorId } = input;
 538 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 539 | 
 540 | 		const appointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, startDate, endDate, doctorId);
 541 | 
 542 | 		const total = appointments.length;
 543 | 		const completed = appointments.filter(a => a.status === "COMPLETED").length;
 544 | 		const cancelled = appointments.filter(a => a.status === "CANCELLED").length;
 545 | 		const noShow = appointments.filter(a => a.status === "NO_SHOW").length;
 546 | 
 547 | 		const totalDuration = appointments.reduce((sum: number, a) => sum + (a.durationMinutes || 30), 0);
 548 | 		const avgDuration = total > 0 ? totalDuration / total : 0;
 549 | 
 550 | 		// Find busiest day
 551 | 		const dayCount = new Map<string, number>();
 552 | 		appointments.forEach(apt => {
 553 | 			const day = apt.appointmentDate.toLocaleDateString();
 554 | 			dayCount.set(day, (dayCount.get(day) || 0) + 1);
 555 | 		});
 556 | 
 557 | 		let busiestDay = "";
 558 | 		let maxCount = 0;
 559 | 		dayCount.forEach((count, day) => {
 560 | 			if (count > maxCount) {
 561 | 				maxCount = count;
 562 | 				busiestDay = day;
 563 | 			}
 564 | 		});
 565 | 
 566 | 		// Group by type and status
 567 | 		const appointmentsByType: Record<string, number> = {};
 568 | 		const appointmentsByStatus: Record<string, number> = {};
 569 | 
 570 | 		appointments.forEach(apt => {
 571 | 			const type = apt.type || "GENERAL";
 572 | 			const status = apt.status || "SCHEDULED";
 573 | 			appointmentsByType[type] = (appointmentsByType[type] || 0) + 1;
 574 | 			appointmentsByStatus[status] = (appointmentsByStatus[status] || 0) + 1;
 575 | 		});
 576 | 
 577 | 		const daysDiff = Math.ceil((endDate.getTime() - startDate.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
 578 | 		const dailyAverage = daysDiff > 0 ? total / daysDiff : 0;
 579 | 
 580 | 		return {
 581 | 			totalAppointments: total,
 582 | 			completedAppointments: completed,
 583 | 			cancelledAppointments: cancelled,
 584 | 			noShowAppointments: noShow,
 585 | 			averageDuration: avgDuration,
 586 | 			busiestDay,
 587 | 			appointmentsByType,
 588 | 			appointmentsByStatus,
 589 | 			dailyAverage
 590 | 		};
 591 | 	});
 592 | 
 593 | // ============================================================================
 594 | // Calendar Router Export
 595 | // ============================================================================
 596 | 
 597 | export const calendarRouter = {
 598 | 	getEvents: getCalendarEvents,
 599 | 	createEvent: createCalendarEvent,
 600 | 	updateEvent: updateCalendarEvent,
 601 | 	deleteEvent: deleteCalendarEvent,
 602 | 	bulkUpdate: bulkUpdateEvents,
 603 | 	getDoctorAvailability,
 604 | 	getAvailableTimeSlots,
 605 | 	getEventDetails,
 606 | 	getStats: getCalendarStats
 607 | };
 608 | function calculateAvailableSlots(
 609 | 	startTime: string,
 610 | 	endTime: string,
 611 | 	duration: number,
 612 | 	bookedSlots: Array<{ start: Date; duration: number }>
 613 | ): Array<{ start: Date; end: Date }> {
 614 | 	const slots: Array<{ start: Date; end: Date }> = [];
 615 | 	const [startHour, startMin] = startTime.split(":").map(Number);
 616 | 	const [endHour, endMin] = endTime.split(":").map(Number);
 617 | 
 618 | 	let current = new Date();
 619 | 	current.setHours(startHour ?? 0, startMin ?? 0, 0, 0);
 620 | 	const dayEnd = new Date();
 621 | 	dayEnd.setHours(endHour ?? 0, endMin ?? 0, 0, 0);
 622 | 
 623 | 	while (current.getTime() + duration * 60000 <= dayEnd.getTime()) {
 624 | 		const slotEnd = new Date(current.getTime() + duration * 60000);
 625 | 		const isBooked = bookedSlots.some(booked => {
 626 | 			const bookedEnd = new Date(booked.start.getTime() + booked.duration * 60000);
 627 | 			return current < bookedEnd && slotEnd > booked.start;
 628 | 		});
 629 | 
 630 | 		if (!isBooked) {
 631 | 			slots.push({ start: new Date(current), end: new Date(slotEnd) });
 632 | 		}
 633 | 
 634 | 		current = new Date(current.getTime() + duration * 60000);
 635 | 	}
 636 | 
 637 | 	return slots;
 638 | }
 639 | 
 640 | function getAvailableTimeSlotsAction(
 641 | 	startTime: string,
 642 | 	endTime: string,
 643 | 	duration: number,
 644 | 	bookedSlots: Array<{ start: Date; duration: number }>
 645 | ): Array<{ start: Date; end: Date }> {
 646 | 	return calculateAvailableSlots(startTime, endTime, duration, bookedSlots);
 647 | }
 648 | 
 649 | function formatEventType(eventType: string | null | undefined): string {
 650 | 	if (!eventType) return "General Visit";
 651 | 	return eventType
 652 | 		.split("-")
 653 | 		.map(word => word.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + word.slice(1))
 654 | 		.join(" ");
 655 | }
 656 | function getEventColor(eventType: string | null | undefined): string {
 657 | 	return getEventColorAction(eventType || "sick-visit");
 658 | }
 659 | function mapAppointmentTypeToEventType(type: string | null | undefined): string {
 660 | 	return type || "sick-visit";
 661 | }

```
