```ts
 179 | 	.input(z.object({ clinicId: z.string() }))
 180 | 	.output(z.any())
 181 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 182 | 		// Use db.query since there's no direct clinic member query yet
 183 | 		const members = await getUserWithAllRelationsAction(input.clinicId);
 184 | 
 185 | 		return members?.data?.clinicMemberships || [];
 186 | 	});
 187 | 
 188 | // Remove member from clinic
 189 | export const removeClinicMember = protectedProcedure
 190 | 	.input(z.object({ userId: z.string(), clinicId: z.string() }))
 191 | 	.output(z.object({ success: z.boolean(), message: z.string() }))
 192 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 193 | 		const deleted = await clinicRepo.deleteClinicMembers(input.userId);
 194 | 
 195 | 		if (deleted) {
 196 | 			// Clear user's clinicId if they're no longer a member
 197 | 			await updateUserAction(input.userId, { clinicId: null });
 198 | 		}
 199 | 
 200 | 		return { success: true, message: "Member removed successfully" };
 201 | 	});
 202 | 
 203 | // Get clinic settings
 204 | export const getClinicSettings = protectedProcedure
 205 | 	.input(z.object({ clinicId: z.string() }))
 206 | 	.output(z.any())
 207 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 208 | 		const settings = await clinicRepo.getFullClinic(input.clinicId);
 209 | 
 210 | 		return settings || null;
 211 | 	});
 212 | 
 213 | // Update clinic settings
 214 | export const updateClinicSettings = protectedProcedure
 215 | 	.input(
 216 | 		z.object({
 217 | 			clinicId: z.string(),
 218 | 			openingTime: z.string().optional(),
 219 | 			closingTime: z.string().optional(),
 220 | 			workingDays: z.string().optional(),
 221 | 			defaultAppointmentDuration: z.number().optional(),
 222 | 			requireEmergencyContact: z.boolean().optional()
 223 | 		})
 224 | 	)
 225 | 	.output(z.any())
 226 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 227 | 		const { clinicId, ...settingsData } = input;
 228 | 
 229 | 		// Get existing settings
 230 | 		const existingSettings = await clinicRepo.getFullClinic(clinicId);
 231 | 
 232 | 		if (!existingSettings) {
 233 | 			// Create new settings if none exist
 234 | 			const newSettings = await systemRepo.createClinicSetting({
 235 | 				id: crypto.randomUUID(),
 236 | 				clinicId,
 237 | 				openingTime: settingsData.openingTime || "09:00",
 238 | 				closingTime: settingsData.closingTime || "17:00",
 239 | 				workingDays: settingsData.workingDays || "MONDAY,TUESDAY,WEDNESDAY,THURSDAY,FRIDAY",
 240 | 				defaultAppointmentDuration: settingsData.defaultAppointmentDuration || 30,
 241 | 				requireEmergencyContact: settingsData.requireEmergencyContact ?? true
 242 | 			});
 243 | 			return newSettings;
 244 | 		}
 245 | 
 246 | 		// Update existing settings
 247 | 		const updatedSettings = await systemRepo.updateClinicSetting(existingSettings.id, settingsData);
 248 | 
 249 | 		return updatedSettings;
 250 | 	});
 251 | 
 252 | // Get clinic statistics for pediatrics
 253 | export const getClinicPediatricStats = protectedProcedure
 254 | 	.input(z.object({ clinicId: z.string(), patientId: z.string() }))
 255 | 	.output(
 256 | 		z.object({
 257 | 			totalPediatricPatients: z.number(),
 258 | 			patientsByAgeGroup: z.object({
 259 | 				infants: z.number(), // 0-12 months
 260 | 				toddlers: z.number(), // 1-3 years
 261 | 				preschoolers: z.number(), // 3-5 years
 262 | 				schoolAge: z.number(), // 5-12 years
 263 | 				adolescents: z.number() // 12-18 years
 264 | 			}),
 265 | 			vaccinationRate: z.number(),
 266 | 			completedWellnessVisits: z.number(),
 267 | 			pendingWellnessVisits: z.number(),
 268 | 			growthConcerns: z.number(),
 269 | 			developmentalDelays: z.number(),
 270 | 			nutritionalIssues: z.number()
 271 | 		})
 272 | 	)
 273 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 274 | 		const { clinicId, patientId } = input;
 275 | 
 276 | 		// Get all patients in clinic
 277 | 		const allPatients = await patientRepo.getPatientsByAgeRange(clinicId, 0, 216); // 0-18 years
 278 | 
 279 | 		// Categorize by age
 280 | 		const now = new Date();
 281 | 		const patientsByAgeGroup = {
 282 | 			infants: 0, // 0-12 months
 283 | 			toddlers: 0, // 1-3 years
 284 | 			preschoolers: 0, // 3-5 years
 285 | 			schoolAge: 0, // 5-12 years
 286 | 			adolescents: 0 // 12-18 years
 287 | 		};
 288 | 
 289 | 		for (const patient of allPatients) {
 290 | 			const ageInMonths = (now.getTime() - patient.dateOfBirth.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 30.44);
 291 | 
 292 | 			if (ageInMonths < 12) patientsByAgeGroup.infants++;
 293 | 			else if (ageInMonths < 36) patientsByAgeGroup.toddlers++;
 294 | 			else if (ageInMonths < 60) patientsByAgeGroup.preschoolers++;
 295 | 			else if (ageInMonths < 144) patientsByAgeGroup.schoolAge++;
 296 | 			else patientsByAgeGroup.adolescents++;
 297 | 		}
 298 | 
 299 | 		// Get vaccination statistics
 300 | 		const vaccineStatus = await pediatricRepo.getVaccineInventoryStatus(clinicId);
 301 | 
 302 | 		// Get growth and development concerns from medical records
 303 | 		const medicalRecords = (await medicalRepo.getPatientMedicalRecords(patientId, clinicId, 100, 0)) || [];
 304 | 
 305 | 		const growthConcerns = medicalRecords.filter(
 306 | 			(r: { notes: string | null }) =>
 307 | 				r.notes?.toLowerCase().includes("growth concern") ||
 308 | 				r.notes?.toLowerCase().includes("failure to thrive")
 309 | 		).length;
 310 | 
 311 | 		const developmentalDelays = medicalRecords.filter(
 312 | 			(r: { notes: string | null }) =>
 313 | 				r.notes?.toLowerCase().includes("developmental delay") ||
 314 | 				r.notes?.toLowerCase().includes("milestone delay")
 315 | 		).length;
 316 | 
 317 | 		const nutritionalIssues = medicalRecords.filter(
 318 | 			(r: { notes: string | null }) =>
 319 | 				r.notes?.toLowerCase().includes("malnutrition") || r.notes?.toLowerCase().includes("nutritional")
 320 | 		).length;
 321 | 
 322 | 		// Get wellness visit completion rate
 323 | 		const allAppointments = await appointmentRepo.getAllAppointments(clinicId);
 324 | 		const wellnessAppointments = allAppointments.filter(a => a.type === "WELLNESS" || a.type === "CHECKUP");
 325 | 		const completedWellnessVisits = wellnessAppointments.filter(a => a.status === "COMPLETED").length;
 326 | 		const pendingWellnessVisits = wellnessAppointments.filter(
 327 | 			a => a.status === "PENDING" || a.status === "CONFIRMED"
 328 | 		).length;
 329 | 
 330 | 		const vaccinationRate =
 331 | 			allPatients.length > 0
 332 | 				? (vaccineStatus.totalDoses / (allPatients.length * 10)) * 100 // Assuming ~10 vaccines per child
 333 | 				: 0;
 334 | 
 335 | 		return {
 336 | 			totalPediatricPatients: allPatients.length,
 337 | 			patientsByAgeGroup,
 338 | 			vaccinationRate: Math.min(vaccinationRate, 100),
 339 | 			completedWellnessVisits,
 340 | 			pendingWellnessVisits,
 341 | 			growthConcerns,
 342 | 			developmentalDelays,
 343 | 			nutritionalIssues
 344 | 		};
 345 | 	});
 346 | 
 347 | // Get clinic revenue report
 348 | export const getClinicRevenueReport = protectedProcedure
 349 | 	.input(
 350 | 		z.object({
 351 | 			clinicId: z.string(),
 352 | 			startDate: z.date(),
 353 | 			endDate: z.date(),
 354 | 			groupBy: z.enum(["day", "week", "month", "year"]).default("month")
 355 | 		})
 356 | 	)
 357 | 	.output(z.any())
 358 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 359 | 		const { clinicId, startDate, endDate } = input;
 360 | 
 361 | 		const analytics = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, startDate, endDate);
 362 | 
 363 | 		return {
 364 | 			period: { startDate, endDate },
 365 | 			totalRevenue: analytics.revenue.total,
 366 | 			revenueByMethod: analytics.revenue.byMethod,
 367 | 			averagePerAppointment: analytics.revenue.averagePerAppointment,
 368 | 			appointmentsCompleted: analytics.appointments.completed,
 369 | 			newPatients: analytics.patients.newPatients,
 370 | 			prescriptionsIssued: analytics.prescriptions
 371 | 		};
 372 | 	});
 373 | 
 374 | // Get doctor performance in clinic
 375 | export const getClinicDoctorPerformance = protectedProcedure
 376 | 	.input(
 377 | 		z.object({
 378 | 			clinicId: z.string(),
 379 | 			startDate: z.date(),
 380 | 			endDate: z.date(),
 381 | 			limit: z.number().default(10)
 382 | 		})
 383 | 	)
 384 | 	.output(z.any())
 385 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 386 | 		const { clinicId, startDate, endDate, limit } = input;
 387 | 
 388 | 		const doctors = await clinicRepo.getDoctorPerformanceReport(clinicId, startDate, endDate);
 389 | 
 390 | 		return doctors.slice(0, limit);
 391 | 	});
 392 | 
 393 | // Get popular services in clinic
 394 | export const getClinicPopularServices = protectedProcedure
 395 | 	.input(
 396 | 		z.object({
 397 | 			clinicId: z.string(),
 398 | 			startDate: z.date(),
 399 | 			endDate: z.date(),
 400 | 			limit: z.number().default(10)
 401 | 		})
 402 | 	)
 403 | 	.output(z.any())
 404 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 405 | 		const { clinicId, startDate, endDate, limit } = input;
 406 | 
 407 | 		const popularServices = await clinicRepo.getPopularServices(clinicId, limit, startDate, endDate);
 408 | 
 409 | 		return popularServices.slice(0, limit);
 410 | 	});
 411 | 
 412 | // Get clinic appointments by date range
 413 | export const getClinicAppointmentsByDateRange = protectedProcedure
 414 | 	.input(
 415 | 		z.object({
 416 | 			clinicId: z.string(),
 417 | 			startDate: z.date(),
 418 | 			endDate: z.date(),
 419 | 			doctorId: z.string().optional(),
 420 | 			status: z.string().optional()
 421 | 		})
 422 | 	)
 423 | 	.output(z.any())
 424 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 425 | 		const { clinicId, startDate, endDate, doctorId, status } = input;
 426 | 
 427 | 		const appointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, startDate, endDate, doctorId);
 428 | 
 429 | 		if (status) {
 430 | 			return appointments.filter(a => a.status === status);
 431 | 		}
 432 | 
 433 | 		return appointments;
 434 | 	});
 435 | 
 436 | // Export all procedures
 437 | export const clinicRouter = {
 438 | 	createClinic,
 439 | 	addClinicMember,
 440 | 	getClinicStats,
 441 | 	getClinicDetails,
 442 | 	updateClinic,
 443 | 	deleteClinic,
 444 | 	restoreClinic,
 445 | 	getClinicMembers,
 446 | 	removeClinicMember,
 447 | 	getClinicSettings,
 448 | 	updateClinicSettings,
 449 | 	getClinicPediatricStats,
 450 | 	getClinicRevenueReport,
 451 | 	getClinicDoctorPerformance,
 452 | 	getClinicPopularServices,
 453 | 	getClinicAppointmentsByDateRange
 454 | };

```

`routers/dashboard.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // lib/orpc/dashboard-procedures.ts
   2 | 
   3 | import { z } from "zod";
   4 | 
   5 | import { appointmentRepo, clinicRepo, patientRepo, pediatricRepo, systemRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   6 | import { calculatePatientSatisfaction, mapActionToActivity } from "@clinic/db/utils";
   7 | 
   8 | import { protectedProcedure } from "../index";
   9 | 
  10 | // Dashboard stats response type
  11 | export type DashboardStats = {
  12 | 	overview: {
  13 | 		totalPatients: number;
  14 | 		totalAppointments: number;
  15 | 		activeDoctors: number;
  16 | 		activeStaff: number;
  17 | 		occupancyRate: number;
  18 | 		pendingPrescriptionsCount: number;
  19 | 		lowStockItemsCount: number;
  20 | 		immunizationsDue: number;
  21 | 		immunizationsTrend: string;
  22 | 		growthMeasurements: number;
  23 | 		growthTrend: string;
  24 | 		todayAppointments: number;
  25 | 		appointmentsTrend: string;
  26 | 	};
  27 | 	today: {
  28 | 		appointments: number;
  29 | 		appointmentsList: Array<{
  30 | 			id: string;
  31 | 			time: string;
  32 | 			patientName: string;
  33 | 			doctorName: string;
  34 | 			status: string;
  35 | 		}>;
  36 | 		revenue: number;
  37 | 		completedAppointments: number;
  38 | 		cancelledAppointments: number;
  39 | 	};
  40 | 	weekly: {
  41 | 		appointmentsCount: number;
  42 | 		appointmentsByDay: Array<{
  43 | 			day: string;
  44 | 			count: number;
  45 | 			date: string;
  46 | 		}>;
  47 | 		newPatientsCount: number;
  48 | 		revenue: number;
  49 | 		topDoctors: Array<{
  50 | 			id: string;
  51 | 			name: string;
  52 | 			appointmentCount: number;
  53 | 			revenue: number;
  54 | 		}>;
  55 | 	};
  56 | 	monthly: {
  57 | 		appointmentsCount: number;
  58 | 		newPatientsCount: number;
  59 | 		revenue: number;
  60 | 		revenueTrend: Array<{
  61 | 			week: number;
  62 | 			revenue: number;
  63 | 			appointments: number;
  64 | 		}>;
  65 | 		averageWaitTime: number;
  66 | 		patientSatisfaction: number;
  67 | 		popularServices: Array<{
  68 | 			id: string;
  69 | 			name: string;
  70 | 			count: number;
  71 | 			revenue: number;
  72 | 		}>;
  73 | 	};
  74 | 	demographics: {
  75 | 		under18: number;
  76 | 		age18to30: number;
  77 | 		age31to50: number;
  78 | 		age51to70: number;
  79 | 		over70: number;
  80 | 	};
  81 | 	alerts: Array<{
  82 | 		id: string;
  83 | 		type: "warning" | "error" | "info";
  84 | 		title: string;
  85 | 		message: string;
  86 | 		timestamp: string;
  87 | 		action?: {
  88 | 			label: string;
  89 | 			href: string;
  90 | 		};
  91 | 	}>;
  92 | 	recentActivity: Array<{
  93 | 		id: string;
  94 | 		type: "appointment" | "patient" | "payment" | "prescription";
  95 | 		action: "created" | "updated" | "cancelled" | "completed";
  96 | 		description: string;
  97 | 		user: string;
  98 | 		timestamp: string;
  99 | 	}>;
 100 | };
 101 | 
 102 | // Base dashboard procedure (extends auth)
 103 | export const dashboardProcedure = protectedProcedure;
 104 | 
 105 | // ============================================
 106 | // Main Dashboard Stats
 107 | // ============================================
 108 | 
 109 | export const getDashboardStats = dashboardProcedure.handler(async ({ context }): Promise<DashboardStats> => {
 110 | 	const { user: ctxUser, clinicId } = context;
 111 | 	if (!clinicId) {
 112 | 		throw new Error("Clinic ID is required");
 113 | 	}
 114 | 
 115 | 	const today = new Date();
 116 | 	today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
 117 | 
 118 | 	const startOfMonth = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth(), 1);
 119 | 	const startOfWeek = new Date(today);
 120 | 	startOfWeek.setDate(today.getDate() - today.getDay());
 121 | 	startOfWeek.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
 122 | 
 123 | 	const endOfWeek = new Date(startOfWeek);
 124 | 	endOfWeek.setDate(startOfWeek.getDate() + 6);
 125 | 	endOfWeek.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
 126 | 
 127 | 	console.debug("Fetching dashboard stats", {
 128 | 		clinicId,
 129 | 		userId: ctxUser?.id,
 130 | 		dateRange: { startOfWeek, endOfWeek, startOfMonth }
 131 | 	});
 132 | 
 133 | 	try {
 134 | 		// Use the reporting queries for analytics
 135 | 		const analytics = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, startOfMonth, new Date());
 136 | 
 137 | 		// Get weekly appointments using appointment queries
 138 | 		const weeklyAppointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, startOfWeek, endOfWeek);
 139 | 
 140 | 		// Get monthly appointments
 141 | 		const monthlyAppointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, startOfMonth, new Date());
 142 | 
 143 | 		// Get popular services
 144 | 		const popularServices = await clinicRepo.getPopularServices(clinicId, 5, startOfMonth, new Date());
 145 | 
 146 | 		// Get doctor performance report
 147 | 		const doctorPerformance = await clinicRepo.getDoctorPerformanceReport(clinicId, startOfMonth, new Date());
 148 | 
 149 | 		// Get patients by age range for demographics (optimized for concurrency)
 150 | 		const [patientsUnder18, patients18to30, patients31to50, patients51to70, patientsOver70] = await Promise.all([
 151 | 			patientRepo.getPatientsByAgeRange(clinicId, 0, 216),
 152 | 			patientRepo.getPatientsByAgeRange(clinicId, 216, 360),
 153 | 			patientRepo.getPatientsByAgeRange(clinicId, 360, 600),
 154 | 			patientRepo.getPatientsByAgeRange(clinicId, 600, 840),
 155 | 			patientRepo.getPatientsByAgeRange(clinicId, 840, 1200)
 156 | 		]);
 157 | 
 158 | 		// Get pediatric specific stats for overview
 159 | 		const [inventoryStatus, overdueImmunizations, growthRecords] = await Promise.all([
 160 | 			pediatricRepo.getVaccineInventoryStatus(clinicId),
 161 | 			pediatricRepo.getOverdueImmunizations(clinicId),
 162 | 			pediatricRepo.getPatientGrowthRecords("", clinicId) // Empty patientId to get clinic-wide if supported, or filter analytics
 163 | 		]);
 164 | 
 165 | 		// Get today's appointments using appointment queries
 166 | 		const todayStart = new Date(today);
 167 | 		const todayEnd = new Date(today);
 168 | 		todayEnd.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
 169 | 
 170 | 		const todayAppointmentsList = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, todayStart, todayEnd);
 171 | 
 172 | 		// Calculate today's stats
 173 | 		const todayAppointments = todayAppointmentsList.filter(
 174 | 			apt => !["CANCELLED", "COMPLETED", "NO_SHOW"].includes(apt.status ?? "")
 175 | 		);
 176 | 		const todayCompletedAppointments = todayAppointmentsList.filter(apt => apt.status === "COMPLETED");
 177 | 		const todayCancelledAppointments = todayAppointmentsList.filter(apt => apt.status === "CANCELLED");
 178 | 
 179 | 		// Format appointments by day of week
 180 | 		const appointmentsByDay = weeklyAppointments.reduce(
 181 | 			(acc, apt) => {
 182 | 				const dayIndex = apt.appointmentDate.getDay();
 183 | 				const dayName = ["Sun", "Mon", "Tue", "Wed", "Thu", "Fri", "Sat"][dayIndex] ?? "Unknown";
 184 | 				const existing = acc.find(d => d.day === dayName);
 185 | 				if (existing) {
 186 | 					existing.count++;
 187 | 				} else {
 188 | 					acc.push({
 189 | 						day: dayName,
 190 | 						count: 1,
 191 | 						date: apt.appointmentDate.toISOString().split("T")[0] ?? ""
 192 | 					});
 193 | 				}
 194 | 				return acc;
 195 | 			},
 196 | 			[] as Array<{ day: string; count: number; date: string }>
 197 | 		);
 198 | 
 199 | 		// Format top doctors
 200 | 		const formattedTopDoctors = doctorPerformance
 201 | 			.map(doc => ({
 202 | 				id: doc.id,
 203 | 				name: doc.name,
 204 | 				appointmentCount: doc.totalAppointments,
 205 | 				revenue: doc.revenue
 206 | 			}))
 207 | 			.slice(0, 5);
 208 | 
 209 | 		// Format revenue trend by week
 210 | 		const revenueTrend = [];
 211 | 		const weeksInMonth = Math.ceil(new Date().getDate() / 7);
 212 | 		for (let week = 1; week <= weeksInMonth; week++) {
 213 | 			const weekStart = new Date(startOfMonth);
 214 | 			weekStart.setDate(weekStart.getDate() + (week - 1) * 7);
 215 | 			const weekEnd = new Date(weekStart);
 216 | 			weekEnd.setDate(weekEnd.getDate() + 6);
 217 | 
 218 | 			const weekRevenue = analytics.revenue.total; // Simplified - would need more granular data
 219 | 			revenueTrend.push({
 220 | 				week,
 221 | 				revenue: weekRevenue / weeksInMonth,
 222 | 				appointments: Math.round(analytics.appointments.total / weeksInMonth)
 223 | 			});
 224 | 		}
 225 | 
 226 | 		// Format popular services
 227 | 		const formattedPopularServices = popularServices.map(service => ({
 228 | 			id: service.id,
 229 | 			name: service.name,
 230 | 			count: service.totalUsage,
 231 | 			revenue: service.price * service.totalUsage
 232 | 		}));
 233 | 
 234 | 		// Create alerts
 235 | 		const alerts: DashboardStats["alerts"] = [];
 236 | 
 237 | 		// Check for pending/expiring prescriptions
 238 | 		if (analytics.prescriptions > 0) {
 239 | 			alerts.push({
 240 | 				id: "pending-prescriptions",
 241 | 				type: "warning",
 242 | 				title: "Active Prescriptions",
 243 | 				message: `${analytics.prescriptions} active prescriptions need attention.`,
 244 | 				timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
 245 | 				action: {
 246 | 					label: "Review Prescriptions",
 247 | 					href: "/prescriptions/pending"
 248 | 				}
 249 | 			});
 250 | 		}
 251 | 
 252 | 		// Check for low patient engagement
 253 | 		const lowEngagementPatients = analytics.appointments.completed < 10 ? 1 : 0;
 254 | 		if (lowEngagementPatients > 0) {
 255 | 			alerts.push({
 256 | 				id: "low-engagement",
 257 | 				type: "info",
 258 | 				title: "Low Patient Engagement",
 259 | 				message: `${lowEngagementPatients} patients haven't visited in over 3 months.`,
 260 | 				timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
 261 | 				action: {
 262 | 					label: "View Patients",
 263 | 					href: "/patients?status=inactive"
 264 | 				}
 265 | 			});
 266 | 		}
 267 | 
 268 | 		// Format recent activity from appointments
 269 | 		const recentAppointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(
 270 | 			clinicId,
 271 | 			new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000),
 272 | 			new Date()
 273 | 		);
 274 | 
 275 | 		const formattedRecentActivity: DashboardStats["recentActivity"] = recentAppointments.slice(0, 10).map(apt => ({
 276 | 			id: apt.id,
 277 | 			type: "appointment" as const,
 278 | 			action: mapActionToActivity(apt.status ?? "updated"),
 279 | 			description: `Appointment for ${apt.patient?.firstName ?? "Patient"} ${apt.patient?.lastName ?? ""} with Dr. ${apt.doctor?.name ?? "Doctor"}`,
 280 | 			user: apt.doctor?.name ?? "System",
 281 | 			timestamp: apt.updatedAt.toISOString()
 282 | 		}));
 283 | 
 284 | 		// Calculate occupancy rate
 285 | 		const occupancyRate =
 286 | 			analytics.appointments.completed > 0 && analytics.appointments.total > 0
 287 | 				? Math.min(100, Math.round((analytics.appointments.completed / analytics.appointments.total) * 100))
 288 | 				: 0;
 289 | 
 290 | 		console.info("Dashboard stats fetched successfully", {
 291 | 			clinicId,
 292 | 			totalPatients: analytics.patients.total,
 293 | 			todayAppointments: todayAppointments.length,
 294 | 			monthlyRevenue: analytics.revenue.total
 295 | 		});
 296 | 
 297 | 		return {
 298 | 			overview: {
 299 | 				totalPatients: analytics.patients.total,
 300 | 				totalAppointments: analytics.appointments.total,
 301 | 				activeDoctors: doctorPerformance.length,
 302 | 				activeStaff: doctorPerformance.length, // Would need staff query
 303 | 				occupancyRate,
 304 | 				pendingPrescriptionsCount: analytics.prescriptions,
 305 | 				lowStockItemsCount: inventoryStatus?.lowStock?.length ?? 0,
 306 | 				immunizationsDue: overdueImmunizations.length,
 307 | 				immunizationsTrend: "+5%",
 308 | 				growthMeasurements: growthRecords.length,
 309 | 				growthTrend: "+10%",
 310 | 				todayAppointments: todayAppointments.length,
 311 | 				appointmentsTrend: "+8%"
 312 | 			},
 313 | 			today: {
 314 | 				appointments: todayAppointments.length,
 315 | 				appointmentsList: todayAppointments.map(apt => ({
 316 | 					id: apt.id,
 317 | 					time: apt.appointmentDate.toLocaleTimeString(),
 318 | 					patientName: apt.patient ? `${apt.patient.firstName} ${apt.patient.lastName}` : "Unknown",
 319 | 					doctorName: apt.doctor?.name ?? "Unknown",
 320 | 					status: apt.status ?? "SCHEDULED"
 321 | 				})),
 322 | 				revenue: analytics.revenue.total / 30, // Approximate daily revenue
 323 | 				completedAppointments: todayCompletedAppointments.length,
 324 | 				cancelledAppointments: todayCancelledAppointments.length
 325 | 			},
 326 | 			weekly: {
 327 | 				appointmentsCount: weeklyAppointments.length,
 328 | 				appointmentsByDay,
 329 | 				newPatientsCount: analytics.patients.newPatients,
 330 | 				revenue: analytics.revenue.total / 4, // Approximate weekly revenue
 331 | 				topDoctors: formattedTopDoctors
 332 | 			},
 333 | 			monthly: {
 334 | 				appointmentsCount: monthlyAppointments.length,
 335 | 				newPatientsCount: analytics.patients.newPatients,
 336 | 				revenue: analytics.revenue.total,
 337 | 				revenueTrend,
 338 | 				averageWaitTime: 15, // Would need actual wait time data
 339 | 				patientSatisfaction: calculatePatientSatisfaction(),
 340 | 				popularServices: formattedPopularServices
 341 | 			},
 342 | 			demographics: {
 343 | 				under18: patientsUnder18.length,
 344 | 				age18to30: patients18to30.length,
 345 | 				age31to50: patients31to50.length,
 346 | 				age51to70: patients51to70.length,
 347 | 				over70: patientsOver70.length
 348 | 			},
 349 | 			alerts,
 350 | 			recentActivity: formattedRecentActivity
 351 | 		};
 352 | 	} catch (error) {

 354 | 		throw error;
 355 | 	}

 362 | export const getRecentAppointments = dashboardProcedure
 363 | 	.input(
 364 | 		z.object({
 365 | 			limit: z.number().int().min(1).max(50).default(10),
 366 | 			status: z.enum(["CONFIRMED", "PENDING", "COMPLETED", "CANCELLED", "NO_SHOW"]).optional()
 367 | 		})
 368 | 	)
 369 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 370 | 		const { clinicId } = context;
 371 | 
 372 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 373 | 			throw new Error("Clinic ID is required");
 374 | 		}
 375 | 
 376 | 		const endDate = new Date();
 377 | 		const startDate = new Date();
 378 | 		startDate.setDate(startDate.getDate() - 30);
 379 | 
 380 | 		const appointments = await appointmentRepo.getAppointmentsInRange(clinicId, startDate, endDate);
 381 | 
 382 | 		const filteredAppointments = input.status
 383 | 			? appointments.filter(apt => apt.status === input.status)
 384 | 			: appointments;
 385 |

 389 | export const getRevenueOverview = dashboardProcedure
 390 | 	.input(
 391 | 		z.object({
 392 | 			startDate: z.coerce.date(),
 393 | 			endDate: z.coerce.date(),
 394 | 			groupBy: z.enum(["day", "week", "month"]).default("day")
 395 | 		})
 396 | 	)
 397 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 398 | 		const { clinicId } = context;
 399 | 		const { startDate, endDate } = input;
 400 | 
 401 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 402 | 			throw new Error("Clinic ID is required");
 403 | 		}
 404 | 
 405 | 		const analytics = await systemRepo.getClinicAnalytics(clinicId, startDate, endDate);
 406 | 
 407 | 		// Format revenue data based on groupBy
 408 | 		const revenueData = [];
 409 | 		const daysDiff = Math.ceil((endDate.getTime() - startDate.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
 410 | 
 411 | 		if (input.groupBy === "day") {
 412 | 			for (let i = 0; i <= daysDiff; i++) {
 413 | 				const date = new Date(startDate);
 414 | 				date.setDate(date.getDate() + i);
 415 | 				revenueData.push({
 416 | 					period: date.toISOString().split("T")[0] ?? "",
 417 | 					total: analytics.revenue.total / daysDiff,
 418 | 					count: Math.round(analytics.appointments.total / daysDiff),
 419 | 					average: analytics.revenue.averagePerAppointment
 420 | 				});
 421 | 			}
 422 | 		} else if (input.groupBy === "week") {
 423 | 			const weeksInRange = Math.ceil(daysDiff / 7);
 424 | 			for (let week = 1; week <= weeksInRange; week++) {
 425 | 				revenueData.push({
 426 | 					period: `Week ${week}`,
 427 | 					total: analytics.revenue.total / weeksInRange,
 428 | 					count: Math.round(analytics.appointments.total / weeksInRange),
 429 | 					average: analytics.revenue.averagePerAppointment
 430 | 				});
 431 | 			}
 432 | 		} else {
 433 | 			// month
 434 | 			revenueData.push({
 435 | 				period: startDate.toLocaleString("default", {
 436 | 					month: "long",
 437 | 					year: "numeric"
 438 | 				}),
 439 | 				total: analytics.revenue.total,
 440 | 				count: analytics.appointments.total,
 441 | 				average: analytics.revenue.averagePerAppointment
 442 | 			});
 443 | 		}
 444 | 
 445 | 		return {
 446 | 			revenue: revenueData,
 447 | 			summary: {
 448 | 				total: analytics.revenue.total,
 449 | 				transactionCount: analytics.appointments.completed,
 450 | 				averageTransaction: analytics.revenue.averagePerAppointment
 451 | 			}
 452 | 		};
 453 | 	});
 454 | 
 455 | export const getPatientDemographics = dashboardProcedure.handler(async ({ context }) => {
 456 | 	const { clinicId } = context;
 457 | 
 458 | 	if (!clinicId) {
 459 | 		throw new Error("Clinic ID is required");
 460 | 	}
 461 | 
 462 | 	// Get patients by age groups
 463 | 	const ageGroups = [
 464 | 		{ name: "0-17", minMonths: 0, maxMonths: 216 },
 465 | 		{ name: "18-30", minMonths: 216, maxMonths: 360 },
 466 | 		{ name: "31-50", minMonths: 360, maxMonths: 600 },
 467 | 		{ name: "51-70", minMonths: 600, maxMonths: 840 },
 468 | 		{ name: "70+", minMonths: 840, maxMonths: 1200 }
 469 | 	];
 470 | 
 471 | 	const ageGroupData = await Promise.all(
 472 | 		ageGroups.map(async group => {
 473 | 			const patients = await patientRepo.getPatientsByAgeRange(clinicId, group.minMonths, group.maxMonths);
 474 | 			return {
 475 | 				age_group: group.name,
 476 | 				count: patients.length
 477 | 			};
 478 | 		})
 479 | 	);
 480 | 
 481 | 	// Get gender distribution
 482 | 	const allPatients = await patientRepo.getPatientsByAgeRange(clinicId, 0, 1200);
 483 | 	const genderDistribution = allPatients.reduce(
 484 | 		(acc, patient) => {
 485 | 			const gender = patient.gender ?? "OTHER";
 486 | 			acc[gender] = (acc[gender] || 0) + 1;
 487 | 			return acc;
 488 | 		},
 489 | 		{} as Record<string, number>
 490 | 	);
 491 | 
 492 | 	const genderData = Object.entries(genderDistribution).map(([gender, count]) => ({
 493 | 		gender,
 494 | 		count
 495 | 	}));
 496 | 
 497 | 	// Get top locations from patient addresses
 498 | 	const locations = allPatients
 499 | 		.filter(p => p.address)
 500 | 		.reduce(
 501 | 			(acc, patient) => {
 502 | 				const city = patient.address?.split(",")[1]?.trim() || "Unknown";
 503 | 				acc[city] = (acc[city] || 0) + 1;
 504 | 				return acc;
 505 | 			},
 506 | 			{} as Record<string, number>
 507 | 		);
 508 | 
 509 | 	const topLocations = Object.entries(locations)
 510 | 		.map(([address, count]) => ({ address, count }))
 511 | 		.sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
 512 | 		.slice(0, 10);
 513 | 
 514 | 	return {
 515 | 		ageGroups: ageGroupData,
 516 | 		genderDistribution: genderData,
 517 | 		topLocations
 518 | 	};
 519 | });

 521 | export const getDoctorPerformance = dashboardProcedure
 522 | 	.input(
 523 | 		z.object({
 524 | 			period: z.enum(["week", "month", "year"]).default("month"),
 525 | 			doctorId: z.string().optional()
 526 | 		})
 527 | 	)
 528 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 529 | 		const { clinicId } = context;
 530 | 
 531 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 532 | 			throw new Error("Clinic ID is required");
 533 | 		}
 534 | 
 535 | 		const { period, doctorId } = input;
 536 | 
 537 | 		const startDate = new Date();
 538 | 		switch (period) {
 539 | 			case "week":
 540 | 				startDate.setDate(startDate.getDate() - 7);
 541 | 				break;
 542 | 			case "month":
 543 | 				startDate.setMonth(startDate.getMonth() - 1);
 544 | 				break;
 545 | 			case "year":
 546 | 				startDate.setFullYear(startDate.getFullYear() - 1);
 547 | 				break;
 548 | 		}
 549 | 
 550 | 		const doctorPerformance = await clinicRepo.getDoctorPerformanceReport(clinicId, startDate, new Date());
 551 | 
 552 | 		const filteredPerformance = doctorId ? doctorPerformance.filter(d => d.id === doctorId) : doctorPerformance;
 553 | 
 554 | 		return filteredPerformance.map(performance => ({
 555 | 			id: performance.id,
 556 | 			name: performance.name,
 557 | 			specialization: performance.specialty,
 558 | 			totalAppointments: performance.totalAppointments,
 559 | 			totalRevenue: performance.revenue,
 560 | 			averageRating: performance.averageRating,
 561 | 			reviewCount: Math.round(performance.averageRating * 10), // Approximate
 562 | 			uniquePatients: Math.round(performance.totalAppointments * 0.8), // Approximate
 563 | 			completionRate: performance.completionRate
 564 | 		}));
 565 | 	});

 576 | 	)

 581 | 			throw new Error("Clinic ID is required");

 586 | 		startDate.setMonth(startDate.getMonth() - input.months);
 587 | 
 588 | 		const monthlyTrends = [];
 589 | 
 590 | 		for (let i = 0; i < input.months; i++) {
 591 | 			const monthStart = new Date(startDate);
 592 | 			monthStart.setMonth(monthStart.getMonth() + i);
 593 | 			const monthEnd = new Date(monthStart);
 594 | 			monthEnd.setMonth(monthEnd.getMonth() + 1);
 595 | 			monthEnd.setDate(0);
 596 |

 598 |

 605 | 				revenue: analytics.revenue.total,
 606 | 				newPatients: analytics.patients.newPatients
 607 | 			});
 608 | 		}
```

```ts
  94 | // Create doctor
  95 | export const createDoctor = protectedProcedure
  96 | 	.input(DoctorCreateSchema)
  97 | 	.output(DoctorSchema)
  98 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  99 | 		const userId = context.user?.id;
 100 | 		if (!userId) {
 101 | 			throw new Error("Unauthorized");
 102 | 		}
 103 | 
 104 | 		const userRecord = await context.db.query.user.findFirst({
 105 | 			where: { id: userId }
 106 | 		});
 107 | 
 108 | 		if (

 110 | 			(userRecord.role !== "admin" && userRecord.role !== "superadmin" && userRecord.role !== "staff")

 113 | 		}

 275 | 			clinicId: z.string().optional(),
 276 | 			sortBy: z.enum(["name", "createdAt", "rating", "specialty"]).default("createdAt"),
 277 | 			sortOrder: z.enum(["asc", "desc"]).default("desc")
 278 | 		})
 279 | 	)
 280 | 	.output(
 281 | 		z.object({
 282 | 			doctors: z.array(DoctorSchema),
 283 | 			total: z.number(),
 284 | 			page: z.number(),
 285 | 			limit: z.number(),
 286 | 			totalPages: z.number()
 287 | 		})
 288 | 	)
 289 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 290 | 		const {
 291 | 			page,
 292 | 			limit,
 293 | 			offset: manualOffset,
 294 | 			search,
 295 | 			status,
 296 | 			isActive,
 297 | 			specialty,
 298 | 			clinicId: inputClinicId,
 299 | 			sortBy,
 300 | 			sortOrder
 301 | 		} = input;
 302 | 		const clinicId = inputClinicId ?? context.clinicId ?? "";
 303 | 
 304 | 		const doctors = await context.db.query.doctor.findMany({
 305 | 			where: {
 306 | 				clinicId,
 307 | 				isDeleted: false,
 308 | 				...(status && { status }),
 309 | 				...(isActive !== undefined && { isActive }),
 310 | 				...(specialty && { specialty }),
 311 | 				...(search && {
 312 | 					OR: [{ name: { ilike: `%${search}%` } }, { specialty: { ilike: `%${search}%` } }]
 313 | 				})
 314 | 			},
 315 | 			orderBy: (table, { asc, desc }) => [sortOrder === "asc" ? asc(table[sortBy]) : desc(table[sortBy])]
 316 | 		});
 317 | 
 318 | 		const total = doctors.length;
 319 | 		const start = manualOffset ?? (page - 1) * limit;
 320 | 		const paginated = doctors.slice(start, start + limit);
 321 | 
 322 | 		return {
 323 | 			doctors: paginated.map(d => ({
 324 | 				...d,
 325 | 				createdAt: d.createdAt,
 326 | 				updatedAt: d.updatedAt,
 327 | 				deletedAt: d.deletedAt
 328 | 			})),
 329 | 			total,
 330 | 			page,
 331 | 			limit,
 332 | 			totalPages: Math.ceil(total / limit)
 333 | 		};
 334 | 	});
 335 | 
 336 | // Get doctors by specialty
 337 | export const getDoctorsBySpecialty = protectedProcedure
 338 | 	.input(
 339 | 		z.object({
 340 | 			specialty: z.string(),
 341 | 			clinicId: z.string().optional()
 342 | 		})
 343 | 	)
 344 | 	.output(z.array(DoctorSchema))
 345 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }): Promise<DbDoctor[]> => {
 346 | 		const clinicId = input.clinicId ?? context.clinicId ?? "";
 347 | 		const doctors = await context.db.query.doctor.findMany({
 348 | 			where: { clinicId, specialty: input.specialty, isDeleted: false },
 349 | 			orderBy: { name: "asc" }
 350 | 		});
 351 | 
 352 | 		return doctors;
 353 | 	});
 354 | 
 355 | // Get doctor statistics
 356 | // Get doctor statistics
 357 | export const getDoctorStatistics = protectedProcedure
 358 | 	.input(
 359 | 		z.object({
 360 | 			doctorId: z.string(),
 361 | 			startDate: z.date().optional(),
 362 | 			endDate: z.date().optional()
 363 | 		})
 364 | 	)
 365 | 	.output(
 366 | 		z.object({
 367 | 			totalAppointments: z.number(),
 368 | 			completedAppointments: z.number(),
 369 | 			cancelledAppointments: z.number(),
 370 | 			averageRating: z.number().nullable(),
 371 | 			totalPatients: z.number(),
 372 | 			totalRevenue: z.number(),
 373 | 			upcomingAppointments: z.number()
 374 | 		})
 375 | 	)

 380 | 			startDate ?? new Date(0),
 381 | 			endDate ?? new Date(),
 382 | 			context.clinicId ?? ""
 383 | 		);
 384 | 
 385 | 		// Map the performance query results to match the expected output schema
 386 | 		return {
 387 | 			totalAppointments: performance.totalAppointments,
 388 | 			completedAppointments: performance.completedAppointments,
 389 | 			cancelledAppointments: performance.cancelledAppointments,
 390 | 			averageRating: performance.averageRating,
 391 | 			totalRevenue: performance.totalRevenue,
 392 | 			totalPatients: 0, // Fallback as query doesn't provide this
 393 | 			upcomingAppointments: 0 // Fallback as query doesn't provide this
 394 | 		};
 395 | 	});
 396 | 
 397 | // Bulk update doctor status
 398 | export const bulkUpdateDoctorStatus = protectedProcedure
 399 | 	.input(
 400 | 		z.object({
 401 | 			doctorIds: z.array(z.string()),
 402 | 			isActive: z.boolean(),
 403 | 			status: z
 404 | 				.enum(["ACTIVE", "INACTIVE", "PENDING", "SUSPENDED", "COMPLETED", "CANCELLED", "EXPIRED", "ON_HOLD"])
 405 | 				.optional()
 406 | 		})
 407 | 	)
 408 | 	.output(z.object({ updatedCount: z.number() }))
 409 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {

 411 | 			isActive: input.isActive,
 412 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId,
 413 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
 414 | 		};

 417 | 			updateData.status = input.status as Status;
 418 | 		}
 419 | 		const result = await doctorRepo.updateManyDoctors(input.doctorIds, updateData);
 420 | 		return { updatedCount: result.length };

```

`routers/encounter.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import z from "zod";
   2 | 
   3 | import { medicalRepo, pharmacyRepo, systemRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   4 | import { DiagnosisCreateSchema, DiagnosisSchema, DiagnosisUpdateSchema } from "@clinic/db/zod";
   5 | import { o, protectedProcedure } from "../index";
   6 | import { AddPrescriptionSchema, AddVitalSignsSchema, CompleteEncounterSchema, ListEncountersSchema } from "../types";
   7 | import { LabTestSchema } from "./labTest.server";
   8 | 
   9 | // Create a new encounter
  10 | export const createEncounter = protectedProcedure
  11 | 	.input(DiagnosisCreateSchema)
  12 | 	.output(DiagnosisSchema)
  13 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  14 | 		const clinicId = input.clinicId ?? context.clinicId ?? "";
  15 | 
  16 | 		const result = await medicalRepo.createMedicalRecord({
  17 | 			id: crypto.randomUUID(),
  18 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
  19 | 			doctorId: input.doctorId,
  20 | 			clinicId,
  21 | 			appointmentId: input.appointmentId ?? "",
  22 | 			diagnosis: input.diagnosis ?? "",
  23 | 			symptoms: input.symptoms ?? "",
  24 | 			treatmentPlan: input.treatment ?? ""
  25 | 		});
  26 | 
  27 | 		const record = await medicalRepo.getEncounterById(
  28 | 			typeof result?.diagnosis === "object" && result.diagnosis !== null && "id" in result.diagnosis
  29 | 				? (result.diagnosis as { id: string }).id
  30 | 				: typeof result?.diagnosis === "string"
  31 | 					? result.diagnosis
  32 | 					: "",
  33 | 			clinicId
  34 | 		);
  35 | 		if (!record) {
  36 | 			throw new Error("Failed to create encounter");
  37 | 		}
  38 | 		return record;
  39 | 	});
  40 | 
  41 | // Update an encounter
  42 | export const updateEncounter = protectedProcedure
  43 | 	.input(DiagnosisUpdateSchema)
  44 | 	.output(DiagnosisSchema)
  45 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  46 | 		if (!input.id) {
  47 | 			throw new Error("Encounter ID is required for update");
  48 | 		}
  49 | 
  50 | 		const updated = await medicalRepo.updateDiagnosis(input.id, {
  51 | 			...input,
  52 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId,
  53 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
  54 | 		});
  55 | 
  56 | 		if (!updated) {
  57 | 			throw new Error("Encounter not found");
  58 | 		}
  59 | 
  60 | 		return updated;
  61 | 	});
  62 | 
  63 | // Complete an encounter with full medical details
  64 | export const completeEncounter = protectedProcedure
  65 | 	.input(CompleteEncounterSchema)
  66 | 	.output(z.object({ success: z.boolean(), encounter: DiagnosisSchema }))
  67 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  68 | 		const encounter = await medicalRepo.updateDiagnosis(input.encounterId, {
  69 | 			diagnosis: input.diagnosis,
  70 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId,
  71 | 			treatment: input.treatment,
  72 | 			notes: input.notes,
  73 | 			followUpPlan: input.followUpDate ? `Follow up on ${input.followUpDate.toISOString()}` : null,
  74 | 			prescribedMedications: input.medications ? JSON.stringify(input.medications) : null,
  75 | 			status: "COMPLETED",
  76 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
  77 | 		});
  78 | 
  79 | 		if (!encounter) {
  80 | 			throw new Error("Encounter not found");
  81 | 		}
  82 | 
  83 | 		// Update related medical record
  84 | 		if (encounter.medicalId) {
  85 | 			await medicalRepo.updateMedicalRecord(encounter.medicalId, {
  86 | 				diagnosis: input.diagnosis,
  87 | 				treatmentPlan: input.treatment,
  88 | 				status: "COMPLETED"
  89 | 			});
  90 | 		}
  91 | 
  92 | 		return { success: true, encounter };
  93 | 	});
  94 | 
  95 | // Add prescription to encounter
  96 | export const addPrescription = protectedProcedure
  97 | 	.input(AddPrescriptionSchema)
  98 | 	.output(z.object({ id: z.string(), success: z.boolean() }))
  99 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 100 | 		const prescriptionRecord = await pharmacyRepo.createPrescription({
 101 | 			medicalRecordId: input.encounterId,
 102 | 			doctorId: input.doctorId,
 103 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 104 | 			encounterId: input.encounterId,
 105 | 			medicationName: input.medicationName,
 106 | 			instructions: input.instructions,
 107 | 			issuedDate: input.issuedDate,
 108 | 			endDate: input.endDate ?? undefined,
 109 | 			status: input.status as "active" | "completed" | "cancelled" | "expired" | "on_hold",
 110 | 			clinicId: "",
 111 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
 112 | 			updatedAt: new Date(),
 113 | 			id: crypto.randomUUID()
 114 | 		});
 115 | 
 116 | 		// Update encounter with prescribed medications
 117 | 		const encounter = await medicalRepo.getEncounterById(input.encounterId, context.clinicId ?? "");
 118 | 
 119 | 		if (encounter) {
 120 | 			const existingMeds = encounter.prescribedMedications ? JSON.parse(encounter.prescribedMedications) : [];
 121 | 			const newMeds = [...existingMeds, { name: input.medicationName, instructions: input.instructions }];
 122 | 			await medicalRepo.updateDiagnosis(input.encounterId, {
 123 | 				prescribedMedications: JSON.stringify(newMeds)
 124 | 			});
 125 | 		}
 126 | 
 127 | 		return { id: prescriptionRecord?.id ?? "", success: true };
 128 | 	});

 315 | export const getEncountersByDateRange = protectedProcedure

 331 | 		});

 352 | // Get encounter statistics
 353 | export const getEncounterStats = protectedProcedure
 354 | 	.input(
 355 | 		z.object({
 356 | 			clinicId: z.string().optional(),
 357 | 			doctorId: z.string().optional(),
 358 | 			startDate: z.date().optional(),
 359 | 			endDate: z.date().optional()
 360 | 		})
 361 | 	)
 362 | 	.output(
 363 | 		z.object({
 364 | 			totalEncounters: z.number(),
 365 | 			activeEncounters: z.number(),
 366 | 			completedEncounters: z.number(),
 367 | 			avgPerDay: z.number(),
 368 | 			topDiagnosis: z.array(
 369 | 				z.object({
 370 | 					diagnosis: z.string(),
 371 | 					count: z.number()
 372 | 				})
 373 | 			),
 374 | 			encountersByType: z.array(
 375 | 				z.object({
 376 | 					type: z.string(),
 377 | 					count: z.number()
 378 | 				})
 379 | 			)
 380 | 		})
 381 | 	)
 382 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 383 | 		const allEncounters = await context.db.query.diagnosis.findMany({
 384 | 			where: {
 385 | 				clinicId: input.clinicId ?? context.clinicId ?? "",
 386 | 				isDeleted: false,
 387 | 				...(input.doctorId && { doctorId: input.doctorId })
 388 | 			}
 389 | 		});
 390 | 
 391 | 		const totalEncounters = allEncounters.length;
 392 | 		const activeEncounters = allEncounters.filter(e => e.status === "ACTIVE").length;
 393 | 		const completedEncounters = allEncounters.filter(e => e.status === "COMPLETED").length;
 394 | 
 395 | 		// Calculate average per day
 396 | 		const dates = allEncounters.map(e => e.date.toDateString());
 397 | 		const uniqueDates = new Set(dates);
 398 | 		const avgPerDay = uniqueDates.size > 0 ? totalEncounters / uniqueDates.size : 0;
 399 | 
 400 | 		// Get top diagnoses
 401 | 		const diagnosisCounts = new Map<string, number>();
 402 | 		for (const encounter of allEncounters) {
 403 | 			if (encounter.diagnosis) {
 404 | 				diagnosisCounts.set(encounter.diagnosis, (diagnosisCounts.get(encounter.diagnosis) ?? 0) + 1);
 405 | 			}
 406 | 		}
 407 | 		const topDiagnosis = Array.from(diagnosisCounts.entries())
 408 | 			.map(([diagnosis, count]) => {
 409 | 				return { diagnosis, count };
 410 | 			})
 411 | 			.sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
 412 | 			.slice(0, 5);
 413 | 
 414 | 		// Get encounters by type
 415 | 		const typeCounts = new Map<string, number>();
 416 | 		for (const diagnosis of allEncounters) {
 417 | 			typeCounts.set(diagnosis.type ?? "", (typeCounts.get(diagnosis.type ?? "") ?? 0) + 1);
 418 | 		}
 419 | 		const encountersByType = Array.from(typeCounts.entries()).map(([type, count]) => {
 420 | 			return {
 421 | 				type,
 422 | 				count
 423 | 			};
 424 | 		});
 425 | 
 426 | 		return {
 427 | 			totalEncounters,
 428 | 			activeEncounters,
 429 | 			completedEncounters,
 430 | 			avgPerDay,
 431 | 			topDiagnosis,
 432 | 			encountersByType
 433 | 		};
 434 | 	});
 435 | 
 436 | export const encounterRouter = o.router({
 437 | 	create: createEncounter,
 438 | 	update: updateEncounter,
 439 | 	complete: completeEncounter,
 440 | 	addPrescription,
 441 | 	addVitalSigns,
 442 | 	get: getEncounter,
 443 | 	list: listEncounters,
 444 | 	delete: deleteEncounter,
 445 | 	getEncountersByDateRange,
 446 | 	getEncounterStats
 447 | });

```

`routers/growth.server.ts`:

```ts
   7 | // Get patient growth history
   8 | export const getPatientGrowthHistory = protectedProcedure
   9 | 	.input(
  10 | 		z.object({
  11 | 			patientId: z.string(),
  12 | 			limit: z.number().optional().default(50),
  13 | 			offset: z.number().optional().default(0)
  14 | 		})
  15 | 	)
  16 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {

  19 | 			input.patientId,
  20 | 			context.clinicId ?? ""
  21 | 		);
  22 | 
  23 | 		if (!growthWithPercentiles) {

  26 | 				total: 0,
  27 | 				limit: input.limit,
  28 | 				offset: input.offset
  29 | 			};
  30 | 		}

  34 | 
  35 | 		return {
  36 | 			records: paginatedRecords,
  37 | 			total: growthWithPercentiles.length,
  38 | 			limit: input.limit,
  39 | 			offset: input.offset
  40 | 		};
  41 | 	});

  43 | // Record growth measurement - Using existing mutation

  47 | 			patientId: z.string(),

  52 | 			notes: z.string().optional()

  58 | 
  59 | 		if (!patientData) {
  60 | 			throw new Error("Patient not found");
  61 | 		}

  63 | 		if (!patientData.gender) {
  64 | 			throw new Error("Patient gender is required");
  65 | 		}
  66 | 
  67 | 		// Calculate BMI if both weight and height are provided

  70 | 			const heightInMeters = input.height / 100;
  71 | 			bmi = Number.parseFloat((input.weight / (heightInMeters * heightInMeters)).toFixed(1));
  72 | 		}

  82 | 			bmi,
  83 | 			notes: input.notes
  84 | 		});
  85 | 
  86 | 		return growthRecord;
  87 | 	});
  88 | 
  89 | // Get growth chart data
  90 | export const getGrowthChart = protectedProcedure
  91 | 	.input(
  92 | 		z.object({
  93 | 			patientId: z.string(),
  94 | 			measurementType: z.enum(["WEIGHT", "HEIGHT", "BMI", "HEAD_CIRCUMFERENCE"]),
  95 | 			fromDate: z.date().optional(),
  96 | 			toDate: z.date().optional()
  97 | 		})
  98 | 	)
  99 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 100 | 		// Build where conditions using RQB v2 syntax
 101 | 		const rqbWhere: Record<string, unknown> = {
 102 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 103 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 104 | 			isDeleted: false
 105 | 		};
 106 | 
 107 | 		if (input.fromDate) {
 108 | 			rqbWhere.date = { gte: input.fromDate };
 109 | 		}
 110 | 		if (input.toDate) {
 111 | 			rqbWhere.date = {
 112 | 				...((rqbWhere.date as object) || {}),
 113 | 				lte: input.toDate
 114 | 			};
 115 | 		}
 116 | 
 117 | 		const records = await pediatricRepo.getPatientGrowthRecords(input.patientId, context.clinicId ?? "");
 118 | 
 119 | 		const chartData = records.map(record => {
 120 | 			let value: number | null = null;
 121 | 			let zScore: number | null = null;
 122 | 
 123 | 			switch (input.measurementType) {
 124 | 				case "WEIGHT":
 125 | 					value = record.weight ?? null;
 126 | 					zScore = record.weightForAgeZ ?? null;
 127 | 					break;
 128 | 				case "HEIGHT":
 129 | 					value = record.height ?? null;
 130 | 					zScore = record.heightForAgeZ ?? null;
 131 | 					break;
 132 | 				case "HEAD_CIRCUMFERENCE":
 133 | 					value = record.headCircumference ?? null;
 134 | 					zScore = record.hcForAgeZ ?? null;

 136 | 				case "BMI":

 148 | 				ageMonths: record.ageMonths,

 153 | 			};

 159 | // Update growth measurement - Using existing mutation
 160 | export const updateGrowthMeasurement = protectedProcedure
 161 | 	.input(
 162 | 		z.object({
 163 | 			id: z.string(),
 164 | 			date: z.date().optional(),
 165 | 			weight: z.number().optional(),
 166 | 			height: z.number().optional(),
 167 | 			headCircumference: z.number().optional(),
 168 | 			notes: z.string().optional()
 169 | 		})
 170 | 	)
 171 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 172 | 		// Verify record exists and belongs to clinic
 173 | 		const existing = await pediatricRepo.getGrowthRecordById(input.id, context.clinicId ?? "");
 174 | 
 175 | 		if (!existing) {
 176 | 			throw new Error("Growth record not found");
 177 | 		}
 178 | 
 179 | 		// Calculate BMI if both weight and height are provided
 180 | 		let bmi: number | undefined;
 181 | 		const weight = input.weight ?? existing.weight;
 182 | 		const height = input.height ?? existing.height;
 183 | 
 184 | 		if (weight && height) {
 185 | 			const heightInMeters = height / 100;
 186 | 			bmi = Number.parseFloat((weight / (heightInMeters * heightInMeters)).toFixed(1));
 187 | 		}
 188 | 
 189 | 		// Use the existing update mutation
 190 | 		const updated = await pediatricRepo.updateGrowthRecord(existing.id, {
 191 | 			date: input.date,
 192 | 			weight: weight,
 193 | 			height: height,
 194 | 			headCircumference: input.headCircumference ?? existing.headCircumference,
 195 | 			bmi,
 196 | 			notes: input.notes
 197 | 		});
 198 | 
 199 | 		if (!updated) {
 200 | 			throw new Error("Failed to update growth record");
 201 | 		}
 202 | 
 203 | 		return updated;
 204 | 	});

 258 | // Get growth velocity (rate of change between measurements)
 259 | export const getGrowthVelocity = protectedProcedure
 260 | 	.input(
 261 | 		z.object({
 262 | 			patientId: z.string()
 263 | 		})
 264 | 	)
 265 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 266 | 		const records = await pediatricRepo.getPatientGrowthRecords(input.patientId, context.clinicId ?? "");
 267 | 
 268 | 		if (records.length < 2) {
 269 | 			return {
 270 | 				velocity: [],
 271 | 				message: "Insufficient data for velocity calculation"
 272 | 			};
 273 | 		}
 274 | 
 275 | 		// Sort by date ascending
 276 | 		const sorted = [...records].sort((a, b) => a.date.getTime() - b.date.getTime());
 277 | 
 278 | 		const velocity = [];
 279 | 		for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {
 280 | 			const prev = sorted[i - 1];
 281 | 			const curr = sorted[i];
 282 | 			if (!prev || !curr) continue;
 283 | 
 284 | 			const daysDiff = Math.ceil((curr.date.getTime() - prev.date.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
 285 | 
 286 | 			if (daysDiff <= 0) continue;
 287 | 
 288 | 			velocity.push({
 289 | 				period: { from: prev.date, to: curr.date, days: daysDiff },
 290 | 				weightVelocity:
 291 | 					prev.weight && curr.weight
 292 | 						? Number(((curr.weight - prev.weight) / (daysDiff / 30.44)).toFixed(2)) // kg/month
 293 | 						: null,
 294 | 				heightVelocity:
 295 | 					prev.height && curr.height
 296 | 						? Number(((curr.height - prev.height) / (daysDiff / 30.44)).toFixed(2)) // cm/month
 297 | 						: null,
 298 | 				headVelocity:
 299 | 					prev.headCircumference && curr.headCircumference
 300 | 						? Number(((curr.headCircumference - prev.headCircumference) / (daysDiff / 30.44)).toFixed(2)) // cm/month
 301 | 						: null
 302 | 			});
 303 | 		}
 304 | 
 305 | 		return {
 306 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 307 | 			velocity
 308 | 		};
 309 | 	});
 310 | 
 311 | // Get growth percentile classification
 312 | export const getGrowthPercentile = protectedProcedure
 313 | 	.input(
 314 | 		z.object({
 315 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 316 | 			date: z.date().optional()
 317 | 		})
 318 | 	)
 319 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 320 | 		const patientData = await pediatricRepo.getGrowthRecordById(input.patientId, context.clinicId ?? "");
 321 | 
 322 | 		if (!patientData) {
 323 | 			throw new Error("Patient not found");
 324 | 		}
 325 | 
 326 | 		const referenceDate = input.date ?? new Date();
 327 | 		const ageDays = calculateAgeInDays(patientData.patient?.dateOfBirth ?? new Date());
 328 | 		const ageMonths = calculateAgeInMonths(patientData.patient?.dateOfBirth ?? new Date(), referenceDate);
 329 | 
 330 | 		// Use existing query to get growth records with percentiles
 331 | 		const growthWithPercentiles = await pediatricRepo.getPatientGrowthRecords(
 332 | 			input.patientId,
 333 | 			context.clinicId ?? ""
 334 | 		);
 335 | 
 336 | 		const latestRecord = growthWithPercentiles?.[0] ?? null;
 337 | 
 338 | 		if (!latestRecord) {
 339 | 			return {
 340 | 				ageDays,
 341 | 				ageMonths,
 342 | 				classifications: null,
 343 | 				message: "No growth records found for this patient"
 344 | 			};
 345 | 		}
 346 | 
 347 | 		const getWeightClassification = (zScore: number | null): string => {
 348 | 			if (zScore === null) return "NO_DATA";
 349 | 			if (zScore < -3) return "SEVERELY_UNDERWEIGHT";
 350 | 			if (zScore < -2) return "UNDERWEIGHT";
 351 | 			if (zScore <= 1) return "NORMAL";
 352 | 			if (zScore <= 2) return "OVERWEIGHT";
 353 | 			return "OBESE";
 354 | 		};
 355 | 
 356 | 		const getStuntingClassification = (zScore: number | null): string => {
 357 | 			if (zScore === null) return "NO_DATA";
 358 | 			if (zScore < -3) return "SEVERELY_STUNTED";
 359 | 			if (zScore < -2) return "STUNTED";
 360 | 			if (zScore <= 1) return "NORMAL";
 361 | 			if (zScore <= 2) return "TALL";
 362 | 			return "VERY_TALL";
 363 | 		};
 364 | 
 365 | 		return {
 366 | 			ageDays,
 367 | 			ageMonths,
 368 | 			classifications: {
 369 | 				weight: {
 370 | 					zScore: latestRecord.weightForAgeZ ?? null,
 371 | 					classification: getWeightClassification(latestRecord.weightForAgeZ ?? null),
 372 | 					percentile: latestRecord.percentile
 373 | 				},
 374 | 				height: {
 375 | 					zScore: latestRecord.heightForAgeZ ?? null,
 376 | 					classification: getStuntingClassification(latestRecord.heightForAgeZ ?? null)
 377 | 				},
 378 | 				headCircumference: {
 379 | 					zScore: latestRecord.hcForAgeZ ?? null,
 380 | 					classification: getWeightClassification(latestRecord.hcForAgeZ ?? null)
 381 | 				},
 382 | 				bmi: {
 383 | 					zScore: latestRecord.bmiForAgeZ ?? null,
 384 | 					classification: getWeightClassification(latestRecord.bmiForAgeZ ?? null)
 385 | 				}
 386 | 			},
 387 | 			lastMeasurement: {
 388 | 				date: latestRecord.date,
 389 | 				weight: latestRecord.weight,
 390 | 				height: latestRecord.height,
 391 | 				headCircumference: latestRecord.headCircumference,
 392 | 				bmi: latestRecord.bmi
 393 | 			}
 394 | 		};
 395 | 	});

 397 | // Bulk import growth records
 398 | export const bulkImportGrowthRecords = protectedProcedure
 399 | 	.input(
 400 | 		z.object({
 401 | 			records: z.array(
 402 | 				z.object({
 403 | 					patientId: z.string(),
 404 | 					date: z.date(),
 405 | 					weight: z.number().optional(),
 406 | 					height: z.number().optional(),
 407 | 					headCircumference: z.number().optional(),
 408 | 					notes: z.string().optional()
 409 | 				})
 410 | 			)
 411 | 		})
 412 | 	)
 413 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 414 | 		const results = [];
 415 | 		const errors = [];
 416 | 
 417 | 		for (const record of input.records) {
 418 | 			try {
 419 | 				// Verify patient exists and belongs to clinic
 420 | 				const patientData = await pediatricRepo.getGrowthRecordById(record.patientId, context.clinicId ?? "");
 421 | 
 422 | 				if (!patientData) {
 423 | 					errors.push({
 424 | 						patientId: record.patientId,
 425 | 						error: "Patient not found"
 426 | 					});
 427 | 					continue;
 428 | 				}
 429 | 
 430 | 				if (!patientData.gender) {
 431 | 					errors.push({
 432 | 						patientId: record.patientId,
 433 | 						error: "Patient gender is required"
 434 | 					});
 435 | 					continue;
 436 | 				}
 437 | 
 438 | 				// Calculate BMI if both weight and height are provided
 439 | 				let bmi: number | undefined;
 440 | 				if (record.weight && record.height) {
 441 | 					const heightInMeters = record.height / 100;
 442 | 					bmi = Number.parseFloat((record.weight / (heightInMeters * heightInMeters)).toFixed(1));
 443 | 				}
 444 | 
 445 | 				const growthRecord = await pediatricRepo.recordGrowthWithPercentiles({
 446 | 					patientId: record.patientId,
 447 | 					clinicId: context.clinicId,
 448 | 					date: record.date,
 449 | 					weight: record.weight,
 450 | 					height: record.height,
 451 | 					headCircumference: record.headCircumference,
 452 | 					bmi,
 453 | 					notes: record.notes
 454 | 				});
 455 | 
 456 | 				results.push(growthRecord);
 457 | 			} catch (error) {
 458 | 				errors.push({
 459 | 					patientId: record.patientId,
 460 | 					error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown error"
 461 | 				});
 462 | 			}
 463 | 		}
 464 | 
 465 | 		return {
 466 | 			success: results.length,
 467 | 			failed: errors.length,
 468 | 			results,
 469 | 			errors
 470 | 		};
 471 | 	});
 472 | 
 473 | // Get growth summary statistics
 474 | export const getGrowthSummary = protectedProcedure
 475 | 	.input(
 476 | 		z.object({
 477 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 478 | 			startDate: z.date().optional(),
 479 | 			endDate: z.date().optional()
 480 | 		})
 481 | 	)
 482 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 483 | 		const rqbWhere: Record<string, unknown> = {
 484 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 485 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 486 | 			isDeleted: false
 487 | 		};
 488 | 
 489 | 		if (input.startDate) {
 490 | 			rqbWhere.date = { gte: input.startDate };
 491 | 		}
 492 | 		if (input.endDate) {
 493 | 			rqbWhere.date = {
 494 | 				...((rqbWhere.date as object) || {}),
 495 | 				lte: input.endDate
 496 | 			};
 497 | 		}
 498 | 
 499 | 		const records = await pediatricRepo.getPatientGrowthRecords(input.patientId, context.clinicId ?? "");
 500 | 
 501 | 		if (records.length === 0) {
 502 | 			return {
 503 | 				count: 0,
 504 | 				summary: null,
 505 | 				message: "No growth records found"
 506 | 			};
 507 | 		}
 508 | 
 509 | 		const firstRecord = records[0];
 510 | 		const lastRecord = records[records.length - 1];
 511 | 
 512 | 		if (!firstRecord || !lastRecord) return { count: 0, summary: null };
 513 | 
 514 | 		let weightGrowthRate: number | null = null;
 515 | 		let heightGrowthRate: number | null = null;
 516 | 		if (firstRecord?.weight && lastRecord?.weight && firstRecord.weight !== lastRecord.weight) {
 517 | 			const daysDiff = Math.ceil(
 518 | 				(lastRecord.date.getTime() - firstRecord.date.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)
 519 | 			);
 520 | 			if (daysDiff > 0) {
 521 | 				weightGrowthRate = Number.parseFloat(((lastRecord.weight - firstRecord.weight) / daysDiff).toFixed(2));
 522 | 			}
 523 | 		}
 524 | 
 525 | 		if (firstRecord?.height && lastRecord?.height && firstRecord.height !== lastRecord.height) {
 526 | 			const daysDiff = Math.ceil(
 527 | 				(lastRecord.date.getTime() - firstRecord.date.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)
 528 | 			);
 529 | 			if (daysDiff > 0) {
 530 | 				heightGrowthRate = Number.parseFloat(((lastRecord.height - firstRecord.height) / daysDiff).toFixed(2));
 531 | 			}
 532 | 		}
 533 | 
 534 | 		return {
 535 | 			count: records.length,
 536 | 			summary: {
 537 | 				firstMeasurement: {
 538 | 					date: firstRecord.date,
 539 | 					weight: firstRecord.weight,
 540 | 					height: firstRecord.height,
 541 | 					headCircumference: firstRecord.headCircumference
 542 | 				},
 543 | 				lastMeasurement: {
 544 | 					date: lastRecord.date,
 545 | 					weight: lastRecord.weight,
 546 | 					height: lastRecord.height,
 547 | 					headCircumference: lastRecord.headCircumference
 548 | 				},
 549 | 				growthRates: {
 550 | 					weightPerDay: weightGrowthRate,
 551 | 					heightPerDay: heightGrowthRate
 552 | 				},
 553 | 				totalWeightGain:
 554 | 					lastRecord.weight && firstRecord.weight ? lastRecord.weight - firstRecord.weight : null,
 555 | 				totalHeightGain: lastRecord.height && firstRecord.height ? lastRecord.height - firstRecord.height : null
 556 | 			}
 557 | 		};
 558 | 	});

 576 | export const listGrowthRecords = protectedProcedure
 577 | 	.input(
 578 | 		z.object({
 579 | 			patientId: z.string().optional(),
 580 | 			limit: z.number().min(1).max(100).default(50),
 581 | 			offset: z.number().default(0)
 582 | 		})
 583 | 	)
 584 | 	.output(
 585 | 		z.object({
 586 | 			records: z.array(z.any()),
 587 | 			total: z.number()

 589 | 	)
 590 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 591 | 		const { limit, offset, patientId } = input;
 592 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 593 | 
 594 | 		const records = await pediatricRepo.getPatientGrowthRecords(patientId ?? "", clinicId);
 595 | 
 596 | 		const total = records.length;
 597 | 		const paginatedRecords = records
 598 | 			.sort((a, b) => b.date.getTime() - a.date.getTime())
 599 | 			.slice(offset, offset + limit);
 600 | 
 601 | 		return {
 602 | 			records: paginatedRecords,
 603 | 			total
 604 | 		};
 605 | 	});
 606 | 
 607 | // Get developmental milestones for a patient
 608 | export const getMilestones = protectedProcedure
 609 | 	.input(
 610 | 		z.object({
 611 | 			patientId: z.string()
 612 | 		})
 613 | 	)
 614 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 615 | 		// Use existing getDevelopmentalProgress query to get milestones
 616 | 		const progressData = await pediatricRepo.getDevelopmentalProgress(input.patientId);
 617 | 
 618 | 		// Flatten the milestones from the grouped structure
 619 | 		const allMilestones = Object.values(progressData.milestones).flat();
 620 | 
 621 | 		// Count achieved vs total milestones
 622 | 		const total = progressData.totalMilestonesAchieved;
 623 | 		const achieved = allMilestones.filter(m => m.dateRecorded).length;
 624 | 
 625 | 		return {
 626 | 			milestones: allMilestones,
 627 | 			total,
 628 | 			achieved,
 629 | 			progress: total > 0 ? (achieved / total) * 100 : 0
 630 | 		};
 631 | 	});
 632 |

 634 | export const updateMilestone = protectedProcedure

 646 | 		const patient = await patientRepo.getPatientById(input.patientId, context.clinicId ?? "");

 649 | 			throw new Error("Patient not found");
 650 | 		}

 657 |

 671 | 			};
 672 | 		}

 676 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 677 | 			milestone: input.milestone,
 678 | 			ageAchieved: input.ageAchieved,
 679 | 			dateRecorded: input.dateRecorded,
 680 | 			notes: input.notes,
 681 | 			createdBy: context.user?.id ?? ""
 682 | 		});

 688 | 		};
 689 | 	});
```
