`routers/health.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import z from "zod";
   2 | 
   3 | import { publicProcedure } from "../index";
   4 | import { env } from '../../env';
   5 | import { checkIsDbReady } from '../../db';
   6 | 
   7 | const HEALTHCHECK_TIMEOUT_MS = 1500;
   8 | 
   9 | // #region Utils
  10 | 
  11 | const CheckResultSchema = z
  12 | 	.object({
  13 | 		error: z.string().optional(),
  14 | 		latencyMs: z.number(),
  15 | 		status: z.enum(["healthy", "unhealthy"])
  16 | 	})
  17 | 	.loose();
  18 | 
  19 | type CheckResult = z.infer<typeof CheckResultSchema>;
  20 | 
  21 | function getErrorMessage(error: unknown): string {
  22 | 	if (error instanceof Error) {
  23 | 		return error.message;
  24 | 	}
  25 | 	return "Unknown error";
  26 | }
  27 | 
  28 | async function withTimeout<T>(promise: Promise<T>, timeoutMs: number): Promise<T> {
  29 | 	let timeoutId: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | undefined;
  30 | 	const timeout = new Promise<never>((_, reject) => {
  31 | 		timeoutId = setTimeout(() => reject(new Error(`Timed out after ${timeoutMs}ms`)), timeoutMs);
  32 | 	});
  33 | 	try {
  34 | 		return await Promise.race([promise, timeout]);
  35 | 	} finally {
  36 | 		if (timeoutId) {
  37 | 			clearTimeout(timeoutId);
  38 | 		}
  39 | 	}
  40 | }
  41 | 
  42 | async function runCheck(check: () => object | Promise<object>): Promise<CheckResult> {
  43 | 	const startedAt = performance.now();
  44 | 	try {
  45 | 		const data = await withTimeout(Promise.resolve(check()), HEALTHCHECK_TIMEOUT_MS);
  46 | 		const latencyMs = Math.round(performance.now() - startedAt);
  47 | 		const result = data as { status?: string };
  48 | 		if (result.status === "unhealthy") {
  49 | 			return { ...data, latencyMs, status: "unhealthy" };
  50 | 		}
  51 | 		return { ...data, latencyMs, status: "healthy" };
  52 | 	} catch (error) {
  53 | 		return {
  54 | 			error: getErrorMessage(error),
  55 | 			latencyMs: Math.round(performance.now() - startedAt),
  56 | 			status: "unhealthy"
  57 | 		};
  58 | 	}
  59 | }
  60 | 
  61 | function buildBaseHealth() {
  62 | 	return {
  63 | 		buildSha: process.env.SOURCE_COMMIT,
  64 | 		environment: env.NODE_ENV,
  65 | 		timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  66 | 		uptimeMs: Math.floor(process.uptime() * 1000),
  67 | 		url: env.BETTER_AUTH_URL
  68 | 	};
  69 | }
  70 | 
  71 | // #region Service Checks
  72 | async function checkDatabase() {
  73 | 	const isReady = await checkIsDbReady();
  74 | 	return { status: isReady ? "healthy" : "unhealthy" };
  75 | }
  76 | 
  77 | function checkSystem() {
  78 | 	return {
  79 | 		memory: process.memoryUsage(),
  80 | 		cpu: process.cpuUsage(),
  81 | 		nodeVersion: process.version,
  82 | 		platform: process.platform,
  83 | 		status: "healthy" as const
  84 | 	};
  85 | }
  86 | 
  87 | const serviceChecks = {
  88 | 	database: checkDatabase,
  89 | 	system: checkSystem
  90 | } satisfies Record<string, () => object | Promise<object>>;
  91 | 
  92 | // #region Router
  93 | 
  94 | export const healthRouter = {
  95 | 	live: publicProcedure
  96 | 		.route({
  97 | 			description: "Check if the server is alive",
  98 | 			method: "GET",
  99 | 			spec: spec => {
 100 | 				return { ...spec, security: [] };
 101 | 			}
 102 | 		})
 103 | 		.errors({})
 104 | 		.handler(() => {
 105 | 			return { status: "healthy", ...buildBaseHealth() };
 106 | 		}),
 107 | 	ready: publicProcedure
 108 | 		.route({
 109 | 			description: "Check if the server is ready to handle requests and connect to external services",
 110 | 			method: "GET",
 111 | 			spec: spec => {
 112 | 				return { ...spec, security: [] };
 113 | 			}
 114 | 		})
 115 | 		.errors({
 116 | 			SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE: {
 117 | 				data: z.object({
 118 | 					checks: z.record(z.string(), CheckResultSchema)
 119 | 				}),
 120 | 				description: "One or more services are unhealthy",
 121 | 				status: 503
 122 | 			}
 123 | 		})
 124 | 		.handler(async ({ errors }) => {
 125 | 			const entries = await Promise.all(
 126 | 				Object.entries(serviceChecks).map(async ([name, check]) => [name, await runCheck(check)])
 127 | 			);
 128 | 			const checks = Object.fromEntries(entries) as Record<string, CheckResult>;
 129 | 			const allHealthy = Object.values(checks).every(r => r.status === "healthy");
 130 | 
 131 | 			if (!allHealthy) {
 132 | 				throw errors.SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE({ data: { checks } });
 133 | 			}
 134 | 
 135 | 			return {
 136 | 				status: "healthy" as const,
 137 | 				...buildBaseHealth(),
 138 | 				checks
 139 | 			};
 140 | 		})
 141 | };

```

`routers/immunization.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import z from "zod";
   2 | 
   3 | import { adminProcedure, protectedProcedure } from "..";
   4 | import type { ImmunizationStatus } from "../../db";
   5 | import { ImmunizationSchema, type PatientSchema, type VaccineScheduleSchema } from "../../db-collections";
   6 | import { mutations } from "../../db/actions/mutations";
   7 | import { patientRepo, pediatricRepo, type queries } from "../../db/queries";
   8 | import { calculateAgeInDays } from "../../utils";
   9 | 
  10 | type ImmunizationRecord = z.infer<typeof ImmunizationSchema>;
  11 | type VaccineScheduleRecord = z.infer<typeof VaccineScheduleSchema>;
  12 | type PatientRecord = z.infer<typeof PatientSchema>;
  13 | 
  14 | type CatchUpDose = {
  15 | 	doseNumber: number;
  16 | 	recommendedDate: Date;
  17 | 	vaccineName: string;
  18 | };
  19 | 
  20 | type CatchUpRecommendation = {
  21 | 	vaccineName: string;
  22 | 	missingDoses: number;
  23 | 	catchUpDoses: CatchUpDose[];
  24 | 	priority: "high" | "medium" | "normal" | "low";
  25 | 	notes: string;
  26 | };
  27 | 
  28 | export const vaccineRouter = {
  29 | 	getPatientVaccineSchedule: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ patientId: z.string() })).handler(async ({ input }) => {
  30 | 		return await pediatricRepo.getPatientVaccineSchedule(input.patientId);
  31 | 	}),
  32 | 
  33 | 	getVaccineInventoryStatus: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ clinicId: z.string() })).handler(async ({ input }) => {
  34 | 		return await pediatricRepo.getVaccineInventoryStatus(input.clinicId);
  35 | 	}),
  36 | 
  37 | 	getOverdueImmunizations: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ clinicId: z.string() })).handler(async ({ input }) => {
  38 | 		return await pediatricRepo.getOverdueImmunizations(input.clinicId);
  39 | 	}),
  40 | 
  41 | 	recordImmunization: adminProcedure
  42 | 		.input(
  43 | 			z.object({
  44 | 				patientId: z.string(),
  45 | 				clinicId: z.string(),
  46 | 				vaccine: z.string(),
  47 | 				date: z.date(),
  48 | 				dose: z.string(),
  49 | 				lotNumber: z.string(),
  50 | 				administeredByStaffId: z.string(),
  51 | 				notes: z.string().optional()
  52 | 			})
  53 | 		)
  54 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  55 | 			return await pediatricRepo.recordImmunization(input);
  56 | 		})
  57 | };
  58 | // Shared logic function for getting immunization schedule (used by reminders)
  59 | async function getPatientImmunizationScheduleLogic(params: { patientId: string; includePastDue?: boolean }) {
  60 | 	const { patientId } = params;
  61 | 
  62 | 	// Use patient queries to get patient data with immunizations
  63 | 	const patientData = await patientRepo.getPatientById(patientId, "");
  64 | 
  65 | 	if (!patientData) {
  66 | 		throw new Error("Patient not found");
  67 | 	}
  68 | 
  69 | 	// Get immunizations using vaccine queries
  70 | 	const scheduleResult = await pediatricRepo.getPatientVaccineSchedule(patientId);
  71 | 	const patientImmunizations = scheduleResult?.administeredVaccines ?? [];
  72 | 
  73 | 	const ageInDays = calculateAgeInDays(patientData.dateOfBirth);
  74 | 	const ageInMonths = Math.floor(ageInDays / 30.44);
  75 | 	const ageInYears = Math.floor(ageInMonths / 12);
  76 | 
  77 | 	console.log(`Patient age: ${ageInYears} years, ${ageInMonths % 12} months, ${ageInDays % 30} days`);
  78 | 
  79 | 	// Get all vaccine schedules using vaccine queries
  80 | 	const allVaccines = (await queries.vaccine?.getAllSchedules?.()) ?? [];
  81 | 
  82 | 	// Create a map of administered vaccines by name
  83 | 	const administeredMap = new Map<string, ImmunizationRecord[]>();
  84 | 	for (const admin of patientImmunizations) {
  85 | 		if (!administeredMap.has(admin.vaccine)) {
  86 | 			administeredMap.set(admin.vaccine, []);
  87 | 		}
  88 | 		administeredMap.get(admin.vaccine)?.push(admin);
  89 | 	}
  90 | 
  91 | 	// Calculate due and upcoming vaccines
  92 | 	const dueVaccines: (VaccineScheduleRecord & {
  93 | 		administeredRecords: ImmunizationRecord[];
  94 | 		completedDoses: number;
  95 | 		totalRequiredDoses: number;
  96 | 		nextDoseNumber: number;
  97 | 		status: string;
  98 | 	})[] = [];
  99 | 	const upcomingVaccines: (VaccineScheduleRecord & {
 100 | 		eligibleDate: Date;
 101 | 		daysUntilEligible: number;
 102 | 	})[] = [];
 103 | 	const completedVaccines: (VaccineScheduleRecord & {
 104 | 		administeredRecords: ImmunizationRecord[];
 105 | 		completedDoses: number;
 106 | 		totalRequiredDoses: number;
 107 | 		status: string;
 108 | 	})[] = [];
 109 | 	const overdueVaccines: (VaccineScheduleRecord & {
 110 | 		administeredRecords: ImmunizationRecord[];
 111 | 		completedDoses: number;
 112 | 		totalRequiredDoses: number;
 113 | 		status: string;
 114 | 		nextDoseNumber?: number;
 115 | 	})[] = [];
 116 | 
 117 | 	for (const vaccine of allVaccines) {
 118 | 		const adminRecords = administeredMap.get(vaccine.vaccineName) ?? [];
 119 | 		const completedDoses = adminRecords.length;
 120 | 		const totalRequiredDoses = (vaccine.totalDoses ?? vaccine.dosesRequired) || 1;
 121 | 		const isComplete = completedDoses >= totalRequiredDoses;
 122 | 
 123 | 		// Check if vaccine is age-appropriate
 124 | 		const minAgeDays = vaccine.ageInDaysMin ?? 0;
 125 | 		const maxAgeDays = vaccine.ageInDaysMax ?? Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
 126 | 		const isAgeAppropriate = ageInDays >= minAgeDays && ageInDays <= maxAgeDays;
 127 | 
 128 | 		if (isComplete) {
 129 | 			completedVaccines.push({
 130 | 				...vaccine,
 131 | 				administeredRecords: adminRecords,
 132 | 				completedDoses,
 133 | 				totalRequiredDoses,
 134 | 				status: "COMPLETED" as const
 135 | 			});
 136 | 		} else if (isAgeAppropriate) {
 137 | 			const nextDoseNumber = completedDoses + 1;
 138 | 			const isOverdue = adminRecords.length === 0 && ageInDays > maxAgeDays;
 139 | 
 140 | 			const vaccineData = {
 141 | 				...vaccine,
 142 | 				administeredRecords: adminRecords,
 143 | 				completedDoses,
 144 | 				totalRequiredDoses,
 145 | 				nextDoseNumber,
 146 | 				status: isOverdue ? ("OVERDUE" as const) : ("PENDING" as const)
 147 | 			};
 148 | 
 149 | 			if (isOverdue) {
 150 | 				overdueVaccines.push(vaccineData);
 151 | 			} else {
 152 | 				dueVaccines.push(vaccineData);
 153 | 			}
 154 | 		} else if (ageInDays < minAgeDays) {
 155 | 			upcomingVaccines.push({
 156 | 				...vaccine,
 157 | 				eligibleDate: new Date(Date.now() + (minAgeDays - ageInDays) * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000),
 158 | 				daysUntilEligible: minAgeDays - ageInDays
 159 | 			});
 160 | 		} else if (ageInDays > maxAgeDays && !isComplete) {
 161 | 			overdueVaccines.push({
 162 | 				...vaccine,
 163 | 				administeredRecords: adminRecords,
 164 | 				completedDoses,
 165 | 				totalRequiredDoses,
 166 | 				status: "OVERDUE" as const
 167 | 			});
 168 | 		}
 169 | 	}
 170 | 
 171 | 	return {
 172 | 		due: dueVaccines,
 173 | 		upcoming: upcomingVaccines,
 174 | 		completed: completedVaccines,
 175 | 		overdue: overdueVaccines
 176 | 	};
 177 | }
 178 | 
 179 | export const listImmunizations = protectedProcedure
 180 | 	.input(
 181 | 		z.object({
 182 | 			patientId: z.string().optional(),
 183 | 			limit: z.number().min(1).max(100).default(50),
 184 | 			offset: z.number().default(0)
 185 | 		})
 186 | 	)
 187 | 	.output(
 188 | 		z.object({
 189 | 			records: z.array(ImmunizationSchema),
 190 | 			total: z.number()
 191 | 		})
 192 | 	)
 193 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 194 | 		const { limit, offset, patientId } = input;
 195 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 196 | 
 197 | 		const { records, total } = await queries.vaccine.listImmunizations({
 198 | 			clinicId,
 199 | 			patientId,
 200 | 			limit,
 201 | 			offset
 202 | 		});
 203 | 
 204 | 		return {
 205 | 			records,
 206 | 			total
 207 | 		};
 208 | 	});
 209 | 
 210 | // Record single immunization with inventory management
 211 | export const recordImmunization = protectedProcedure
 212 | 	.input(
 213 | 		z.object({
 214 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 215 | 			vaccineName: z.string(),
 216 | 			date: z.date(),
 217 | 			dose: z.string(),
 218 | 			lotNumber: z.string().optional(),
 219 | 			administeredByStaffId: z.string().optional(),
 220 | 			notes: z.string().optional(),
 221 | 			batchId: z.string().optional()
 222 | 		})
 223 | 	)
 224 | 	.output(z.any())
 225 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 226 | 		// Check and decrement inventory if batchId provided
 227 | 		if (input.batchId) {
 228 | 			const inventoryStatus = await queries.vaccine?.getVaccineInventoryStatus?.(context.clinicId ?? "");
 229 | 			const batch = inventoryStatus?.inventoryByVaccine?.find(v => v.id === input.batchId);
 230 | 
 231 | 			if (!batch || batch.quantity <= 0) {
 232 | 				throw new Error("Insufficient vaccine stock");
 233 | 			}
 234 | 
 235 | 			// Update inventory using mutation
 236 | 			await mutations.vaccine.updateInventory?.(input.batchId, {
 237 | 				quantity: batch.quantity - 1
 238 | 			});
 239 | 		}
 240 | 
 241 | 		// Record immunization using the immunization mutation
 242 | 		const record = await mutations.vaccine.recordImmunization?.({
 243 | 			id: crypto.randomUUID(),
 244 | 			recordId: crypto.randomUUID(),
 245 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 246 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 247 | 			vaccine: input.vaccineName,
 248 | 			date: input.date,
 249 | 			dose: input.dose,
 250 | 			lotNumber: input.lotNumber,
 251 | 			administeredByStaffId: input.administeredByStaffId,
 252 | 			notes: input.notes
 253 | 		});
 254 | 
 255 | 		return record;
 256 | 	});
 257 | 
 258 | // Batch immunization recording
 259 | export const batchRecordImmunizations = protectedProcedure
 260 | 	.input(
 261 | 		z.object({
 262 | 			immunizations: z.array(
 263 | 				z.object({
 264 | 					patientId: z.string(),
 265 | 					vaccineName: z.string(),
 266 | 					dose: z.string(),
 267 | 					lotNumber: z.string().optional(),
 268 | 					notes: z.string().optional()
 269 | 				})
 270 | 			),
 271 | 			administeredByStaffId: z.string(),
 272 | 			administrationDate: z.date()
 273 | 		})
 274 | 	)
 275 | 	.output(z.any())
 276 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 277 | 		const results: ImmunizationRecord[] = [];
 278 | 		const errors: {
 279 | 			patientId: string;
 280 | 			vaccineName: string;
 281 | 			error: string;
 282 | 		}[] = [];
 283 | 
 284 | 		for (const imm of input.immunizations) {
 285 | 			try {
 286 | 				const record = await mutations.vaccine.recordImmunization?.({
 287 | 					id: crypto.randomUUID(),
 288 | 					recordId: crypto.randomUUID(),
 289 | 					patientId: imm.patientId,
 290 | 					clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 291 | 					vaccine: imm.vaccineName,
 292 | 					date: input.administrationDate,
 293 | 					dose: imm.dose,
 294 | 					lotNumber: imm.lotNumber,
 295 | 					administeredByStaffId: input.administeredByStaffId,
 296 | 					notes: imm.notes
 297 | 				});
 298 | 
 299 | 				if (record) {
 300 | 					results.push(record);
 301 | 				}
 302 | 			} catch (error) {
 303 | 				errors.push({
 304 | 					patientId: imm.patientId,
 305 | 					vaccineName: imm.vaccineName,
 306 | 					error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
 307 | 				});
 308 | 			}
 309 | 		}
 310 | 
 311 | 		return {
 312 | 			successful: results,
 313 | 			failed: errors,
 314 | 			totalSuccess: results.length,
 315 | 			totalFailed: errors.length
 316 | 		};
 317 | 	});
 318 | 
 319 | // Get immunization schedule for patient with comprehensive age calculation
 320 | export const getPatientImmunizationSchedule = protectedProcedure
 321 | 	.input(
 322 | 		z.object({
 323 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 324 | 			includePastDue: z.boolean().default(true)
 325 | 		})
 326 | 	)
 327 | 	.output(z.any())
 328 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 329 | 		// Use patient query to get patient data
 330 | 		const patientData = await patientRepo.getPatientById(input.patientId, "");
 331 | 
 332 | 		if (!patientData) {
 333 | 			throw new Error("Patient not found");
 334 | 		}
 335 | 
 336 | 		const ageInDays = calculateAgeInDays(patientData.dateOfBirth);
 337 | 		const ageInMonths = Math.floor(ageInDays / 30.44);
 338 | 		const ageInYears = Math.floor(ageInMonths / 12);
 339 | 
 340 | 		// Get vaccine schedule using vaccine queries
 341 | 		const scheduleResult = await pediatricRepo.getPatientVaccineSchedule(input.patientId);
 342 | 		const patientImmunizations = scheduleResult?.administeredVaccines ?? [];
 343 | 		const allVaccines = (await queries.vaccine?.getAllSchedules?.()) ?? [];
 344 | 
 345 | 		// Create a map of administered vaccines by name
 346 | 		const administeredMap = new Map<string, ImmunizationRecord[]>();
 347 | 		for (const admin of patientImmunizations) {
 348 | 			if (!administeredMap.has(admin.vaccine)) {
 349 | 				administeredMap.set(admin.vaccine, []);
 350 | 			}
 351 | 			administeredMap.get(admin.vaccine)?.push(admin);
 352 | 		}
 353 | 
 354 | 		// Calculate due and upcoming vaccines
 355 | 		const dueVaccines: (VaccineScheduleRecord & {
 356 | 			administeredRecords: ImmunizationRecord[];
 357 | 			completedDoses: number;
 358 | 			totalRequiredDoses: number;
 359 | 			nextDoseNumber: number;
 360 | 			status: ImmunizationStatus;
 361 | 		})[] = [];
 362 | 		const upcomingVaccines: (VaccineScheduleRecord & {
 363 | 			eligibleDate: Date;
 364 | 			daysUntilEligible: number;
 365 | 		})[] = [];
 366 | 		const completedVaccines: (VaccineScheduleRecord & {
 367 | 			administeredRecords: ImmunizationRecord[];
 368 | 			completedDoses: number;
 369 | 			totalRequiredDoses: number;
 370 | 			status: ImmunizationStatus;
 371 | 		})[] = [];
 372 | 		const overdueVaccines: (VaccineScheduleRecord & {
 373 | 			administeredRecords: ImmunizationRecord[];
 374 | 			completedDoses: number;
 375 | 			totalRequiredDoses: number;
 376 | 			status: ImmunizationStatus;
 377 | 			nextDoseNumber?: number;
 378 | 		})[] = [];
 379 | 
 380 | 		for (const vaccine of allVaccines) {
 381 | 			const adminRecords = administeredMap.get(vaccine.vaccineName) ?? [];
 382 | 			const completedDoses = adminRecords.length;
 383 | 			const totalRequiredDoses = (vaccine.totalDoses ?? vaccine.dosesRequired) || 1;
 384 | 			const isComplete = completedDoses >= totalRequiredDoses;
 385 | 
 386 | 			// Check if vaccine is age-appropriate
 387 | 			const minAgeDays = vaccine.ageInDaysMin ?? 0;
 388 | 			const maxAgeDays = vaccine.ageInDaysMax ?? Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
 389 | 			const isAgeAppropriate = ageInDays >= minAgeDays && ageInDays <= maxAgeDays;
 390 | 
 391 | 			if (isComplete) {
 392 | 				completedVaccines.push({
 393 | 					...vaccine,
 394 | 					dosesRequired: totalRequiredDoses,
 395 | 					administeredRecords: adminRecords,
 396 | 					completedDoses,
 397 | 					totalRequiredDoses,
 398 | 					status: "COMPLETED"
 399 | 				});
 400 | 			} else if (isAgeAppropriate) {
 401 | 				const nextDoseNumber = completedDoses + 1;
 402 | 				const isOverdue = adminRecords.length === 0 && ageInDays > maxAgeDays;
 403 | 
 404 | 				const vaccineData = {
 405 | 					...vaccine,
 406 | 					dosesRequired: totalRequiredDoses,
 407 | 					administeredRecords: adminRecords,
 408 | 					completedDoses,
 409 | 					totalRequiredDoses,
 410 | 					nextDoseNumber,
 411 | 					status: (isOverdue ? "OVERDUE" : "PENDING") as ImmunizationStatus
 412 | 				};
 413 | 
 414 | 				if (isOverdue && input.includePastDue) {
 415 | 					overdueVaccines.push(vaccineData);
 416 | 				} else if (!isOverdue) {
 417 | 					dueVaccines.push(vaccineData);
 418 | 				}
 419 | 			} else if (ageInDays < minAgeDays) {
 420 | 				upcomingVaccines.push({
 421 | 					...vaccine,
 422 | 					dosesRequired: totalRequiredDoses,
 423 | 					eligibleDate: new Date(Date.now() + (minAgeDays - ageInDays) * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000),
 424 | 					daysUntilEligible: minAgeDays - ageInDays
 425 | 				});
 426 | 			} else if (ageInDays > maxAgeDays && !isComplete && input.includePastDue) {
 427 | 				overdueVaccines.push({
 428 | 					...vaccine,
 429 | 					dosesRequired: totalRequiredDoses,
 430 | 					administeredRecords: adminRecords,
 431 | 					completedDoses,
 432 | 					totalRequiredDoses,
 433 | 					status: "OVERDUE"
 434 | 				});
 435 | 			}
 436 | 		}
 437 | 
 438 | 		// Get catch-up recommendations
 439 | 		const catchUpRecommendations = generateCatchUpSchedule(allVaccines as VaccineScheduleRecord[], administeredMap);
 440 | 
 441 | 		return {
 442 | 			patient: {
 443 | 				id: patientData.id,
 444 | 				name: `${patientData.firstName} ${patientData.lastName}`,
 445 | 				dateOfBirth: patientData.dateOfBirth,
 446 | 				age: {
 447 | 					years: ageInYears,
 448 | 					months: ageInMonths,
 449 | 					days: ageInDays
 450 | 				}
 451 | 			},
 452 | 			schedule: {
 453 | 				due: dueVaccines,
 454 | 				upcoming: upcomingVaccines,
 455 | 				completed: completedVaccines,
 456 | 				overdue: overdueVaccines
 457 | 			},
 458 | 			catchUpSchedule: catchUpRecommendations,
 459 | 			summary: {
 460 | 				totalDue: dueVaccines.length,
 461 | 				totalCompleted: completedVaccines.length,
 462 | 				totalOverdue: overdueVaccines.length,
 463 | 				totalUpcoming: upcomingVaccines.length,
 464 | 				overallCompliance:
 465 | 					allVaccines.length > 0 ? Math.round((completedVaccines.length / allVaccines.length) * 100) : 0
 466 | 			}
 467 | 		};
 468 | 	});
 469 | 
 470 | // Generate catch-up immunization schedule
 471 | function generateCatchUpSchedule(
 472 | 	allVaccines: VaccineScheduleRecord[],
 473 | 	administeredMap: Map<string, ImmunizationRecord[]>
 474 | ): CatchUpRecommendation[] {
 475 | 	const catchUpSchedule: CatchUpRecommendation[] = [];
 476 | 	const currentDate = new Date();
 477 | 
 478 | 	for (const vaccine of allVaccines) {
 479 | 		const adminRecords = administeredMap.get(vaccine.vaccineName) ?? [];
 480 | 		const completedDoses = adminRecords.length;
 481 | 		const totalRequiredDoses = (vaccine.totalDoses ?? vaccine.dosesRequired) || 1;
 482 | 
 483 | 		if (completedDoses < totalRequiredDoses) {
 484 | 			// Calculate accelerated schedule for catch-up
 485 | 			const missingDoses = totalRequiredDoses - completedDoses;
 486 | 			const recommendedInterval = vaccine.minimumInterval ?? 28; // Default 4 weeks
 487 | 			const startDate = new Date(currentDate);
 488 | 
 489 | 			const catchUpDoses: CatchUpDose[] = [];
 490 | 			for (let i = 0; i < missingDoses; i++) {
 491 | 				catchUpDoses.push({
 492 | 					doseNumber: completedDoses + i + 1,
 493 | 					recommendedDate: new Date(startDate.getTime() + i * recommendedInterval * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000),
 494 | 					vaccineName: vaccine.vaccineName
 495 | 				});
 496 | 			}
 497 | 
 498 | 			catchUpSchedule.push({
 499 | 				vaccineName: vaccine.vaccineName,
 500 | 				missingDoses,
 501 | 				catchUpDoses,
 502 | 				priority: "normal" as const,
 503 | 				notes: vaccine.description ?? "Follow standard catch-up schedule"
 504 | 			});
 505 | 		}
 506 | 	}
 507 | 
 508 | 	return catchUpSchedule.sort((a, b) => {
 509 | 		const priorityOrder: Record<string, number> = {
 510 | 			high: 1,
 511 | 			medium: 2,
 512 | 			normal: 3,
 513 | 			low: 4
 514 | 		};
 515 | 		return (priorityOrder[a.priority] ?? 3) - (priorityOrder[b.priority] ?? 3);
 516 | 	});
 517 | }
 518 | 
 519 | // Record adverse event for immunization
 520 | export const recordAdverseEvent = protectedProcedure
 521 | 	.input(
 522 | 		z.object({
 523 | 			immunizationId: z.string(),
 524 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 525 | 			vaccineName: z.string(),
 526 | 			eventType: z.enum(["allergic_reaction", "fever", "pain", "swelling", "other"]),
 527 | 			severity: z.enum(["MILD", "MODERATE", "SEVERE", "CRITICAL"]),
 528 | 			dateReported: z.date(),
 529 | 			description: z.string(),
 530 | 			outcome: z.string().optional(),
 531 | 			treatment: z.string().optional(),
 532 | 			reportedByStaffId: z.string().optional()
 533 | 		})
 534 | 	)
 535 | 	.output(z.any())
 536 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 537 | 		// Use adverse event mutation if available
 538 | 		const event = await mutations.vaccine.recordAdverseEvent({
 539 | 			id: crypto.randomUUID(),
 540 | 			immunizationId: input.immunizationId,
 541 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 542 | 			vaccineName: input.vaccineName,
 543 | 			eventType: input.eventType,
 544 | 			severity: input.severity,
 545 | 			description: input.description,
 546 | 			outcome: input.outcome,
 547 | 			treatment: input.treatment,
 548 | 			dateReported: input.dateReported,
 549 | 			reportedByStaffId: context.user?.id ?? ""
 550 | 		});
 551 | 
 552 | 		return event;
 553 | 	});

 555 | // Get immunization history with adverse events
 556 | export const getImmunizationHistory = protectedProcedure
 557 | 	.input(
 558 | 		z.object({
 559 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 560 | 			limit: z.number().optional().default(50),
 561 | 			offset: z.number().optional().default(0)
 562 | 		})
 563 | 	)
 564 | 	.output(z.any())
 565 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 566 | 		// Use vaccine query to get immunization history
 567 | 		const scheduleResult = await pediatricRepo.getPatientVaccineSchedule(input.patientId);
 568 | 		const immunizations = scheduleResult?.administeredVaccines ?? [];
 569 | 
 570 | 		// Get patient data
 571 | 		const patientData = await patientRepo.getPatientById(input.patientId, "");
 572 | 
 573 | 		// Generate immunization certificate data
 574 | 		if (!patientData) {
 575 | 			throw new Error("Patient not found");
 576 | 		}
 577 | 
 578 | 		const certificate = generateImmunizationCertificate(immunizations, patientData as PatientRecord);
 579 | 
 580 | 		return {
 581 | 			immunizations,
 582 | 			limit: input.limit,
 583 | 			offset: input.offset,
 584 | 			certificate,
 585 | 			compliance: calculateComplianceMetrics(immunizations)
 586 | 		};
 587 | 	});
 588 | 
 589 | // Generate immunization certificate
 590 | function generateImmunizationCertificate(immunizations: ImmunizationRecord[], patientData: PatientRecord) {
 591 | 	const isFullyImmunized = immunizations.length >= 10; // Threshold for fully immunized child
 592 | 
 593 | 	return {
 594 | 		isFullyImmunized,
 595 | 		certificateNumber: `IMM-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 11)}`,
 596 | 		generatedDate: new Date(),
 597 | 		patientName: patientData ? `${patientData.firstName} ${patientData.lastName}` : "Unknown",
 598 | 		immunizations: immunizations.map(imm => {
 599 | 			return {
 600 | 				vaccine: imm.vaccine,
 601 | 				date: imm.date,
 602 | 				dose: imm.dose,
 603 | 				administeredBy: imm.administeredByStaffId ?? "Unknown",
 604 | 				lotNumber: imm.lotNumber ?? "N/A"
 605 | 			};
 606 | 		})
 607 | 	};
 608 | }
 609 | 
 610 | // Calculate compliance metrics
 611 | function calculateComplianceMetrics(immunizations: ImmunizationRecord[]) {
 612 | 	const vaccinesByType = new Map<string, ImmunizationRecord[]>();
 613 | 
 614 | 	for (const imm of immunizations) {
 615 | 		let list = vaccinesByType.get(imm.vaccine);
 616 | 		if (!list) {
 617 | 			list = [];
 618 | 			vaccinesByType.set(imm.vaccine, list);
 619 | 		}
 620 | 		list.push(imm);
 621 | 	}
 622 | 
 623 | 	return {
 624 | 		totalVaccines: immunizations.length,
 625 | 		uniqueVaccines: vaccinesByType.size,
 626 | 		completenessScore: Math.min(100, (immunizations.length / 15) * 100)
 627 | 	};
 628 | }

 630 | // Generate immunization reminders
 631 | export const generateImmunizationReminders = protectedProcedure
 632 | 	.input(
 633 | 		z.object({
 634 | 			clinicId: z.string(),
 635 | 			reminderDays: z.number().default(7)
 636 | 		})
 637 | 	)
 638 | 	.output(
 639 | 		z.array(
 640 | 			z.object({
 641 | 				patientId: z.string(),
 642 | 				patientName: z.string(),
 643 | 				phone: z.string().nullable(),
 644 | 				email: z.string().nullable(),
 645 | 				dueVaccines: z.array(z.any()),
 646 | 				overdueVaccines: z.array(z.any()),
 647 | 				reminderDate: z.date()
 648 | 			})
 649 | 		)
 650 | 	)
 651 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 652 | 		// Fetch only active patients in the specific clinic
 653 | 		const patients = (await patientRepo.getPatientsByClinic?.(input.clinicId)) ?? [];
 654 | 
 655 | 		const reminders: {
 656 | 			patientId: string;
 657 | 			patientName: string;
 658 | 			phone: string | null;
 659 | 			email: string | null;
 660 | 			dueVaccines: Record<string, unknown>[];
 661 | 			overdueVaccines: Record<string, unknown>[];
 662 | 			reminderDate: Date;
 663 | 		}[] = [];
 664 | 
 665 | 		for (const patient of patients) {
 666 | 			if (!patient.isActive || patient.isDeleted) continue;
 667 | 
 668 | 			const schedule = await getPatientImmunizationScheduleLogic({
 669 | 				patientId: patient.id
 670 | 			});
 671 | 
 672 | 			const hasDue = schedule.due.length > 0;
 673 | 			const hasOverdue = schedule.overdue.length > 0;
 674 | 
 675 | 			if (hasDue || hasOverdue) {
 676 | 				reminders.push({
 677 | 					patientId: patient.id,
 678 | 					patientName: `${patient.firstName} ${patient.lastName}`,
 679 | 					phone: patient.phone,
 680 | 					email: patient.email,
 681 | 					dueVaccines: schedule.due,
 682 | 					overdueVaccines: schedule.overdue,
 683 | 					reminderDate: new Date()
 684 | 				});
 685 | 			}
 686 | 		}
 687 | 
 688 | 		return reminders;
 689 | 	});
 690 | 
 691 | // Export bulk immunization data for reporting
 692 | export const exportImmunizationData = protectedProcedure
 693 | 	.input(
 694 | 		z.object({
 695 | 			startDate: z.date(),
 696 | 			endDate: z.date(),
 697 | 			clinicId: z.string(),
 698 | 			format: z.enum(["json", "csv"]).default("json")
 699 | 		})
 700 | 	)
 701 | 	.output(z.any())
 702 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 703 | 		// Get overdue immunizations for the clinic
 704 | 		const overdueImmunizations = await pediatricRepo.getOverdueImmunizations(input.clinicId);
 705 | 
 706 | 		// Filter by date range
 707 | 		const filteredImmunizations = overdueImmunizations.filter(imm => {
 708 | 			const immDate = new Date(imm.date);
 709 | 			return immDate >= input.startDate && immDate <= input.endDate;
 710 | 		});
 711 | 
 712 | 		// Generate statistics
 713 | 		const stats = {
 714 | 			totalImmunizations: filteredImmunizations.length,
 715 | 			uniquePatients: new Set(filteredImmunizations.map(i => i.patientId)).size,
 716 | 			vaccinesByType: {} as Record<string, number>,
 717 | 			adverseEvents: 0,
 718 | 			coverageRate: 0
 719 | 		};
 720 | 
 721 | 		for (const imm of filteredImmunizations) {
 722 | 			const vaccineName = imm.vaccine;
 723 | 			stats.vaccinesByType[vaccineName] = (stats.vaccinesByType[vaccineName] ?? 0) + 1;
 724 | 		}
 725 | 
 726 | 		if (input.format === "csv") {
 727 | 			const csvRows = [
 728 | 				["Date", "Patient Name", "Vaccine", "Dose", "Lot Number", "Administered By", "Adverse Event"],
 729 | 				...filteredImmunizations.map(imm => [
 730 | 					imm.date.toISOString(),
 731 | 					`${imm.patient?.firstName} ${imm.patient?.lastName}`,
 732 | 					imm.vaccine,
 733 | 					imm.dose,
 734 | 					imm.lotNumber ?? "",
 735 | 					imm.administeredByStaffId ?? "",
 736 | 					"No"
 737 | 				])
 738 | 			];
 739 | 			return { csv: csvRows.map(row => row.join(",")).join("\n"), stats };
 740 | 		}
 741 | 
 742 | 		return { data: filteredImmunizations, stats };
 743 | 	});
```

`routers/index.1.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import type { RouterClient } from "@orpc/server";
   2 | 
   3 | import { o, protectedProcedure, publicProcedure } from "../index";
   4 | 
   5 | export const appRouter = o.router({
   6 | 	healthCheck: publicProcedure.handler(() => "OK"),
   7 | 	privateData: protectedProcedure.handler(({ context }) => {
   8 | 		return {
   9 | 			message: "This is private",
  10 | 			user: context?.user
  11 | 		};
  12 | 	}),
  13 | 
  14 | });
  15 | 
  16 | export type AppRouter = typeof appRouter;
  17 | export type AppRouterClient = RouterClient<typeof appRouter>;
  18 | const router = appRouter;
  19 | export default router;

```

```ts
   9 |   getDashboardStats,

  15 | import { doctorRouter } from "./doctor.server";
```

`routers/labTest.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // src/orpc/router/lab-test.ts
   2 | 
   3 | import { z } from "zod";
   4 | 
   5 | import { generateId } from "@clinic/db/utils/id";
   6 | import { labsRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   7 | 
   8 | import { protectedProcedure } from "../index";
   9 | 
  10 | export const LabTestSchema = z.object({
  11 | 	id: z.string(),
  12 | 	patientId: z.string().nullable(),
  13 | 	recordId: z.string(),
  14 | 	serviceId: z.string(),
  15 | 	testDate: z.date(),
  16 | 	result: z.string(),
  17 | 	status: z.enum(["PENDING", "IN_PROGRESS", "COMPLETED", "CANCELLED"]),
  18 | 	notes: z.string().nullable().optional(),
  19 | 	createdAt: z.date().optional(),
  20 | 	updatedAt: z.date().optional()
  21 | });
  22 | 
  23 | export const labTestRouter = {
  24 | 	create: protectedProcedure
  25 | 		.input(LabTestSchema.omit({ id: true, createdAt: true, updatedAt: true }))
  26 | 		.output(LabTestSchema)
  27 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  28 | 			const id = generateId();
  29 | 			const newTest = await labsRepo.createLabTest({
  30 | 				...input,
  31 | 				id
  32 | 			});
  33 | 			if (!newTest) throw new Error("Failed to create lab test order");
  34 | 			return newTest;
  35 | 		}),
  36 | 
  37 | 	get: protectedProcedure
  38 | 		.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
  39 | 		.output(LabTestSchema.nullable())
  40 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  41 | 			const result = await labsRepo.getById(input.id);
  42 | 			return result ?? null;
  43 | 		}),
  44 | 
  45 | 	listByPatient: protectedProcedure
  46 | 		.input(z.object({ patientId: z.string() }))
  47 | 		.output(z.array(LabTestSchema))
  48 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  49 | 			return await labsRepo.getByPatientId(input.patientId);
  50 | 		}),
  51 | 
  52 | 	updateResults: protectedProcedure
  53 | 		.input(
  54 | 			z.object({
  55 | 				id: z.string(),
  56 | 				result: z.string(),
  57 | 				status: z.enum(["COMPLETED", "IN_PROGRESS"]).default("COMPLETED"),
  58 | 				notes: z.string().optional()
  59 | 			})
  60 | 		)
  61 | 		.output(LabTestSchema)
  62 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  63 | 			const updated = await labsRepo.updateLabTest(input.id, {
  64 | 				...input,
  65 | 				updatedAt: new Date()
  66 | 			});
  67 | 			if (!updated) throw new Error("Lab test not found");
  68 | 			return updated;
  69 | 		}),
  70 | 
  71 | 	delete: protectedProcedure
  72 | 		.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
  73 | 		.output(z.boolean())
  74 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  75 | 			await labsRepo.deleteLabTest(input.id);
  76 | 			return true;
  77 | 		}),
  78 | 
  79 | 	getPendingTests: protectedProcedure
  80 | 		.input(z.object({ clinicId: z.string().optional() }))
  81 | 		.output(z.array(LabTestSchema))
  82 | 		.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  83 | 			const clinicId = input.clinicId ?? context.clinicId ?? "";
  84 | 			return await labsRepo.getPendingLabTests();
  85 | 		})
  86 | };

```

`routers/medical-record.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // orpc/router/medical-record.router.ts
   2 | 
   3 | import z from "zod";
   4 | 
   5 | import { appointmentRepo, medicalRepo, patientRepo, pediatricRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   6 | import { appointmentStatusEnum } from "@clinic/db/schema/index";
   7 | import { generateId } from "@clinic/db/utils/id";
   8 | import {
   9 |   DiagnosisCreateSchema,
  10 |   DiagnosisSchema,
  11 |   GrowthRecordSchema,
  12 |   MedicalRecordCreateSchema,
  13 |   MedicalRecordSchema,
  14 |   MedicalRecordUpdateSchema,
  15 |   VitalSignSchema
  16 | } from "@clinic/db/zod";
  17 | import { adminProcedure, o, protectedProcedure } from "../index";
  18 | 
  19 | export const medicalRecordProcedures = {
  20 | 	completeEncounter: adminProcedure
  21 | 		.input(
  22 | 			z.object({
  23 | 				medicalRecordId: z.string(),
  24 | 				diagnosisId: z.string().optional(),
  25 | 				notes: z.string().optional(),
  26 | 				followUpDate: z.date().optional(),
  27 | 				prescribedMedications: z
  28 | 					.array(
  29 | 						z.object({
  30 | 							drugId: z.string(),
  31 | 							dosageValue: z.number(),
  32 | 							dosageUnit: z.string(),
  33 | 							frequency: z.enum([
  34 | 								"ONCE_DAILY",
  35 | 								"TWICE_DAILY",
  36 | 								"THREE_TIMES_DAILY",
  37 | 								"FOUR_TIMES_DAILY",
  38 | 								"EVERY_OTHER_DAY",
  39 | 								"WEEKLY",
  40 | 								"MONTHLY",
  41 | 								"AS_NEEDED"
  42 | 							]),
  43 | 							duration: z.string(),
  44 | 							instructions: z.string().optional()
  45 | 						})
  46 | 					)
  47 | 					.optional()
  48 | 			})
  49 | 		)
  50 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  51 | 			return await medicalRepo.completeEncounter({
  52 | 				medicalRecordId: input.medicalRecordId,
  53 | 				diagnosisId: input.diagnosisId,
  54 | 				notes: input.notes,
  55 | 				followUpDate: input.followUpDate,
  56 | 				prescribedMedications: input.prescribedMedications?.map(m => ({
  57 | 					...m,
  58 | 					frequency: m.frequency
  59 | 				}))
  60 | 			});
  61 | 		}),
  62 | 
  63 | 	addVitalSignsToMedicalRecord: adminProcedure
  64 | 		.input(
  65 | 			z.object({
  66 | 				medicalRecordId: z.string(),
  67 | 				vitalSigns: z.object({
  68 | 					patientId: z.string(),
  69 | 					clinicId: z.string().optional(),
  70 | 					temperature: z.number().optional(),
  71 | 					bloodPressureSystolic: z.number().optional(),
  72 | 					bloodPressureDiastolic: z.number().optional(),
  73 | 					heartRate: z.number().optional(),
  74 | 					respiratoryRate: z.number().optional(),
  75 | 					oxygenSaturation: z.number().min(0).max(100).optional(),
  76 | 					weight: z.number().optional(),
  77 | 					height: z.number().optional()
  78 | 				})
  79 | 			})
  80 | 		)
  81 | 		.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  82 | 			const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  83 | 			return await medicalRepo.addVitalSignsToMedicalRecord(input.medicalRecordId, {
  84 | 				...input.vitalSigns,
  85 | 				clinicId
  86 | 			});
  87 | 		})
  88 | } as const;
  89 | 
  90 | // ================ MEDICAL RECORD PROCEDURES ================
  91 | 
  92 | // Create complete medical record with diagnosis and vitals
  93 | export const createMedicalRecord = protectedProcedure
  94 | 	.input(
  95 | 		z.object({
  96 | 			record: MedicalRecordCreateSchema,
  97 | 			diagnosis: DiagnosisCreateSchema.optional(),
  98 | 			vitals: VitalSignSchema.optional()
  99 | 		})
 100 | 	)
 101 | 	.output(MedicalRecordSchema)
 102 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 103 | 		const recordId = generateId();
 104 | 
 105 | 		// Create medical record
 106 | 		const record = await medicalRepo.createMedicalRecord({
 107 | 			id: recordId,
 108 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 109 | 			doctorId: input.record.doctorId,
 110 | 			patientId: input.record.patientId,
 111 | 			appointmentId: input.record.appointmentId,
 112 | 			diagnosisDate: input.record.diagnosisDate
 113 | 		});
 114 | 
 115 | 		// Create diagnosis if provided
 116 | 		if (input.diagnosis) {
 117 | 			await medicalRepo.createDiagnosis({
 118 | 				id: generateId(),
 119 | 				medicalId: recordId,
 120 | 				patientId: input.record.patientId,
 121 | 				doctorId: input.diagnosis.doctorId ?? "",
 122 | 				appointmentId: input.record.appointmentId,
 123 | 				symptoms: input.diagnosis.symptoms,
 124 | 				diagnosis: input.diagnosis.diagnosis,
 125 | 				treatment: input.diagnosis.treatment,
 126 | 				type: input.diagnosis.type,
 127 | 				notes: input.diagnosis.notes,
 128 | 				prescribedMedications: input.diagnosis.prescribedMedications,
 129 | 				followUpPlan: input.diagnosis.followUpPlan,
 130 | 				date: new Date(),
 131 | 				createdAt: new Date(),
 132 | 				updatedAt: new Date()
 133 | 			});
 134 | 		}
 135 | 
 136 | 		// Create vitals if provided
 137 | 		if (input.vitals) {
 138 | 			await medicalRepo.createVitalSign({
 139 | 				id: generateId(),
 140 | 				medicalId: recordId,
 141 | 				patientId: input.vitals.patientId,
 142 | 				encounterId: input.vitals.encounterId,
 143 | 				bodyTemperature: input.vitals.bodyTemperature,
 144 | 				systolic: input.vitals.systolic,
 145 | 				diastolic: input.vitals.diastolic,
 146 | 				heartRate: input.vitals.heartRate,
 147 | 				respiratoryRate: input.vitals.respiratoryRate,
 148 | 				oxygenSaturation: input.vitals.oxygenSaturation,
 149 | 				gender: input.vitals.gender,
 150 | 				notes: input.vitals.notes,
 151 | 				ageDays: input.vitals.ageDays,
 152 | 				ageMonths: input.vitals.ageMonths,
 153 | 				recordedAt: new Date(),
 154 | 				createdAt: new Date(),
 155 | 				updatedAt: new Date()
 156 | 			});
 157 | 		}
 158 | 
 159 | 		if (!record) {
 160 | 			throw new Error("Failed to create medical record");
 161 | 		}
 162 | 
 163 | 		return record as z.infer<typeof MedicalRecordSchema>;
 164 | 	});
 165 | 
 166 | // Get medical record by ID with full relations
 167 | export const getMedicalRecordById = protectedProcedure
 168 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 169 | 	.output(
 170 | 		MedicalRecordSchema.extend({
 171 | 			patient: z
 172 | 				.object({
 173 | 					id: z.string(),
 174 | 					firstName: z.string(),
 175 | 					lastName: z.string(),
 176 | 					dateOfBirth: z.date(),
 177 | 					gender: z.string().nullable(),
 178 | 					mrn: z.string().nullable()
 179 | 				})
 180 | 				.nullable(),
 181 | 			doctor: z
 182 | 				.object({
 183 | 					id: z.string(),
 184 | 					name: z.string(),
 185 | 					specialty: z.string()
 186 | 				})
 187 | 				.nullable(),
 188 | 			appointment: z
 189 | 				.object({
 190 | 					id: z.string(),
 191 | 					appointmentDate: z.date(),
 192 | 					status: z.enum(appointmentStatusEnum.enumValues).nullable()
 193 | 				})
 194 | 				.nullable(),
 195 | 			encounter: z.array(DiagnosisSchema).nullable(),
 196 | 			vitalSigns: z.array(VitalSignSchema).nullable(),
 197 | 			prescriptions: z.array(z.any()).nullable()
 198 | 		})
 199 | 	)
 200 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 201 | 		const record = await medicalRepo.getMedicalRecordById(input.id, context.clinicId ?? "");
 202 | 
 203 | 		if (!record) {
 204 | 			throw new Error("Medical record not found");
 205 | 		}
 206 | 
 207 | 		return {
 208 | 			...record,
 209 | 			encounter: (record.encounters ?? []).map(e => {
 210 | 				return {
 211 | 					...e,
 212 | 					type: e.type ?? null,
 213 | 					diagnosis: e.diagnosis ?? null,
 214 | 					treatment: e.treatment ?? null
 215 | 				};
 216 | 			})
 217 | 		};
 218 | 	});
 219 | 
 220 | // Get patient medical history (using only queries from queries.ts)
 221 | export const getPatientMedicalHistory = protectedProcedure
 222 | 	.input(
 223 | 		z.object({
 224 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 225 | 			limit: z.number().default(20),
 226 | 			offset: z.number().default(0),
 227 | 			includeDeleted: z.boolean().default(false)
 228 | 		})
 229 | 	)
 230 | 	.output(
 231 | 		z.object({
 232 | 			records: z.array(
 233 | 				MedicalRecordSchema.extend({
 234 | 					doctor: z
 235 | 						.object({
 236 | 							id: z.string(),
 237 | 							name: z.string(),
 238 | 							specialty: z.string()
 239 | 						})
 240 | 						.nullable(),
 241 | 					appointment: z
 242 | 						.object({
 243 | 							id: z.string(),
 244 | 							appointmentDate: z.date()
 245 | 						})
 246 | 						.nullable(),
 247 | 					diagnosisCount: z.number(),
 248 | 					vitalSignsCount: z.number()
 249 | 				})
 250 | 			),
 251 | 			total: z.number(),
 252 | 			hasMore: z.boolean()
 253 | 		})
 254 | 	)
 255 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 256 | 		const { patientId, limit, offset, includeDeleted } = input;
 257 | 
 258 | 		// Use the patient query to get full history
 259 | 		const patientHistory = await patientRepo.getPatientFullHistory(patientId, context.clinicId ?? "");
 260 | 
 261 | 		if (!patientHistory) {
 262 | 			return { records: [], total: 0, hasMore: false };
 263 | 		}
 264 | 
 265 | 		// Filter medical records based on includeDeleted flag
 266 | 		const filteredRecords = includeDeleted
 267 | 			? patientHistory.medicalRecords
 268 | 			: patientHistory.medicalRecords.filter(record => !record.isDeleted);
 269 | 
 270 | 		// Apply pagination
 271 | 		const paginatedRecords = filteredRecords.slice(offset, offset + limit);
 272 | 
 273 | 		// Enrich records with counts
 274 | 		const enrichedRecords = paginatedRecords.map(record => ({
 275 | 			...record,
 276 | 			diagnosisCount: record.encounters?.length || 0,
 277 | 			vitalSignsCount: record.vitalSigns?.length || 0,
 278 | 			doctor: record.doctor
 279 | 				? {
 280 | 						id: record.doctor.id,
 281 | 						name: record.doctor.name,
 282 | 						specialty: record.doctor.specialty
 283 | 					}
 284 | 				: null,
 285 | 			appointment: record.appointment
 286 | 				? {
 287 | 						id: record.appointment.id,
 288 | 						appointmentDate: record.appointment.appointmentDate
 289 | 					}
 290 | 				: null
 291 | 		}));
 292 | 
 293 | 		const total = filteredRecords.length;
 294 | 		const hasMore = offset + limit < total;
 295 | 
 296 | 		return { records: enrichedRecords, total, hasMore };
 297 | 	});
 298 | // Update medical record
 299 | export const updateMedicalRecord = protectedProcedure
 300 | 	.input(

 302 | 			id: z.string(),

 304 | 		})
 305 | 	)
 306 | 	.output(MedicalRecordSchema)
 307 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 308 | 		const updated = await medicalRepo.updateMedicalRecord(input.id, input.data);
 309 | 
 310 | 		if (!updated) {
 311 | 			throw new Error("Medical record not found");
 312 | 		}
 313 | 
 314 | 		return updated;
 315 | 	});

 449 | 						.nullable()
 450 | 				})
 451 | 			),
 452 | 			total: z.number()
 453 | 		})
 454 | 	)
 455 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 456 | 		const { limit, offset, patientId, doctorId } = input;
 457 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 458 | 
 459 | 		const records = await medicalRepo.listMedicalRecord(patientId, doctorId, clinicId, limit, offset);
 460 | 
 461 | 		const total = await medicalRepo.countMedicalRecord(clinicId, patientId, doctorId);
 462 | 
 463 | 		const formattedRecords = records.map(record => ({
 464 | 			...record,
 465 | 			patient: record.patient
 466 | 				? {
 467 | 						id: record.patient.id,
 468 | 						firstName: record.patient.firstName,
 469 | 						lastName: record.patient.lastName ?? null
 470 | 					}
 471 | 				: null,
 472 | 			doctor: record.doctor
 473 | 				? {
 474 | 						id: record.doctor.id,
 475 | 						name: record.doctor.name
 476 | 					}
 477 | 				: null
 478 | 		}));
 479 | 
 480 | 		return {
 481 | 			records: formattedRecords,
 482 | 			total
 483 | 		};
 484 | 	});
 485 | // ================ COMPLETE MEDICAL ENCOUNTER ================
 486 | 
 487 | // Create a complete medical encounter (record + diagnosis + vitals)
 488 | export const createCompleteEncounter = protectedProcedure
 489 | 	.input(
 490 | 		z.object({
 491 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 492 | 			appointmentId: z.string(),
 493 | 			doctorId: z.string(),
 494 | 			diagnosis: z.object({
 495 | 				symptoms: z.string(),
 496 | 				diagnosis: z.string().optional(),
 497 | 				treatment: z.string().optional(),
 498 | 				type: z.string().optional(),
 499 | 				prescribedMedications: z.string().optional(),
 500 | 				followUpPlan: z.string().optional()
 501 | 			}),
 502 | 			vitals: z
 503 | 				.object({
 504 | 					bodyTemperature: z.number().optional(),
 505 | 					systolic: z.number().optional(),
 506 | 					diastolic: z.number().optional(),
 507 | 					heartRate: z.number().optional(),
 508 | 					respiratoryRate: z.number().optional(),
 509 | 					oxygenSaturation: z.number().optional(),
 510 | 					notes: z.string().optional()
 511 | 				})
 512 | 				.optional(),
 513 | 			medicalRecord: z
 514 | 				.object({
 515 | 					notes: z.string().optional(),
 516 | 					treatmentPlan: z.string().optional(),
 517 | 					labRequest: z.string().optional(),
 518 | 					medications: z.string().optional(),
 519 | 					followUpDate: z.date().optional()
 520 | 				})
 521 | 				.optional(),
 522 | 			growth: z
 523 | 				.object({
 524 | 					weight: z.number().optional(),
 525 | 					height: z.number().optional(),
 526 | 					headCircumference: z.number().optional(),
 527 | 					notes: z.string().optional()
 528 | 				})
 529 | 				.optional()
 530 | 		})
 531 | 	)
 532 | 	.output(
 533 | 		z.object({
 534 | 			medicalRecord: MedicalRecordSchema,
 535 | 			diagnosis: DiagnosisSchema,
 536 | 			vitalSigns: VitalSignSchema.optional(),
 537 | 			growthRecord: GrowthRecordSchema.optional()
 538 | 		})
 539 | 	)
 540 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 541 | 		const recordId = generateId();
 542 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 543 | 
 544 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 545 | 			throw new Error("Clinic ID is required - not authenticated to a clinic");
 546 | 		}
 547 | 
 548 | 		// Update appointment status to completed
 549 | 		await appointmentRepo.updateAppointment(input.appointmentId, {
 550 | 			status: "COMPLETED"
 551 | 		});
 552 | 		// Create medical record
 553 | 		const record = await medicalRepo.createMedicalRecord({
 554 | 			id: recordId,
 555 | 			clinicId,
 556 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 557 | 			appointmentId: input.appointmentId,
 558 | 			doctorId: input.doctorId,
 559 | 			notes: input.medicalRecord?.notes,
 560 | 			treatmentPlan: input.medicalRecord?.treatmentPlan,
 561 | 			labRequest: input.medicalRecord?.labRequest,
 562 | 			medications: input.medicalRecord?.medications,
 563 | 			followUpDate: input.medicalRecord?.followUpDate,
 564 | 			diagnosisDate: new Date(),
 565 | 			status: "ACTIVE",
 566 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
 567 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
 568 | 		});
 569 | 
 570 | 		// Create diagnosis
 571 | 		const diagnosisRecord = await medicalRepo.createDiagnosis({
 572 | 			medicalId: recordId,
 573 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 574 | 			doctorId: input.doctorId,
 575 | 			appointmentId: input.appointmentId,
 576 | 			symptoms: input.diagnosis.symptoms,
 577 | 			diagnosis: input.diagnosis.diagnosis,
 578 | 			treatment: input.diagnosis.treatment,
 579 | 			type: input.diagnosis.type,
 580 | 			prescribedMedications: input.diagnosis.prescribedMedications,
 581 | 			followUpPlan: input.diagnosis.followUpPlan,
 582 | 			date: new Date(),
 583 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
 584 | 			updatedAt: new Date(),
 585 | 			id: ""
 586 | 		});
 587 | 
 588 | 		if (!(record && diagnosisRecord)) {
 589 | 			throw new Error("Failed to create encounter records");
 590 | 		}
 591 | 
 592 | 		let vitalRecord: z.infer<typeof VitalSignSchema> | undefined;
 593 | 
 594 | 		// Create vitals if provided
 595 | 		if (input.vitals) {
 596 | 			const vital = await medicalRepo.createVitalSign({
 597 | 				id: generateId(),
 598 | 				medicalId: recordId,
 599 | 				patientId: input.patientId,
 600 | 				encounterId: diagnosisRecord.id,
 601 | 				bodyTemperature: input.vitals.bodyTemperature,
 602 | 				systolic: input.vitals.systolic,
 603 | 				diastolic: input.vitals.diastolic,
 604 | 				heartRate: input.vitals.heartRate,
 605 | 				respiratoryRate: input.vitals.respiratoryRate,
 606 | 				oxygenSaturation: input.vitals.oxygenSaturation,
 607 | 				notes: input.vitals.notes,
 608 | 				recordedAt: new Date(),
 609 | 				createdAt: new Date(),
 610 | 				updatedAt: new Date()
 611 | 			});
 612 | 
 613 | 			vitalRecord = vital;
 614 | 		}
 615 | 
 616 | 		let growth: z.infer<typeof GrowthRecordSchema> | undefined;
 617 | 
 618 | 		// Create growth record if provided
 619 | 		if (input.growth) {
 620 | 			const newGrowth = await pediatricRepo.recordGrowthWithPercentiles({
 621 | 				patientId: input.patientId,
 622 | 				weight: input.growth.weight,
 623 | 				height: input.growth.height,
 624 | 				headCircumference: input.growth.headCircumference,
 625 | 				notes: input.growth.notes,
 626 | 				date: new Date(),
 627 | 				recordedAt: new Date(),
 628 | 				createdAt: new Date(),
 629 | 				updatedAt: new Date()
 630 | 			});
 631 | 			growth = newGrowth;
 632 | 		}
 633 | 
 634 | 		return {
 635 | 			medicalRecord: record,
 636 | 			diagnosis: diagnosisRecord,
 637 | 			vitalSigns: vitalRecord,
 638 | 			growthRecord: growth
 639 | 		};
 640 | 	});
 641 | 
 642 | export const medicalRecordRouter = o.router({
 643 | 	list: listMedicalRecords,
 644 | 	create: createMedicalRecord,
 645 | 	getById: getMedicalRecordById,
 646 | 	getPatientHistory: getPatientMedicalHistory,
 647 | 	update: updateMedicalRecord,
 648 | 	delete: deleteMedicalRecord,
 649 | 	getDiagnoses: getDiagnosesByMedicalRecord,
 650 | 	createDiagnosis,
 651 | 	updateDiagnosis,
 652 | 	getVitalSigns: getVitalSignsByMedicalRecord,
 653 | 	createVitalSign,
 654 | 	getLatestVitalSigns,
 655 | 	createCompleteEncounter
 656 | });
```

`routers/notifications.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { z } from "zod";
   2 | 
   3 | import { queries } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   4 | 
   5 | import { adminProcedure, protectedProcedure } from "../index";
   6 | 
   7 | export const listNotifications = protectedProcedure
   8 | 	.input(
   9 | 		z.object({
  10 | 			status: z.enum(["all", "read", "unread"]).default("all"),
  11 | 			type: z.string().nullish(),
  12 | 			search: z.string().default(""),
  13 | 			limit: z.number().default(20),
  14 | 			offset: z.number().default(0)
  15 | 		})
  16 | 	)
  17 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  18 | 		const { status, type, search, limit, offset } = input;
  19 | 		const userId = context.user?.id ?? "";
  20 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId;
  21 | 
  22 | 		const result = await queries.system.listNotifications({
  23 | 			userId,
  24 | 			clinicId: clinicId ?? undefined,
  25 | 			status: status,
  26 | 			type: type ?? undefined,
  27 | 			search,
  28 | 			limit,
  29 | 			offset
  30 | 		});
  31 | 
  32 | 		return {
  33 | 			notifications: result.items,
  34 | 			total: result.total,
  35 | 			unreadCount: result.unreadCount,
  36 | 			hasMore: offset + limit < result.total
  37 | 		};
  38 | 	});
  39 | 
  40 | export const getUserNotifications = protectedProcedure.handler(async ({ context }) => {
  41 | 	const userId = context.user?.id ?? "";
  42 | 	const clinicId = context.clinicId;
  43 | 
  44 | 	return await queries.system.getUserNotifications(userId, clinicId ?? undefined, 5);
  45 | });
  46 | 
  47 | export const createNotification = protectedProcedure
  48 | 	.input(
  49 | 		z.object({
  50 | 			userId: z.string(),
  51 | 			title: z.string(),
  52 | 			clinicId: z.string().nullish(),
  53 | 			type: z.string(),
  54 | 			body: z.string(),
  55 | 			priority: z.enum(["low", "medium", "high"]).default("medium"),
  56 | 			metadata: z.record(z.string(), z.string()).nullish(),
  57 | 			actions: z
  58 | 				.array(
  59 | 					z.object({
  60 | 						id: z.string(),
  61 | 						label: z.string(),
  62 | 						type: z.enum(["redirect", "workflow", "none"]),
  63 | 						payload: z.record(z.string(), z.any()).optional()
  64 | 					})
  65 | 				)
  66 | 				.nullish()
  67 | 		})
  68 | 	)
  69 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  70 | 		const { userId, clinicId, type, body, actions, title, priority, metadata } = input;
  71 | 
  72 | 		const newNotification = await queries.system.createNotifications({
  73 | 			id: crypto.randomUUID(),
  74 | 			userId,
  75 | 			title,
  76 | 			clinicId: clinicId ?? "",
  77 | 			type,
  78 | 			body,
  79 | 			priority,
  80 | 			metadata: metadata ?? {},
  81 | 			actions: actions ?? [],
  82 | 			status: "unread",
  83 | 			createdAt: new Date()
  84 | 		});
  85 | 
  86 | 		return newNotification;
  87 | 	});
  88 | 
  89 | export const markAsRead = protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.string() })).handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  90 | 	await queries.system.markNotificationsAsRead(input.id, context.user?.id);
  91 | 	return { success: true };
  92 | });
  93 | 
  94 | export const markAllAsRead = protectedProcedure.handler(async ({ context }) => {
  95 | 	const userId = context.user?.id ?? "";
  96 | 	const clinicId = context.clinicId;
  97 | 
  98 | 	await queries.system.markAllNotificationsAsRead(userId, clinicId ?? undefined);
  99 | 	return { success: true };
 100 | });
 101 | 
 102 | export const deleteNotification = protectedProcedure
 103 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 104 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 105 | 		await queries.system.deleteNotification(input.id, context.user?.id ?? "");
 106 | 		return { success: true };
 107 | 	});
 108 | 
 109 | export const clearAll = protectedProcedure.handler(async ({ context }) => {
 110 | 	const userId = context.user?.id ?? "";
 111 | 	const clinicId = context.clinicId;
 112 | 
 113 | 	await queries.system.clearAllNotifications(userId, clinicId ?? undefined);
 114 | 	return { success: true };
 115 | });
 116 | 
 117 | export const notificationRouter = {
 118 | 	list: listNotifications,
 119 | 	get: getUserNotifications,
 120 | 	create: createNotification,
 121 | 	markAsRead,
 122 | 	markAllAsRead,
 123 | 	delete: deleteNotification,
 124 | 	clearAll
 125 | };
 126 | export const notificationProcedures = {
 127 | 	getUserNotifications: adminProcedure
 128 | 		.input(
 129 | 			z.object({
 130 | 				userId: z.string(),
 131 | 				limit: z.number().min(1).max(100).default(20),
 132 | 				offset: z.number().min(0).default(0)
 133 | 			})
 134 | 		)
 135 | 		.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 136 | 			const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 137 | 			return await queries.system.getUserNotifications(input.userId, clinicId, input.limit, input.offset);
 138 | 		}),
 139 | 
 140 | 	markNotificationAsRead: adminProcedure
 141 | 		.input(z.object({ notificationId: z.string() }))
 142 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 143 | 			return await queries.system.markNotificationsAsRead(input.notificationId);
 144 | 		}),
 145 | 
 146 | 	markAllNotificationsAsRead: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ userId: z.string() })).handler(async ({ input }) => {
 147 | 		return await queries.system.markAllNotificationsAsRead(input.userId);
 148 | 	})
 149 | } as const;
```
