`routers/nutrition.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // src/orpc/routers/nutrition.server.ts
   2 | 
   3 | import { z } from "zod";
   4 | 
   5 | import type { NutritionalAssessment } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   6 | import { patientRepo, pediatricRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   7 | import { feedingTypeEnum } from "@clinic/db/schema";
   8 | import { generateId } from "@clinic/db/utils/id";
   9 | import { protectedProcedure } from "../index";
  10 | 
  11 | // ============================================
  12 | // Schemas
  13 | // ============================================
  14 | 
  15 | const FeedingLogSchema = z.object({
  16 | 	id: z.string(),
  17 | 	patientId: z.string(),
  18 | 	date: z.date(),
  19 | 	type: z.enum(feedingTypeEnum.enumValues),
  20 | 	duration: z.number().optional(),
  21 | 	amount: z.number().optional(),
  22 | 	breast: z.enum(["LEFT", "RIGHT", "BOTH"]).optional(),
  23 | 	notes: z.string().optional()
  24 | });
  25 | 
  26 | const CreateFeedingLogSchema = FeedingLogSchema.omit({ id: true });
  27 | 
  28 | const UpdateFeedingLogSchema = CreateFeedingLogSchema.partial();
  29 | 
  30 | const GetNutritionDataSchema = z.object({
  31 | 	patientId: z.string(),
  32 | 	startDate: z.date().optional(),
  33 | 	endDate: z.date().optional()
  34 | });
  35 | 
  36 | const GetFeedingSummarySchema = z.object({
  37 | 	patientId: z.string(),
  38 | 	days: z.number().min(1).max(365).default(30)
  39 | });
  40 | 
  41 | const NutritionAssessmentOutputSchema = z.object({
  42 | 	patientId: z.string(),
  43 | 	assessmentDate: z.date(),
  44 | 	nutritionalStatus: z.enum(["NORMAL", "UNDERWEIGHT", "OVERWEIGHT", "OBESE", "MALNOURISHED"]),
  45 | 	dietaryRestrictions: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
  46 | 	recommendations: z.array(z.string()),
  47 | 	followUpDate: z.date().optional(),
  48 | 	notes: z.string().optional()
  49 | });
  50 | 
  51 | // ============================================
  52 | // Helpers
  53 | // ============================================
  54 | 
  55 | /** Map a DB feedingLog row to the FeedingLogSchema shape. */
  56 | function mapFeedingLog(log: {
  57 | 	id: string;
  58 | 	patientId: string;
  59 | 	date: Date;
  60 | 	type: (typeof feedingTypeEnum.enumValues)[number];
  61 | 	duration: number | null;
  62 | 	amount: number | null;
  63 | 	breast: "LEFT" | "RIGHT" | "BOTH" | null;
  64 | 	notes: string | null;
  65 | }) {
  66 | 	return {
  67 | 		id: log.id,
  68 | 		patientId: log.patientId,
  69 | 		date: log.date,
  70 | 		type: log.type,
  71 | 		duration: log.duration ?? undefined,
  72 | 		amount: log.amount ?? undefined,
  73 | 		breast: log.breast ?? undefined,
  74 | 		notes: log.notes ?? undefined
  75 | 	};
  76 | }
  77 | 
  78 | /** Map a NutritionAssessment to the output schema shape. */
  79 | function mapAssessment(a: NutritionalAssessment) {
  80 | 	return {
  81 | 		patientId: a.patientId,
  82 | 		assessmentDate: a.assessmentDate,
  83 | 		nutritionalStatus: a.nutritionalStatus,
  84 | 		dietaryRestrictions: a.dietaryRestrictions,
  85 | 		recommendations: a.recommendations,
  86 | 		followUpDate: a.followUpDate ?? undefined,
  87 | 		notes: a.notes ?? undefined
  88 | 	};
  89 | }
  90 | 
  91 | /** ISO date string without the time component, no non-null assertion needed. */
  92 | function toDateKey(d: Date): string {
  93 | 	return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
  94 | }
  95 | 
  96 | // ============================================
  97 | // Nutrition Procedures
  98 | // ============================================
  99 | 
 100 | // Log a feeding record
 101 | export const logFeeding = protectedProcedure
 102 | 	.input(CreateFeedingLogSchema)
 103 | 	.output(FeedingLogSchema)
 104 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 105 | 		const feedingLog = await pediatricRepo.createFeedingLog({
 106 | 			...input,
 107 | 			id: generateId()
 108 | 		});
 109 | 
 110 | 		if (!feedingLog) {
 111 | 			throw new Error("Failed to create feeding log");
 112 | 		}
 113 | 
 114 | 		return mapFeedingLog(feedingLog);
 115 | 	});
 116 | 
 117 | // Update a feeding record
 118 | export const updateFeedingLog = protectedProcedure
 119 | 	.input(
 120 | 		z.object({
 121 | 			id: z.string(),
 122 | 			data: UpdateFeedingLogSchema
 123 | 		})
 124 | 	)
 125 | 	.output(FeedingLogSchema)
 126 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 127 | 		const updated = await pediatricRepo.updateFeedingLog(input.id, input.data);
 128 | 
 129 | 		if (!updated) {
 130 | 			throw new Error("Feeding log not found");
 131 | 		}
 132 | 
 133 | 		return mapFeedingLog(updated);
 134 | 	});
 135 | 
 136 | // Delete a feeding record
 137 | export const deleteFeedingLog = protectedProcedure
 138 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 139 | 	.output(z.object({ success: z.boolean() }))
 140 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 141 | 		await pediatricRepo.deleteFeedingLog(input.id);
 142 | 		return { success: true };
 143 | 	});
 144 | 
 145 | // Get feeding logs for a patient
 146 | // feedingLogQueries.list() returns { logs, total, hasMore } — not a plain array.
 147 | export const getFeedingLogs = protectedProcedure
 148 | 	.input(
 149 | 		z.object({
 150 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 151 | 			limit: z.number().min(1).max(100).default(50),
 152 | 			offset: z.number().default(0),
 153 | 			startDate: z.date().optional(),
 154 | 			endDate: z.date().optional()
 155 | 		})
 156 | 	)
 157 | 	.output(
 158 | 		z.object({
 159 | 			logs: z.array(FeedingLogSchema),
 160 | 			total: z.number(),
 161 | 			hasMore: z.boolean()
 162 | 		})
 163 | 	)
 164 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 165 | 		const { patientId, limit, offset, startDate, endDate } = input;
 166 | 
 167 | 		const result = await pediatricRepo.list({
 168 | 			patientId,
 169 | 			limit,
 170 | 			offset,
 171 | 			startDate,
 172 | 			endDate
 173 | 		} as any);
 174 | 
 175 | 		return {
 176 | 			logs: result.logs.map(mapFeedingLog),
 177 | 			total: result.total,
 178 | 			hasMore: result.hasMore
 179 | 		};
 180 | 	});
 181 | 
 182 | // Get feeding summary statistics
 183 | export const getFeedingSummary = protectedProcedure
 184 | 	.input(GetFeedingSummarySchema)
 185 | 	.output(
 186 | 		z.object({
 187 | 			totalFeedings: z.number(),
 188 | 			byType: z.record(z.string(), z.number()),
 189 | 			averageDuration: z.number(),
 190 | 			totalAmount: z.number(),
 191 | 			feedingsByDay: z.array(
 192 | 				z.object({
 193 | 					date: z.string(),
 194 | 					count: z.number(),
 195 | 					totalDuration: z.number(),
 196 | 					totalAmount: z.number()
 197 | 				})
 198 | 			),
 199 | 			recentFeedings: z.array(FeedingLogSchema)
 200 | 		})
 201 | 	)
 202 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 203 | 		const { patientId, days } = input;
 204 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 205 | 
 206 | 		// feedingLogQueries.getStats already computes all of this efficiently
 207 | 		const stats = await pediatricRepo.getFeedingStats(patientId, clinicId, days);
 208 | 
 209 | 		// Fetch the 10 most recent logs for the recentFeedings field
 210 | 		const recent = await pediatricRepo.list({
 211 | 			patientId,
 212 | 			clinicId,
 213 | 			limit: 10,
 214 | 			offset: 0
 215 | 		});
 216 | 
 217 | 		return {
 218 | 			totalFeedings: stats.totalFeedings,
 219 | 			byType: stats.byType,
 220 | 			averageDuration: stats.averageDuration,
 221 | 			totalAmount: stats.totalAmount,
 222 | 			feedingsByDay: stats.feedingsByDay,
 223 | 			recentFeedings: recent.logs.map(mapFeedingLog)
 224 | 		};
 225 | 	});
 226 | 
 227 | // Get breastfeeding statistics
 228 | export const getBreastfeedingStats = protectedProcedure
 229 | 	.input(
 230 | 		z.object({
 231 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 232 | 			days: z.number().min(1).max(365).default(30)
 233 | 		})
 234 | 	)
 235 | 	.output(
 236 | 		z.object({
 237 | 			todayTotal: z.number(),
 238 | 			weeklyAverage: z.number(),
 239 | 			totalSessions: z.number(),
 240 | 			averageDuration: z.number(),
 241 | 			weeklyData: z.array(
 242 | 				z.object({
 243 | 					date: z.string(),
 244 | 					duration: z.number(),
 245 | 					count: z.number()
 246 | 				})
 247 | 			),
 248 | 			sessionsByTimeOfDay: z.object({
 249 | 				morning: z.number(),
 250 | 				afternoon: z.number(),
 251 | 				evening: z.number(),
 252 | 				night: z.number()
 253 | 			})
 254 | 		})
 255 | 	)
 256 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 257 | 		const { patientId, days } = input;
 258 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 259 | 
 260 | 		// Delegate entirely to the existing query helper which already does all
 261 | 		// the breastfeeding-specific aggregation correctly.
 262 | 		const stats = await pediatricRepo.getBreastfeedingStats(patientId, clinicId, days);
 263 | 
 264 | 		return {
 265 | 			todayTotal: stats.todayTotal,
 266 | 			weeklyAverage: stats.weeklyAverage,
 267 | 			totalSessions: stats.totalSessions,
 268 | 			averageDuration: stats.averageDuration,
 269 | 			// weeklyData from the query includes leftDuration/rightDuration which
 270 | 			// aren't in the output schema — pick only the fields we expose.
 271 | 			weeklyData: stats.weeklyData.map(d => ({
 272 | 				date: d.date,
 273 | 				duration: d.duration,
 274 | 				count: d.count
 275 | 			})),
 276 | 			sessionsByTimeOfDay: stats.sessionsByTimeOfDay
 277 | 		};
 278 | 	});
 279 | 
 280 | // Get nutrition assessment for a patient
 281 | export const getNutritionAssessment = protectedProcedure
 282 | 	.input(
 283 | 		z.object({
 284 | 			patientId: z.string()
 285 | 		})
 286 | 	)
 287 | 	.output(
 288 | 		z.object({
 289 | 			currentAssessment: NutritionAssessmentOutputSchema.nullable(),
 290 | 			history: z.array(NutritionAssessmentOutputSchema)
 291 | 		})
 292 | 	)
 293 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 294 | 		const { patientId } = input;
 295 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 296 | 
 297 | 		// nutritionAssessmentQueries is the correct export — queries.nutrition
 298 | 		// does not exist on the queries barrel object.
 299 | 		const assessments = await pediatricRepo.getAssessments(patientId, clinicId);
 300 | 
 301 | 		const currentAssessment = assessments.length > 0 ? mapAssessment(assessments[0] as NutritionalAssessment) : null;
 302 | 
 303 | 		return {
 304 | 			currentAssessment,
 305 | 			history: assessments.slice(1).map(mapAssessment)
 306 | 		};
 307 | 	});
 308 | 
 309 | // Save nutrition assessment
 310 | // There is no dedicated nutrition_assessment table — assessments are stored
 311 | // as JSON inside medicalRecord.notes (see nutritionAssessmentQueries).
 312 | // mutations.assessment.create wraps that pattern.
 313 | export const saveNutritionAssessment = protectedProcedure
 314 | 	.input(NutritionAssessmentOutputSchema)
 315 | 	.output(NutritionAssessmentOutputSchema)
 316 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 317 | 		const assessment = await pediatricRepo.createNutritionAssessment({
 318 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 319 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 320 | 			nutritionalStatus: input.nutritionalStatus,
 321 | 			recommendations: input.recommendations,
 322 | 			dietaryRestrictions: input.dietaryRestrictions,
 323 | 			createdAt: input.assessmentDate,
 324 | 			updatedAt: input.followUpDate,
 325 | 			notes: input.notes,
 326 | 			id: generateId()
 327 | 		} as any);
 328 | 
 329 | 		if (!assessment) {
 330 | 			throw new Error("Failed to save nutrition assessment");
 331 | 		}
 332 | 
 333 | 		return mapAssessment(assessment as unknown as NutritionalAssessment);
 334 | 	});
 335 | 
 336 | // Update nutrition assessment
 337 | export const updateNutritionAssessment = protectedProcedure
 338 | 	.input(
 339 | 		z.object({
 340 | 			id: z.string(),
 341 | 			data: NutritionAssessmentOutputSchema.partial()
 342 | 		})
 343 | 	)
 344 | 	.output(NutritionAssessmentOutputSchema)
 345 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 346 | 		const updated = await pediatricRepo.updateNutritionAssessment(input.id, {
 347 | 			...input.data,
 348 | 			updatedAt: input.data.followUpDate
 349 | 		} as any);
 350 | 
 351 | 		if (!updated) {
 352 | 			throw new Error("Nutrition assessment not found");
 353 | 		}
 354 | 
 355 | 		return mapAssessment(updated as unknown as NutritionalAssessment);
 356 | 	});
 357 | 
 358 | // Delete nutrition assessment
 359 | export const deleteNutritionAssessment = protectedProcedure
 360 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 361 | 	.output(z.object({ success: z.boolean() }))
 362 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 363 | 		await pediatricRepo.deleteNutritionAssessment(input.id);
 364 | 		return { success: true };
 365 | 	});
 366 | 
 367 | // Get nutrition dashboard data
 368 | export const getNutritionDashboard = protectedProcedure
 369 | 	.input(
 370 | 		z.object({
 371 | 			patientId: z.string()
 372 | 		})
 373 | 	)
 374 | 	.output(
 375 | 		z.object({
 376 | 			feedingSummary: z.object({
 377 | 				totalFeedings: z.number(),
 378 | 				byType: z.record(z.string(), z.number()),
 379 | 				averageDailyFeedings: z.number()
 380 | 			}),
 381 | 			breastfeedingStats: z.object({
 382 | 				todayTotal: z.number(),
 383 | 				weeklyAverage: z.number(),
 384 | 				averageDuration: z.number()
 385 | 			}),
 386 | 			nutritionalStatus: z.object({
 387 | 				status: z.enum(["NORMAL", "UNDERWEIGHT", "OVERWEIGHT", "OBESE", "MALNOURISHED"]),
 388 | 				lastAssessmentDate: z.date().nullable(),
 389 | 				trend: z.enum(["improving", "stable", "declining"]).nullable()
 390 | 			}),
 391 | 			alerts: z.array(
 392 | 				z.object({
 393 | 					type: z.enum(["warning", "info", "success"]),
 394 | 					message: z.string(),
 395 | 					suggestion: z.string().optional()
 396 | 				})
 397 | 			)
 398 | 		})
 399 | 	)
 400 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 401 | 		const { patientId } = input;
 402 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 403 | 
 404 | 		// Run all queries in parallel
 405 | 		const [feedingStats, breastfeedingStats, assessments, patient] = await Promise.all([
 406 | 			pediatricRepo.getFeedingStats(patientId, clinicId, 30),
 407 | 			pediatricRepo.getBreastfeedingStats(patientId, clinicId, 30),
 408 | 			pediatricRepo.getAssessments(patientId, clinicId),
 409 | 			patientRepo.getPatientById(patientId, clinicId)
 410 | 		]);
 411 | 
 412 | 		const currentAssessment = assessments.length > 0 ? (assessments[0] as NutritionalAssessment) : null;
 413 | 
 414 | 		// Average daily feedings
 415 | 		const uniqueDays = feedingStats.feedingsByDay.length;
 416 | 		const averageDailyFeedings = uniqueDays > 0 ? feedingStats.totalFeedings / uniqueDays : 0;
 417 | 
 418 | 		// Generate alerts
 419 | 		const alerts: Array<{
 420 | 			type: "warning" | "info" | "success";
 421 | 			message: string;
 422 | 			suggestion?: string;
 423 | 		}> = [];
 424 | 
 425 | 		// Check feeding frequency for infants (< 6 months)
 426 | 		if (patient) {
 427 | 			const ageInMonths = Math.floor(
 428 | 				(Date.now() - patient.dateOfBirth.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 30.44)
 429 | 			);
 430 | 
 431 | 			if (ageInMonths < 6) {
 432 | 				if (averageDailyFeedings < 6) {
 433 | 					alerts.push({
 434 | 						type: "warning",
 435 | 						message: "Low feeding frequency detected",
 436 | 						suggestion: "Newborns typically feed 8-12 times per day. Consider more frequent feedings."
 437 | 					});
 438 | 				} else if (averageDailyFeedings >= 8) {
 439 | 					alerts.push({
 440 | 						type: "success",
 441 | 						message: "Good feeding frequency",
 442 | 						suggestion: "Continue with current feeding schedule."
 443 | 					});
 444 | 				}
 445 | 			}
 446 | 		}
 447 | 
 448 | 		if (breastfeedingStats.totalSessions === 0 && feedingStats.totalFeedings > 0) {
 449 | 			alerts.push({
 450 | 				type: "info",
 451 | 				message: "No breastfeeding records found",
 452 | 				suggestion: "Consider tracking breastfeeding sessions for better insights."
 453 | 			});
 454 | 		}
 455 | 
 456 | 		if (currentAssessment) {
 457 | 			if (currentAssessment.nutritionalStatus === "UNDERWEIGHT") {
 458 | 				alerts.push({
 459 | 					type: "warning",
 460 | 					message: "Patient is underweight",
 461 | 					suggestion: "Consult with a nutritionist for dietary recommendations."
 462 | 				});
 463 | 			} else if (
 464 | 				currentAssessment.nutritionalStatus === "OVERWEIGHT" ||
 465 | 				currentAssessment.nutritionalStatus === "OBESE"
 466 | 			) {
 467 | 				alerts.push({
 468 | 					type: "warning",
 469 | 					message: "Weight management concern detected",
 470 | 					suggestion: "Review dietary habits and consider physical activity recommendations."
 471 | 				});
 472 | 			} else if (currentAssessment.nutritionalStatus === "NORMAL") {
 473 | 				alerts.push({
 474 | 					type: "success",
 475 | 					message: "Normal nutritional status",
 476 | 					suggestion: "Continue with current healthy habits."
 477 | 				});
 478 | 			}
 479 | 		}
 480 | 
 481 | 		// Calculate trend from assessment history
 482 | 		let trend: "improving" | "stable" | "declining" | null = null;
 483 | 		if (assessments.length >= 2) {
 484 | 			const statusOrder: Record<string, number> = {
 485 | 				MALNOURISHED: 0,
 486 | 				OBESE: 0,
 487 | 				UNDERWEIGHT: 1,
 488 | 				OVERWEIGHT: 1,
 489 | 				NORMAL: 2
 490 | 			};
 491 | 			const currentScore = statusOrder[currentAssessment?.nutritionalStatus ?? "NORMAL"] ?? 1;
 492 | 			const prevScore = statusOrder[assessments[1]?.nutritionalStatus ?? "NORMAL"] ?? 1;
 493 | 
 494 | 			if (currentScore > prevScore) trend = "improving";
 495 | 			else if (currentScore < prevScore) trend = "declining";
 496 | 			else trend = "stable";
 497 | 		}
 498 | 
 499 | 		return {
 500 | 			feedingSummary: {
 501 | 				totalFeedings: feedingStats.totalFeedings,
 502 | 				byType: feedingStats.byType,
 503 | 				averageDailyFeedings: Math.round(averageDailyFeedings * 10) / 10
 504 | 			},
 505 | 			breastfeedingStats: {
 506 | 				todayTotal: breastfeedingStats.todayTotal,
 507 | 				weeklyAverage: breastfeedingStats.weeklyAverage,
 508 | 				averageDuration: breastfeedingStats.averageDuration
 509 | 			},
 510 | 			nutritionalStatus: {
 511 | 				status: currentAssessment?.nutritionalStatus ?? "NORMAL",
 512 | 				lastAssessmentDate: currentAssessment?.assessmentDate ?? null,
 513 | 				trend
 514 | 			},
 515 | 			alerts
 516 | 		};
 517 | 	});
 518 | 
 519 | // Get nutrition data (combined endpoint for the nutrition dashboard page)
 520 | export const getNutritionData = protectedProcedure
 521 | 	.input(GetNutritionDataSchema)
 522 | 	.output(
 523 | 		z.object({
 524 | 			feedingHistory: z.array(FeedingLogSchema),
 525 | 			breastfeeding: z
 526 | 				.object({
 527 | 					records: z.array(FeedingLogSchema),
 528 | 					stats: z.object({
 529 | 						todayTotal: z.number(),
 530 | 						weeklyAverage: z.number(),
 531 | 						totalSessions: z.number(),
 532 | 						averageDuration: z.number()
 533 | 					})
 534 | 				})
 535 | 				.optional(),
 536 | 			assessment: NutritionAssessmentOutputSchema.nullable()
 537 | 		})
 538 | 	)
 539 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 540 | 		const { patientId, startDate, endDate } = input;
 541 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
 542 | 
 543 | 		const actualEndDate = endDate ?? new Date();
 544 | 		const actualStartDate =
 545 | 			startDate ??
 546 | 			(() => {
 547 | 				const d = new Date();
 548 | 				d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - 3);
 549 | 				return d;
 550 | 			})();
 551 | 
 552 | 		// Run all queries in parallel
 553 | 		const [feedingResult, assessments] = await Promise.all([
 554 | 			pediatricRepo.list({
 555 | 				patientId,
 556 | 				clinicId,
 557 | 				startDate: actualStartDate,
 558 | 				endDate: actualEndDate,
 559 | 				limit: 500,
 560 | 				offset: 0
 561 | 			} as any),
 562 | 			pediatricRepo.getAssessments(patientId, clinicId)
 563 | 		]);
 564 | 
 565 | 		const feedingLogs = feedingResult.logs;
 566 | 		const breastfeedingLogs = feedingLogs.filter(log => log.type === "BREAST");
 567 | 
 568 | 		const today = toDateKey(new Date());
 569 | 		const todayFeedings = breastfeedingLogs.filter(log => toDateKey(log.date) === today);
 570 | 
 571 | 		const totalDuration = breastfeedingLogs.reduce((sum: number, log) => sum + (log.duration ?? 0), 0);
 572 | 		const averageDuration = breastfeedingLogs.length > 0 ? totalDuration / breastfeedingLogs.length : 0;
 573 | 
 574 | 		return {
 575 | 			feedingHistory: feedingLogs.map(mapFeedingLog),
 576 | 			breastfeeding: {
 577 | 				records: breastfeedingLogs.map(mapFeedingLog),
 578 | 				stats: {
 579 | 					todayTotal: todayFeedings.length,
 580 | 					weeklyAverage: Math.round(breastfeedingLogs.length / 4),
 581 | 					totalSessions: breastfeedingLogs.length,
 582 | 					averageDuration: Math.round(averageDuration)
 583 | 				}
 584 | 			},
 585 | 			assessment: assessments.length > 0 ? mapAssessment(assessments[0] as NutritionalAssessment) : null
 586 | 		};
 587 | 	});
 588 | 
 589 | // ============================================
 590 | // Export Router
 591 | // ============================================
 592 | 
 593 | export const nutritionRouter = {
 594 | 	// Feeding log operations
 595 | 	logFeeding,
 596 | 	updateFeedingLog,
 597 | 	deleteFeedingLog,
 598 | 	getFeedingLogs,
 599 | 	getFeedingSummary,
 600 | 	getBreastfeedingStats,
 601 | 
 602 | 	// Nutrition assessment operations
 603 | 	getNutritionAssessment,
 604 | 	saveNutritionAssessment,
 605 | 	updateNutritionAssessment,
 606 | 	deleteNutritionAssessment,
 607 | 
 608 | 	// Dashboard endpoints
 609 | 	getNutritionDashboard,
 610 | 	getNutritionData
 611 | };

```

```ts
 247 | // Bulk create patients
 248 | export const bulkCreatePatients = protectedProcedure
 249 | 	.input(z.array(PatientCreateSchema))
 250 | 	.output(z.array(PatientSchema))
 251 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 252 | 		const patientsToInsert = input.map(patientData => {
 253 | 			return {
 254 | 				...patientData,
 255 | 				id: crypto.randomUUID(),
 256 | 				clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 257 | 				createdById: context.user?.id ?? "",
 258 | 				createdAt: new Date(),
 259 | 				updatedAt: new Date()
 260 | 			};
 261 | 		});
 262 | 
 263 | 		const results = await context.db.insert(schema.patient).values(patientsToInsert).returning();
 264 | 		return results;
 265 | 	});
 266 | 
 267 | // Export all procedures
 268 | export const patientRouter = {
 269 | 	getNeonatalAssessment,
 270 | 	create: createPatient,
 271 | 	get: getPatient,
 272 | 	getWithDetails: getPatientWithDetails,
 273 | 	list: listPatients,
 274 | 	update: updatePatient,
 275 | 	delete: deletePatient,
 276 | 	hardDelete: hardDeletePatient,
 277 | 	getStats: getPatientStats,
 278 | 	search: searchPatients,
 279 | 	bulkCreatePatients
 280 | };
```

```ts
  57 | 	const userId = session?.user?.id;
  58 | 
  59 | 	if (!userId) {
  60 | 		throw new ORPCError("UNAUTHORIZED", {
  61 | 			message: "Authentication required"
  62 | 		});

  65 | 	const isAdmin = await checkRole("admin");
  66 | 	const isDoctor = await checkRole("doctor");
  67 |

  69 | 		throw new ORPCError("FORBIDDEN", {
  70 | 			message: "Admin or Doctor access required"
  71 | 		});
  72 | 	}
  73 | 
  74 | 	return { userId, isAdmin, isDoctor };
  75 | };

  85 | 		})
  86 | 		.input(PaymentPaginationSchema)
  87 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  88 | 			await requireAdminOrDoctor();
  89 | 
  90 | 			try {
  91 | 				const PAGE_NUMBER = input.page <= 0 ? 1 : input.page;
  92 | 				const LIMIT = input.limit || 10;
  93 |

  95 | 					page: PAGE_NUMBER,
  96 | 					limit: LIMIT,
  97 | 					search: input.search,

  99 | 					startDate: input.startDate ? new Date(input.startDate) : undefined,
 100 | 					endDate: input.endDate ? new Date(input.endDate) : undefined
 101 | 				});
 102 |

 110 | 				};
 111 | 			} catch (error) {
 112 | 				console.error("Get payment records error:", error);
 113 | 				throw new ORPCError("INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR", {

 115 | 				});
 116 | 			}
```

`routers/prescription.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // src/server/routers/prescription.router.ts
   2 | 
   3 | import { z } from "zod";
   4 | 
   5 | import { type DbDrug, type Frequency, prescriptionStatusEnum } from "@clinic/db/schema";
   6 | 
   7 | import { queries } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   8 | import { generateId } from "@clinic/db/utils/id";
   9 | import { calculateAdherenceMetrics, calculateExpectedDoses, PrescribedItemCreateSchema } from "@clinic/db/zod";
  10 | 
  11 | 
  12 | import { calculateDaysSupply, calculateRefillInterval, generateAdherenceRecommendations, getAdherenceStatus, groupByDoctor, groupByDrug, groupByMonth } from '@clinic/db/helper';
  13 | import { o, protectedProcedure } from "../index";
  14 | // type Patient = InferSelectModel<typeof patient>;
  15 | // Types for enhanced prescriptions
  16 | type PrescriptionWithRelations = NonNullable<
  17 | 	Awaited<ReturnType<typeof queries.pharmacy.getPatientActivePrescriptions>>[number]
  18 | >;
  19 | 
  20 | type EnhancedPrescribedItem = PrescriptionWithRelations["prescribedItems"][number] & {
  21 | 	refillsRemaining: number;
  22 | 	daysSupply: number;
  23 | 	isDueForRefill: boolean;
  24 | };
  25 | 
  26 | type EnhancedPrescription = Omit<PrescriptionWithRelations, "prescribedItems"> & {
  27 | 	items: EnhancedPrescribedItem[];
  28 | };
  29 | 
  30 | // Create prescription with drug interaction checking
  31 | export const createPrescription = protectedProcedure
  32 | 	.input(
  33 | 		z.object({
  34 | 			medicalRecordId: z.string(),
  35 | 			patientId: z.string(),
  36 | 			doctorId: z.string(),
  37 | 			encounterId: z.string(),
  38 | 			items: z.array(PrescribedItemCreateSchema),
  39 | 			notes: z.string().optional(),
  40 | 			validUntil: z.date().optional()
  41 | 		})
  42 | 	)
  43 | 	.output(
  44 | 		z.object({
  45 | 			id: z.string(),
  46 | 			medicalRecordId: z.string(),
  47 | 			patientId: z.string(),
  48 | 			doctorId: z.string().nullable(),
  49 | 			encounterId: z.string(),
  50 | 			clinicId: z.string().nullable(),
  51 | 			status: z.enum(prescriptionStatusEnum.enumValues),
  52 | 			items: z.array(
  53 | 				z.object({
  54 | 					id: z.string(),
  55 | 					drugId: z.string(),
  56 | 					dosageValue: z.number(),
  57 | 					dosageUnit: z.string(),
  58 | 					frequency: z.string()
  59 | 				})
  60 | 			),
  61 | 			interactions: z.array(
  62 | 				z.object({
  63 | 					drug1: z.string().optional(),
  64 | 					drug2: z.string().optional(),
  65 | 					severity: z.enum(["moderate", "high"]),
  66 | 					recommendation: z.string()
  67 | 				})
  68 | 			),
  69 | 			doseCalculations: z.array(
  70 | 				z.object({
  71 | 					drugId: z.string(),
  72 | 					drugName: z.string().optional(),
  73 | 					recommendedDose: z.number(),
  74 | 					prescribedDose: z.number()
  75 | 				})
  76 | 			),
  77 | 			warnings: z.array(z.string())
  78 | 		})
  79 | 	)
  80 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  81 | 		const prescriptionId = crypto.randomUUID();
  82 | 
  83 | 		// Get patient details for dose calculation
  84 | 		const patientData = await queries.patient.getPatientFullHistory(input.patientId, context.clinicId ?? "");
  85 | 		const growthRecordData = patientData?.growthRecords?.[0];
  86 | 
  87 | 		let weight = 0;
  88 | 		if (growthRecordData) {
  89 | 			weight = growthRecordData.weight ?? 0;
  90 | 		}
  91 | 
  92 | 		if (!patientData) {
  93 | 			throw new Error("Patient not found");
  94 | 		}
  95 | 
  96 | 		// Calculate patient age in days for dosing
  97 | 		const patientAgeInDays = Math.floor(
  98 | 			(Date.now() - new Date(patientData.dateOfBirth).getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)
  99 | 		);
 100 | 
 101 | 		// Check for drug interactions and allergies
 102 | 		const drugIds = input.items.map(item => item.drugId);
 103 | 		const drugsData = await queries.pharmacy.getDrugsByIds(drugIds);
 104 | 
 105 | 		const drugMap = new Map(drugsData.map(d => [d.id, d]));
 106 | 
 107 | 		// Check for potential interactions
 108 | 		const interactions: Array<{
 109 | 			drug1: string | undefined;
 110 | 			drug2: string | undefined;
 111 | 			severity: "moderate" | "high";
 112 | 			recommendation: string;
 113 | 		}> = [];
 114 | 		for (let i = 0; i < input.items.length; i++) {
 115 | 			for (let j = i + 1; j < input.items.length; j++) {
 116 | 				const drug1 = drugMap.get(input.items[i]?.drugId ?? "");
 117 | 				const drug2 = drugMap.get(input.items[j]?.drugId ?? "");
 118 | 				if (
 119 | 					drug1?.interactions?.includes(drug2?.name ?? "") ||
 120 | 					drug2?.interactions?.includes(drug1?.name ?? "")
 121 | 				) {
 122 | 					interactions.push({
 123 | 						drug1: drug1?.name,
 124 | 						drug2: drug2?.name,
 125 | 						severity: "moderate",
 126 | 						recommendation: "Monitor patient closely for adverse effects"
 127 | 					});
 128 | 				}
 129 | 			}
 130 | 		}
 131 | 
 132 | 		// Calculate doses based on patient weight and age
 133 | 		const calculatedDoses: Array<{
 134 | 			drugId: string;
 135 | 			drugName: string | undefined;
 136 | 			prescribedDose: number;
 137 | 			recommendedDose: number;
 138 | 			difference: number;
 139 | 			warning?: string;
 140 | 		}> = [];
 141 | 		for (const item of input.items) {
 142 | 			const guidelines = await context.db.query.doseGuideline.findMany({
 143 | 				where: {
 144 | 					drugId: item.drugId,
 145 | 					AND: [
 146 | 						{ postNatalAgeDaysMin: { lte: patientAgeInDays } },
 147 | 						{ postNatalAgeDaysMax: { gte: patientAgeInDays } }
 148 | 					]
 149 | 				}
 150 | 			});
 151 | 
 152 | 			if (guidelines.length > 0 && weight) {
 153 | 				const guideline = guidelines[0];
 154 | 				const calculatedDose = (guideline?.minDosePerKg ?? 0) * weight;
 155 | 				calculatedDoses.push({
 156 | 					drugId: item.drugId,
 157 | 					drugName: drugMap.get(item.drugId)?.name,
 158 | 					prescribedDose: item.dosageValue,
 159 | 					recommendedDose: calculatedDose,
 160 | 					difference: item.dosageValue - calculatedDose,
 161 | 					warning:
 162 | 						Math.abs(item.dosageValue - calculatedDose) > calculatedDose * 0.2
 163 | 							? "Dose deviates significantly from recommended range"
 164 | 							: undefined
 165 | 				});
 166 | 			}
 167 | 		}
 168 | 
 169 | 		// Create prescription
 170 | 		const newPrescription = await queries.pharmacy.createPrescription({
 171 | 			id: prescriptionId,
 172 | 			medicalRecordId: input.medicalRecordId,
 173 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 174 | 			doctorId: input.doctorId,
 175 | 			encounterId: input.encounterId,
 176 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 177 | 			instructions: input.notes,
 178 | 			endDate: input.validUntil ?? new Date(Date.now() + 90 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000),
 179 | 			status: "active",
 180 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
 181 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
 182 | 		});
 183 | 
 184 | 		// Create prescribed items
 185 | 		const prescribedItems = await Promise.all(
 186 | 			input.items.map(async item => {
 187 | 				return await queries.pharmacy.createPrescribedItems({
 188 | 					id: crypto.randomUUID(),
 189 | 					clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 190 | 					prescriptionId,
 191 | 					drugId: item.drugId,
 192 | 					dosageValue: item.dosageValue,
 193 | 					dosageUnit: item.dosageUnit,
 194 | 					frequency: item.frequency as Frequency,
 195 | 					duration: item.duration,
 196 | 					instructions: item.instructions ?? "",
 197 | 					drugRoute: item.drugRoute
 198 | 				});
 199 | 			})
 200 | 		);
 201 | 
 202 | 		// Log prescription creation
 203 | 		await queries.pharmacy.createPrescriptionLog({
 204 | 			id: generateId(),
 205 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
 206 | 			prescriptionId,
 207 | 			action: "created",
 208 | 			performedBy: context.user?.id ?? "system",
 209 | 			details: JSON.stringify({ interactions, calculatedDoses })
 210 | 		});
 211 | 
 212 | 		if (!newPrescription) {
 213 | 			throw new Error("Failed to create prescription");
 214 | 		}
 215 | 
 216 | 		return {
 217 | 			id: newPrescription.id,
 218 | 			medicalRecordId: newPrescription.medicalRecordId,
 219 | 			patientId: newPrescription.patientId,
 220 | 			doctorId: newPrescription.doctorId,
 221 | 			encounterId: newPrescription.encounterId,
 222 | 			clinicId: newPrescription.clinicId,
 223 | 			status: newPrescription.status,
 224 | 			items: prescribedItems
 225 | 				.filter((item): item is NonNullable<typeof item> => !!item)
 226 | 				.map(item => ({
 227 | 					id: item.id,
 228 | 					drugId: item.drugId,
 229 | 					dosageValue: item.dosageValue,
 230 | 					dosageUnit: item.dosageUnit,
 231 | 					frequency: item.frequency
 232 | 				})),
 233 | 			interactions,
 234 | 			doseCalculations: calculatedDoses,
 235 | 			warnings: calculatedDoses.map(d => d.warning).filter((w): w is string => !!w)
 236 | 		};
 237 | 	});

 243 | 		})
 244 | 	)

 288 | 		})

 300 | // Helper to enhance prescriptions with refill status
 301 | 
 302 | // Helper to enhance prescriptions with refill status
 303 | function enhancePrescriptionsWithRefillStatus(prescriptions: PrescriptionWithRelations[]): EnhancedPrescription[] {
 304 | 	const now = Date.now();
 305 | 
 306 | 	return prescriptions.map(prescription => {
 307 | 		return {
 308 | 			...prescription,
 309 | 			items: prescription.prescribedItems.map(item => {
 310 | 				const refillsRemaining = item.refillsRemaining ?? 0;
 311 | 				const daysSupply = calculateDaysSupply(item);
 312 | 				const refillInterval = calculateRefillInterval(item);
 313 | 
 314 | 				let isDueForRefill = false;
 315 | 				if (refillsRemaining > 0) {
 316 | 					if (item.lastRefillDate) {
 317 | 						const lastRefillTime = new Date(item.lastRefillDate).getTime();
 318 | 						isDueForRefill = lastRefillTime < now - refillInterval;
 319 | 					} else {
 320 | 						isDueForRefill = true;
 321 | 					}
 322 | 				}
 323 | 
 324 | 				return {
 325 | 					...item,
 326 | 					refillsRemaining,
 327 | 					daysSupply,
 328 | 					isDueForRefill
 329 | 				};
 330 | 			})
 331 | 		};
 332 | 	});
 333 | }

 586 | // Renew prescription
 587 | export const renewPrescription = protectedProcedure
 588 | 	.input(
 589 | 		z.object({
 590 | 			prescriptionId: z.string(),
 591 | 			renewForDays: z.number().default(30),
 592 | 			doctorNotes: z.string().optional()
 593 | 		})
 594 | 	)
 595 | 	.output(z.any())
 596 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 597 | 		// Get original prescription
 598 | 		const originalPrescription = await queries.pharmacy.getPrescriptionWithItems(
 599 | 			input.prescriptionId,
 600 | 			context.clinicId ?? undefined
 601 | 		);
 602 | 
 603 | 		if (!originalPrescription) {
 604 | 			throw new Error("Prescription not found");
 605 | 		}
 606 | 
 607 | 		// Create renewal prescription
 608 | 		const newPrescriptionId = crypto.randomUUID();
 609 | 		const newValidUntil = new Date();
 610 | 		newValidUntil.setDate(newValidUntil.getDate() + input.renewForDays);
 611 | 
 612 | 		const newPrescription = await queries.pharmacy.createPrescription({
 613 | 			id: newPrescriptionId,
 614 | 			medicalRecordId: originalPrescription.medicalRecordId,
 615 | 			patientId: originalPrescription.patientId,
 616 | 			doctorId: originalPrescription.doctorId,
 617 | 			encounterId: originalPrescription.encounterId,
 618 | 			clinicId: context.clinicId,
 619 | 			instructions: `Renewal of prescription ${originalPrescription.id}. ${input.doctorNotes ?? ""}`,
 620 | 			endDate: newValidUntil,
 621 | 			status: "active",
 622 | 			renewedFromId: originalPrescription.id
 623 | 		});
 624 | 
 625 | 		if (!newPrescription) {
 626 | 			throw new Error("Failed to create renewal prescription");
 627 | 		}
 628 | 
 629 | 		// Copy prescribed items with new refills
 630 | 		const newItems = await Promise.all(
 631 | 			originalPrescription.prescribedItems.map(async item => {
 632 | 				const newItem = await queries.pharmacy.createPrescribedItems({
 633 | 					id: generateId(),
 634 | 					clinicId: context.clinicId ?? "",
 635 | 					prescriptionId: newPrescriptionId,
 636 | 					drugId: item.drugId,
 637 | 					dosageValue: item.dosageValue,
 638 | 					dosageUnit: item.dosageUnit,
 639 | 					frequency: item.frequency,
 640 | 					duration: `${input.renewForDays} days`,
 641 | 					instructions: item.instructions,
 642 | 					drugRoute: item.drugRoute,
 643 | 					refillsRemaining: item.totalRefills,
 644 | 					totalRefills: item.totalRefills
 645 | 				});
 646 | 				return newItem;
 647 | 			})
 648 | 		);
 649 | 
 650 | 		return {
 651 | 			...newPrescription,
 652 | 			items: newItems,
 653 | 			originalPrescriptionId: originalPrescription.id
 654 | 		};
 655 | 	});

 657 | // Get medication adherence report
 658 | export const getMedicationAdherence = protectedProcedure
 659 | 	.input(
 660 | 		z.object({
 661 | 			patientId: z.string(),
 662 | 			startDate: z.date(),
 663 | 			endDate: z.date()
 664 | 		})
 665 | 	)
 666 | 	.output(z.any())
 667 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 668 | 		const prescriptions = await queries.pharmacy.getPrescriptionsByDateRange(
 669 | 			input.patientId,
 670 | 			input.startDate,
 671 | 			input.endDate
 672 | 		);
 673 | 
 674 | 		const adherenceData: Array<{
 675 | 			drugId: string;
 676 | 			drugName: string | undefined;
 677 | 			prescribedDosage: string;
 678 | 			expectedDoses: number;
 679 | 			adherenceRate: number;
 680 | 			status: string;
 681 | 			lastDispensed: Date | null | undefined;
 682 | 			refillsRemaining: number | null;
 683 | 		}> = [];
 684 | 		for (const prescription of prescriptions) {
 685 | 			for (const item of prescription.prescribedItems) {
 686 | 				const expectedDoses = calculateExpectedDoses(
 687 | 					item,
 688 | 					prescription.issuedDate,
 689 | 					prescription.endDate ?? new Date()
 690 | 				);
 691 | 
 692 | 				const dispensedDoses =
 693 | 					item.dispenses?.reduce(
 694 | 						(sum, dispense) => sum + dispense.quantityDispensed / (item.dosageValue || 1),
 695 | 						0
 696 | 					) || 0;
 697 | 
 698 | 				const adherenceRate = expectedDoses > 0 ? (dispensedDoses / expectedDoses) * 100 : 0;
 699 | 
 700 | 				adherenceData.push({
 701 | 					drugId: item.drugId,
 702 | 					drugName: item.drug?.name,
 703 | 					prescribedDosage: `${item.dosageValue} ${item.dosageUnit} ${item.frequency}`,
 704 | 					expectedDoses,
 705 | 					adherenceRate,
 706 | 					status: getAdherenceStatus(adherenceRate),
 707 | 					lastDispensed: item.lastRefillDate,
 708 | 					refillsRemaining: item.refillsRemaining
 709 | 				});
 710 | 			}
 711 | 		}
 712 | 
 713 | 		// const overallAdherence =
 714 | 		// adherenceData.reduce((sum, data) /=> sum + data.adherenceRate, 0) / adherenceData.length;
 715 | 
 716 | 		return {
 717 | 			patientId: input.patientId,
 718 | 			period: { startDate: input.startDate, endDate: input.endDate },
 719 | 			medications: adherenceData,
 720 | 			// overallAdherence,
 721 | 			// status: getAdherenceStatus(overallAdherence),
 722 | 			recommendations: generateAdherenceRecommendations(adherenceData)
 723 | 		};
 724 | 	});

 726 | // Drug interaction checker
 727 | export const checkDrugInteractions = protectedProcedure
 728 | 	.input(
 729 | 		z.object({
 730 | 			drugIds: z.array(z.string()),
 731 | 			patientId: z.string().optional()
 732 | 		})
 733 | 	)
 734 | 	.output(z.any())
 735 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 736 | 		const drugsData = await queries.pharmacy.getDrugsByIds(input.drugIds, context.clinicId ?? "");
 737 | 
 738 | 		const interactions: Array<{
 739 | 			severity: "moderate" | "high";
 740 | 			drugs: (string | null | undefined)[];
 741 | 			description: string;
 742 | 			recommendation: string;
 743 | 		}> = [];
 744 | 		const drugMap = new Map(drugsData.map(d => [d.id, d]));
 745 | 
 746 | 		// Check pairwise interactions
 747 | 		for (let i = 0; i < input.drugIds.length; i++) {
 748 | 			for (let j = i + 1; j < input.drugIds.length; j++) {
 749 | 				const drug1 = drugMap.get(input.drugIds[i] ?? "");
 750 | 				const drug2 = drugMap.get(input.drugIds[j] ?? "");
 751 | 
 752 | 				if (
 753 | 					drug1?.interactions?.includes(drug2?.name ?? "") ||
 754 | 					drug2?.interactions?.includes(drug1?.name ?? "")
 755 | 				) {
 756 | 					interactions.push({
 757 | 						severity: "moderate",
 758 | 						drugs: [drug1?.name, drug2?.name],
 759 | 						description: `Potential interaction between ${drug1?.name} and ${drug2?.name}`,
 760 | 						recommendation: "Monitor patient closely"
 761 | 					});
 762 | 				}
 763 | 			}
 764 | 		}
 765 | 
 766 | 		// Check patient allergies if patientId provided
 767 | 		let allergies: string[] = [];
 768 | 		if (input.patientId) {
 769 | 			const allergiesStr = await queries.pharmacy.getPatientAllergies(input.patientId);
 770 | 
 771 | 			if (allergiesStr) {
 772 | 				allergies = allergiesStr.split(",").map(a => a.trim());
 773 | 				for (const drug of drugsData) {
 774 | 					if (
 775 | 						allergies.some(
 776 | 							allergy =>
 777 | 								drug.name?.toLowerCase().includes(allergy.toLowerCase()) ||
 778 | 								drug.genericName?.toLowerCase().includes(allergy.toLowerCase())
 779 | 						)
 780 | 					) {
 781 | 						interactions.push({
 782 | 							severity: "high",
 783 | 							drugs: [drug.name],
 784 | 							description: `Patient has allergy to ${drug.name} or its class`,
 785 | 							recommendation: "Do not prescribe - alternative medication required"
 786 | 						});
 787 | 					}
 788 | 				}
 789 | 			}
 790 | 		}
 791 | 
 792 | 		return {
 793 | 			drugs: drugsData,
 794 | 			interactions,
 795 | 			hasSevereInteractions: interactions.some(i => i.severity === "high"),
 796 | 			recommendation:
 797 | 				interactions.length === 0
 798 | 					? "No significant interactions detected"
 799 | 					: "Consult drug interaction database before prescribing"
 800 | 		};
 801 | 	});

 809 | 		total: number;
 810 | 		hasMore: boolean;
 811 | 	};
 812 | };

 824 | 	.output(
 825 | 		z.object({
 826 | 			drugs: z.array(z.any()), // Replace z.any() with your actual Drug schema
 827 | 			pagination: z.object({
 828 | 				limit: z.number(),
 829 | 				offset: z.number(),
 830 | 				total: z.number(),
 831 | 				hasMore: z.boolean()
 832 | 			})
 833 | 		})
 834 | 	)
 835 | 	.handler(async ({ input }): Promise<ListDrugsResponse> => {
 836 | 		const { search, category, limit, offset } = input;
 837 | 
 838 | 		return await queries.pharmacy.listDrugs(search, category, limit, offset);
 839 | 	});
 840 | 
 841 | // Update prescription status
 842 | export const updatePrescription = protectedProcedure
 843 | 	.input(
 844 | 		z.object({
 845 | 			prescriptionId: z.string(),
 846 | 			status: z.enum(["active", "completed", "cancelled", "expired", "on_hold"]),
 847 | 			reason: z.string().optional()
 848 | 		})
 849 | 	)
 850 | 	.output(z.any())
 851 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 852 | 		const { prescriptionId, status, reason } = input;
 853 | 
 854 | 		const updated = await queries.pharmacy.updatePrescription(prescriptionId, {
 855 | 			status,
 856 | 			updatedAt: new Date(),
 857 | 			...(status === "cancelled" && {
 858 | 				cancelledAt: new Date(),
 859 | 				cancellationReason: reason
 860 | 			})
 861 | 		});
 862 | 
 863 | 		// Log status change
 864 | 		await queries.pharmacy.createPrescriptionLog({
 865 | 			id: crypto.randomUUID(),
 866 | 			prescriptionId,
 867 | 			action: `status_changed_to_${status}`,
 868 | 			performedBy: context.user?.id ?? "system",
 869 | 			details: reason ?? "",
 870 | 			createdAt: new Date()
 871 | 		});
 872 | 
 873 | 		return updated ?? undefined;
 874 | 	});
 875 | 
 876 | // Get prescription analytics
 877 | export const getPrescriptionAnalytics = protectedProcedure
 878 | 	.input(
 879 | 		z.object({
 880 | 			clinicId: z.string(),
 881 | 			startDate: z.date(),
 882 | 			endDate: z.date(),
 883 | 			groupBy: z.enum(["doctor", "drug", "month"]).default("month")
 884 | 		})
 885 | 	)
 886 | 	.output(z.any())
 887 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 888 | 		const prescriptions = await queries.pharmacy.getPrescriptionsForAnalytics(
 889 | 			input.clinicId,
 890 | 			input.startDate,
 891 | 			input.endDate
 892 | 		);
 893 | 
 894 | 		let analytics: unknown = null;
 895 | 
 896 | 		switch (input.groupBy) {
 897 | 			case "doctor":
 898 | 				analytics = groupByDoctor(prescriptions);
 899 | 				break;
 900 | 			case "drug":
 901 | 				analytics = groupByDrug(prescriptions);
 902 | 				break;
 903 | 			case "month":
 904 | 				analytics = groupByMonth(prescriptions);
 905 | 				break;
 906 | 			default:
 907 | 				analytics = {};
 908 | 				break;
 909 | 		}
 910 | 
 911 | 		return {
 912 | 			period: { startDate: input.startDate, endDate: input.endDate },
 913 | 			totalPrescriptions: prescriptions.length,
 914 | 			totalItems: prescriptions.reduce((sum: number, p) => sum + p.prescribedItems.length, 0),
 915 | 			activePrescriptions: prescriptions.filter(p => p.status === "active").length,
 916 | 			completionRate: (prescriptions.filter(p => p.status === "completed").length / prescriptions.length) * 100,
 917 | 			analytics
 918 | 		};
 919 | 	});
 920 | export const dispenseMedication = protectedProcedure
 921 | 	.input(
 922 | 		z.object({
 923 | 			prescribedItemId: z.string(),
 924 | 			quantity: z.number().min(1),
 925 | 			notes: z.string().optional()
 926 | 		})
 927 | 	)
 928 | 	.output(z.any())
 929 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 930 | 		const { prescribedItemId, quantity, notes } = input;
 931 | 
 932 | 		// 1. Get the prescribed item to check refills
 933 | 		const item = await context.db.query.prescribedItem.findFirst({
 934 | 			where: { id: prescribedItemId },
 935 | 			with: {
 936 | 				prescription: true,
 937 | 				dispenses: true
 938 | 			}
 939 | 		});
 940 | 
 941 | 		if (!item) throw new Error("Prescribed item not found");
 942 | 		if (item.refillsRemaining !== null && item.refillsRemaining <= 0) {
 943 | 			throw new Error("No refills remaining for this medication");
 944 | 		}
 945 | 
 946 | 		// 2. Create the dispense record
 947 | 		const dispense = await queries.pharmacy.createDispense({
 948 | 			id: generateId(),
 949 | 			prescriptionId: item.prescriptionId,
 950 | 			prescribedItemId,
 951 | 			quantityDispensed: quantity,
 952 | 			dispensedAt: new Date(),
 953 | 			dispensedBy: context.user?.id ?? "system",
 954 | 			notes: notes ?? ""
 955 | 		});
 956 | 
 957 | 		// 3. Decrement refills remaining
 958 | 		await queries.pharmacy.updatePrescribedItems(prescribedItemId, {
 959 | 			refillsRemaining: item.refillsRemaining ? item.refillsRemaining - 1 : 0,
 960 | 			lastRefillDate: new Date()
 961 | 		});
 962 | 
 963 | 		return { success: true, dispense };
 964 | 	});
 965 | 
 966 | export const prescriptionRouter = o.router({
 967 | 	list: listPatientActivePrescriptions,
 968 | 	create: createPrescription,
 969 | 	get: getPrescription,
 970 | 	getPatientActivePrescriptions,
 971 | 	dispenseMedication,
 972 | 	delete: deletePrescription,
 973 | 	renew: renewPrescription,
 974 | 	getMedicationAdherence,
 975 | 	checkDrugInteractions,
 976 | 	listDrugs,
 977 | 	update: updatePrescription,
 978 | 	getPrescriptionAnalytics
 979 | });

```

```ts
  24 | });

  86 | 			ageGroupFilter: z.string()
  87 | 		})
  88 | 	)

  92 | 			throw new Error("Clinic ID is required");
  93 | 		}

  96 | 		const endDate = new Date(input.endDate);
  97 | 
  98 | 		const report = await reportingRepo.getClinicalReport(clinicId, startDate, endDate, {
  99 | 			includeVitals: input.includeVitals,
 100 | 			includeDiagnoses: input.includeDiagnoses,
 101 | 			includeImmunizations: input.includeImmunizations,
 102 | 			includeGrowthData: input.includeGrowthData,
 103 | 			ageGroup: input.ageGroup
 104 | 		});
 105 | 
 106 | 		return {
 107 | 			period: { startDate, endDate },
 108 | 			summary: {
 109 | 				patientCount: report.totalPatients,
 110 | 				newPatientRate: report.totalPatients > 0 ? (report.newPatients / report.totalPatients) * 100 : 0,
 111 | 				appointmentCompletionRate: report.completionRate,
 112 | 				averagePatientsPerDay: report.averagePatientsPerDay,
 113 | 				immunizationCoverageRate: report.immunizationCoverageRate
 114 | 			},
 115 | 			diagnoses: {
 116 | 				total: report.topDiagnoses.reduce((sum, d) => sum + d.count, 0),
 117 | 				topDiagnoses: report.topDiagnoses.map(d => ({ name: d.diagnosis, count: d.count })),
 118 | 				byType: report.diagnosesByType
 119 | 			},
 120 | 			immunizations: input.includeImmunizations ? {
 121 | 				total: report.immunizationSummary.total,
 122 | 				byVaccine: report.immunizationSummary.byVaccine,
 123 | 				coverage: {
 124 | 					total: report.immunizationSummary.total,
 125 | 					byStatus: report.immunizationSummary.byStatus
 126 | 				}
 127 | 			} : null,
 128 | 			vitalSigns: input.includeVitals ? report.vitalSignsSummary : null,
 129 | 			growthData: input.includeGrowthData ? report.growthSummary : null,
 130 | 			ageGroupFilter: input.ageGroup
 131 | 		};
 132 | 	});
```

`routers/service.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { z } from "zod";
   2 | 
   3 | import { queries } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   4 | import { protectedProcedure } from "../index";
   5 | 
   6 | export const listServices = protectedProcedure
   7 | 	.input(
   8 | 		z.object({
   9 | 			search: z.string().optional(),
  10 | 			category: z.string().optional(),
  11 | 			page: z.number().int().min(1).default(1),
  12 | 			pageSize: z.number().int().min(1).max(100).default(50)
  13 | 		})
  14 | 	)
  15 | 	.output(
  16 | 		z.object({
  17 | 			services: z.array(z.any()),
  18 | 			total: z.number(),
  19 | 			page: z.number(),
  20 | 			totalPages: z.number()
  21 | 		})
  22 | 	)
  23 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  24 | 		const { search, category, page, pageSize } = input;
  25 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId ?? "";
  26 | 
  27 | 		return await queries.clinic.listServices({
  28 | 			clinicId,
  29 | 			search,
  30 | 			category,
  31 | 			page,
  32 | 			pageSize
  33 | 		});
  34 | 	});
  35 | 
  36 | export const getService = protectedProcedure
  37 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
  38 | 	.output(z.any())
  39 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  40 | 		const found = await queries.clinic.getServiceById(input.id, context.clinicId ?? undefined);
  41 | 
  42 | 		if (!found) {
  43 | 			throw new Error("Service not found");
  44 | 		}
  45 | 		return found;
  46 | 	});

```

`routers/sse.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { eventIterator, os } from "@orpc/server";
   2 | import * as z from "zod";
   3 | 
   4 | const MAX_EVENTS = 5;
   5 | 
   6 | export const sse = os
   7 | 	.route({
   8 | 		method: "GET",
   9 | 		path: "/sse",
  10 | 		tags: ["SSE"],
  11 | 		summary: "Server-Sent Events"
  12 | 	})
  13 | 	.output(eventIterator(z.object({ time: z.date() })))
  14 | 	.handler(async function* () {
  15 | 		let count = 0;
  16 | 
  17 | 		while (count < MAX_EVENTS) {
  18 | 			count++;
  19 | 			yield { time: new Date() };
  20 | 			await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
  21 | 		}
  22 | 	});

```

`routers/staff.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { ORPCError } from "@orpc/server";
   2 | import { z } from "zod";
   3 | 
   4 | import { queries, staffRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   5 | import { generateId } from '@clinic/db/utils/id';
   6 | import { clinicProcedure, protectedProcedure } from "../index";
   7 | 
   8 | // ============================================================
   9 | // Shared schemas
  10 | // ============================================================
  11 | 
  12 | const RoleEnum = z.enum(["admin", "doctor", "staff", "patient"]);
  13 | const StatusEnum = z.enum(["ACTIVE", "INACTIVE", "PENDING", "SUSPENDED"]);
  14 | 
  15 | // The DB statusEnum covers all entity types; staff only uses these four,
  16 | // but the column type is the full union so the output schema must accept all values.
  17 | const StaffStatusInputEnum = z.enum(["ACTIVE", "INACTIVE", "PENDING", "SUSPENDED"]);
  18 | const StaffStatusOutputEnum = z.enum([
  19 | 	"ACTIVE",
  20 | 	"INACTIVE",
  21 | 	"PENDING",
  22 | 	"SUSPENDED",
  23 | 	"COMPLETED",
  24 | 	"CANCELLED",
  25 | 	"EXPIRED",
  26 | 	"ON_HOLD"
  27 | ]);
  28 | 
  29 | const StaffOutputSchema = z.object({
  30 | 	id: z.string(),
  31 | 	name: z.string(),
  32 | 	email: z.string().nullable(),
  33 | 	phone: z.string().nullable(),
  34 | 	role: RoleEnum,
  35 | 	clinicId: z.string().nullable(),
  36 | 	department: z.string().nullable(),
  37 | 	address: z.string().nullable(),
  38 | 	img: z.string().nullable(),
  39 | 	colorCode: z.string().nullable(),
  40 | 	licenseNumber: z.string().nullable(),
  41 | 	hireDate: z.date().nullable(),
  42 | 	salary: z.number().nullable(),
  43 | 	status: StaffStatusOutputEnum.nullable(),
  44 | 	isActive: z.boolean().nullable(),
  45 | 	deletedAt: z.date().nullable(),
  46 | 	createdAt: z.date(),
  47 | 	updatedAt: z.date()
  48 | });
  49 | 
  50 | // ============================================================
  51 | // list — GET /staff
  52 | // ============================================================
  53 | 
  54 | export const list = clinicProcedure
  55 | 	.input(
  56 | 		z
  57 | 			.object({
  58 | 				page: z.number().int().min(1).default(1).optional(),
  59 | 				limit: z.number().int().min(1).max(100).default(20).optional(),
  60 | 				search: z.string().optional(),
  61 | 				role: RoleEnum.optional(),
  62 | 				status: StaffStatusInputEnum.optional()
  63 | 			})
  64 | 			.optional()
  65 | 	)
  66 | 	.output(
  67 | 		z.object({
  68 | 			items: z.array(StaffOutputSchema),
  69 | 			total: z.number(),
  70 | 			totalPages: z.number(),
  71 | 			onDutyToday: z.number(),
  72 | 			onLeave: z.number(),
  73 | 			departmentCount: z.number()
  74 | 		})
  75 | 	)
  76 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  77 | 		const clinicId = context.clinicId;
  78 | 
  79 | 		const result = await queries.staff.listStaff({
  80 | 			clinicId,
  81 | 			page: input?.page ?? 1,
  82 | 			limit: input?.limit ?? 20,
  83 | 			search: input?.search,
  84 | 			role: input?.role,
  85 | 			status: input?.status
  86 | 		});
  87 | 
  88 | 		// Derive summary stats from the full active list
  89 | 		const onDutyToday = result.staff.filter(s => s.status === "ACTIVE" && s.isActive).length;
  90 | 		const onLeave = result.staff.filter(s => s.status === "INACTIVE").length;
  91 | 		const departments = new Set(result.staff.map(s => s.department).filter(Boolean));
  92 | 
  93 | 		return {
  94 | 			items: result.staff,
  95 | 			total: result.total,
  96 | 			totalPages: result.totalPages,
  97 | 			onDutyToday,
  98 | 			onLeave,
  99 | 			departmentCount: departments.size
 100 | 		};
 101 | 	});
 102 | 
 103 | // ============================================================
 104 | // getById — GET /staff/:id
 105 | // ============================================================
 106 | 
 107 | export const getById = protectedProcedure
 108 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 109 | 	.output(StaffOutputSchema)
 110 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 111 | 		const clinicId = context.user?.clinicId ?? "";
 112 | 		const staff = await queries.staff.getStaffById(input.id, clinicId);
 113 | 		if (!staff) {
 114 | 			throw new ORPCError("NOT_FOUND", { message: "Staff member not found" });
 115 | 		}
 116 | 		return staff;
 117 | 	});
 118 | 
 119 | // ============================================================
 120 | // add — POST /staff
 121 | // ============================================================
 122 | 
 123 | export const add = protectedProcedure
 124 | 	.input(
 125 | 		z.object({
 126 | 			id: z.string().optional(),
 127 | 			name: z.string().min(1),
 128 | 			email: z.string().optional().nullable(),
 129 | 			phone: z.string().optional(),
 130 | 			role: RoleEnum.default("staff"),
 131 | 			department: z.string().optional(),
 132 | 			address: z.string().optional(),
 133 | 			img: z.string().optional(),
 134 | 			colorCode: z.string().optional(),
 135 | 			licenseNumber: z.string().optional(),
 136 | 			hireDate: z.date().optional(),
 137 | 			salary: z.number().min(0).optional(),
 138 | 			status: StatusEnum.default("ACTIVE"),
 139 | 			isActive: z.boolean().default(true),
 140 | 			userId: z.string().optional()
 141 | 		})
 142 | 	)
 143 | 	.output(StaffOutputSchema)
 144 | 	.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 145 | 		const clinicId = context.user?.clinicId ?? "";
 146 | 		const created = await staffRepo.createStaff({
 147 | 			...input,
 148 | 			id: input.id ?? generateId(),
 149 | 			clinicId,
 150 | 			address: input.address ?? ""
 151 | 		});
 152 | 
 153 | 		if (!created) {
 154 | 			throw new ORPCError("INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR", {
 155 | 				message: "Failed to create staff member"
 156 | 			});
 157 | 		}
 158 | 
 159 | 		return created;
 160 | 	});
 161 | 
 162 | // ============================================================
 163 | // update — PATCH /staff/:id
 164 | // ============================================================
 165 | 
 166 | export const update = protectedProcedure
 167 | 	.input(
 168 | 		z.object({
 169 | 			id: z.string(),
 170 | 			name: z.string().min(1).optional(),
 171 | 			email: z.string().optional().nullable(),
 172 | 			phone: z.string().optional(),
 173 | 			role: RoleEnum.optional(),
 174 | 			department: z.string().optional(),
 175 | 			address: z.string().optional(),
 176 | 			img: z.string().optional(),
 177 | 			colorCode: z.string().optional(),
 178 | 			licenseNumber: z.string().optional(),
 179 | 			hireDate: z.date().optional(),
 180 | 			salary: z.number().min(0).optional(),
 181 | 			status: StatusEnum.optional(),
 182 | 			isActive: z.boolean().optional()
 183 | 		})
 184 | 	)
 185 | 	.output(StaffOutputSchema)
 186 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 187 | 		const { id, ...data } = input;
 188 | 		const updated = await staffRepo.updateStaff(id, data);
 189 | 
 190 | 		if (!updated) {
 191 | 			throw new ORPCError("NOT_FOUND", { message: "Staff member not found" });
 192 | 		}
 193 | 
 194 | 		return updated;
 195 | 	});
 196 | 
 197 | // ============================================================
 198 | // remove — DELETE /staff/:id  (soft delete)
 199 | // ============================================================
 200 | 
 201 | export const remove = protectedProcedure
 202 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 203 | 	.output(z.object({ success: z.boolean() }))
 204 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 205 | 		await staffRepo.deleteStaff(input.id);
 206 | 		return { success: true };
 207 | 	});
 208 | 
 209 | // ============================================================
 210 | // restore — POST /staff/:id/restore
 211 | // ============================================================
 212 | 
 213 | export const restore = protectedProcedure
 214 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 215 | 	.output(StaffOutputSchema)
 216 | 	.handler(async ({ input }) => {
 217 | 		const restored = await  staffRepo.restoreStaff(input.id);
 218 | 		if (!restored) {
 219 | 			throw new ORPCError("NOT_FOUND", { message: "Staff member not found" });
 220 | 		}
 221 | 		return restored;
 222 | 	});
 223 | 
 224 | // ============================================================
 225 | // Router export
 226 | // ============================================================
 227 | 
 228 | export const staffRouter = {
 229 | 	list,
 230 | 	getById,
 231 | 	add,
 232 | 	update,
 233 | 	remove,
 234 | 	restore
 235 | };
```

```ts
   1 | import { os } from "@orpc/server";
   2 | import * as z from "zod";
   3 | 
   4 | const todos = [
   5 | 	{ id: 1, name: "Get groceries" },
   6 | 	{ id: 2, name: "Buy a new phone" },
   7 | 	{ id: 3, name: "Finish the project" }
   8 | ];
   9 | 
  10 | export const listTodos = os.input(z.object({})).handler(() => {
  11 | 	return todos;
  12 | });
  13 | 
  14 | export const addTodo = os.input(z.object({ name: z.string() })).handler(({ input }) => {
  15 | 	const newTodo = { id: todos.length + 1, name: input.name };
  16 | 	todos.push(newTodo);
  17 | 	return newTodo;
  18 | });
```

`routers/users.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { z } from "zod";
   2 | 
   3 | import {
   4 | 	createUserAction,
   5 | 	deleteUser,
   6 | 	getUserWithAllRelationsAction,
   7 | 	updateUserAction
   8 | } from "@clinic/db/actions/auth.actions";
   9 | import { queries } from "@clinic/db/queries";
  10 | import { UserCreateSchema, UserUpdateSchema } from "@clinic/db/zod";
  11 | 
  12 | import { adminProcedure, protectedProcedure } from "../index";
  13 | 
  14 | const userListFiltersSchema = z.object({
  15 | 	page: z.number().min(1).default(1),
  16 | 	limit: z.number().min(1).max(100).default(10),
  17 | 	search: z.string().optional(),
  18 | 	role: z.enum(["admin", "doctor", "patient", "staff"]).optional(),
  19 | 	clinicId: z.string().optional()
  20 | });
  21 | 
  22 | const createUserSchema = UserCreateSchema.extend({
  23 | 	password: z.string().min(6).optional()
  24 | });
  25 | 
  26 | const updateUserSchema = UserUpdateSchema.partial();
  27 | 
  28 | const bulkUserUpdateSchema = z.object({
  29 | 	ids: z.array(z.string()),
  30 | 	data: z.object({
  31 | 		role: z.enum(["admin", "doctor", "patient", "staff"]).optional(),
  32 | 		clinicId: z.string().optional(),
  33 | 		isActive: z.boolean().optional()
  34 | 	})
  35 | });
  36 | 
  37 | export const usersRouter = {
  38 | 	// List users with pagination and filters
  39 | 	list: protectedProcedure
  40 | 		.input(userListFiltersSchema)
  41 | 		.output(z.any())
  42 | 		.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  43 | 			// Check permissions
  44 | 			if (context.user?.role !== "admin" && context.user?.role !== "staff") {
  45 | 				throw new Error("Unauthorized: Only admins and staff can list users");
  46 | 			}
  47 | 
  48 | 			return await getUserWithAllRelationsAction(input.clinicId || context.clinicId || "");
  49 | 		}),
  50 | 
  51 | 	// Get user by ID
  52 | 	getById: protectedProcedure
  53 | 		.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
  54 | 		.output(z.any())
  55 | 		.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  56 | 			// Users can view their own profile, admins can view any
  57 | 			if (context.user?.id !== input.id && context.user?.role !== "admin") {
  58 | 				throw new Error("Unauthorized: You can only view your own profile");
  59 | 			}
  60 | 
  61 | 			return await getUserWithAllRelationsAction(input.id);
  62 | 		}),
  63 | 
  64 | 	// Create new user (admin only)
  65 | 	create: adminProcedure
  66 | 		.input(createUserSchema)
  67 | 		.output(z.any())
  68 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  69 | 			return await createUserAction(input);
  70 | 		}),
  71 | 
  72 | 	// Update user
  73 | 	update: protectedProcedure
  74 | 		.input(
  75 | 			z.object({
  76 | 				id: z.string(),
  77 | 				data: updateUserSchema
  78 | 			})
  79 | 		)
  80 | 		.output(z.any())
  81 | 		.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
  82 | 			// Users can update themselves, admins can update any
  83 | 			if (context.user?.id !== input.id && context.user?.role !== "admin") {
  84 | 				throw new Error("Unauthorized: You can only update your own profile");
  85 | 			}
  86 | 
  87 | 			return await updateUserAction(input.id, input.data);
  88 | 		}),
  89 | 
  90 | 	// Delete user (soft delete)
  91 | 	delete: adminProcedure
  92 | 		.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
  93 | 		.output(z.object({ success: z.boolean(), id: z.string() }))
  94 | 		.handler(async ({ input }) => {
  95 | 			await deleteUser(input.id);
  96 | 			return { success: true, id: input.id };
  97 | 		}),
  98 | 
  99 | 	// Get user statistics (admin only)
 100 | 	stats: adminProcedure.output(z.any()).handler(async ({ context }) => {
 101 | 		return await queries.clinic.getClinicDashboard(context.clinicId || "");
 102 | 	}),
 103 | 
 104 | 	// Get current user profile
 105 | 	me: protectedProcedure.output(z.any()).handler(async ({ context }) => {
 106 | 		const userData = await getUserWithAllRelationsAction(context.user?.id || "");
 107 | 		if (!userData) {
 108 | 			throw new Error("User not found");
 109 | 		}
 110 | 		return userData;
 111 | 	}),
 112 | 
 113 | 	// Update current user's own profile
 114 | 	updateMe: protectedProcedure
 115 | 		.input(updateUserSchema)
 116 | 		.output(z.any())
 117 | 		.handler(async ({ input, context }) => {
 118 | 			return await updateUserAction(context.user?.id || "", input);
 119 | 		})
 120 | };

```

`routers/vital-sign.server.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // routers/vital-signs.router.ts
   2 | import { startOfDay, subDays } from "date-fns";
   3 | import { z } from "zod";
   4 | 
   5 | import { medicalRepo } from "@clinic/db/queries";
   6 | import { VitalSignCreateSchema, VitalSignUpdateSchema } from "@clinic/db/zod";
   7 | import { protectedProcedure } from "../index";
   8 | 
   9 | // ============================================
  10 | // Schemas
  11 | // ============================================
  12 | 
  13 | const ListVitalSignsSchema = z.object({
  14 | 	patientId: z.string(),
  15 | 	page: z.number().int().min(1).default(1),
  16 | 	pageSize: z.number().int().min(1).max(100).default(20),
  17 | 	fromDate: z.date().optional(),
  18 | 	toDate: z.date().optional(),
  19 | 	encounterId: z.string().optional()
  20 | });
  21 | 
  22 | const VitalSignsTrendSchema = z.object({
  23 | 	patientId: z.string(),
  24 | 	days: z.number().int().min(1).max(365).default(30),
  25 | 	metrics: z
  26 | 		.array(z.enum(["temperature", "bloodPressure", "heartRate", "oxygen"]))
  27 | 		.default(["temperature", "heartRate", "oxygen"])
  28 | });
  29 | 
  30 | // ============================================
  31 | // Vital Signs Procedures
  32 | // ============================================
  33 | 
  34 | export const createVitalSigns = protectedProcedure.input(VitalSignCreateSchema).handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
  35 | 	const { clinicId, db } = context;
  36 | 
  37 | 	if (!clinicId) {
  38 | 		throw new Error("Clinic context missing");
  39 | 	}
  40 | 
  41 | 	console.info("Recording vital signs", {
  42 | 		patientId: input.patientId,
  43 | 		medicalId: input.medicalId
  44 | 	});
  45 | 
  46 | 	// Verify medical record exists using queries
  47 | 	const medicalRecordExists = await db.query.medicalRecord.findFirst({
  48 | 		where: {
  49 | 			id: input.medicalId,
  50 | 			clinicId,
  51 | 			isDeleted: false
  52 | 		}
  53 | 	});
  54 | 
  55 | 	if (!medicalRecordExists) {
  56 | 		throw new Error("Medical record not found");
  57 | 	}
  58 | 
  59 | 	// Verify patient exists using queries
  60 | 	const patientData = await db.query.patient.findFirst({
  61 | 		where: { id: input.patientId, clinicId, isDeleted: false }
  62 | 	});
  63 | 
  64 | 	if (!patientData) {
  65 | 		throw new Error("Patient not found");
  66 | 	}
  67 | 
  68 | 	// Check if vital signs already exist for this medical record
  69 | 	const existing = await db.query.vitalSign.findFirst({
  70 | 		where: { medicalId: input.medicalId, clinicId }
  71 | 	});
  72 | 
  73 | 	if (existing) {
  74 | 		throw new Error("Vital signs already recorded for this medical record");
  75 | 	}
  76 | 
  77 | 	// Use mutation to create vital signs
  78 | 	const vitalSignsRecord = await medicalRepo.createVitalSign({
  79 | 		...input,
  80 | 		id: crypto.randomUUID(),
  81 | 		clinicId: clinicId ?? "",
  82 | 		gender: input.gender ?? patientData.gender
  83 | 	});
  84 | 
  85 | 	// Update medical record using mutation
  86 | 	if (vitalSignsRecord) {
  87 | 		await medicalRepo.updateMedicalRecord(input.medicalId, {
  88 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
  89 | 		});
  90 | 	}
  91 | 
  92 | 	console.info("Vital signs recorded successfully", {
  93 | 		vitalSignsId: vitalSignsRecord?.id ?? ""
  94 | 	});
  95 | 
  96 | 	// Fetch the complete record using queries
  97 | 	const completeRecord = await medicalRepo.getVitalSignById(vitalSignsRecord?.id ?? "", clinicId);
  98 | 
  99 | 	return completeRecord;
 100 | });
 101 | 
 102 | export const getPatientHistory = protectedProcedure
 103 | 	.input(z.object({ patientId: z.string() }))
 104 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 105 | 		const { clinicId, db } = context;
 106 | 		const { patientId } = input;
 107 | 
 108 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 109 | 			throw new Error("Clinic context missing");
 110 | 		}
 111 | 
 112 | 		// Use queries to get patient history
 113 | 		const history = await db.query.vitalSign.findMany({
 114 | 			where: { patientId, clinicId },
 115 | 			with: {
 116 | 				medical: {
 117 | 					columns: {
 118 | 						id: true,
 119 | 						createdAt: true
 120 | 					}
 121 | 				},
 122 | 				encounter: {
 123 | 					columns: {
 124 | 						id: true,
 125 | 						diagnosis: true
 126 | 					}
 127 | 				}
 128 | 			},
 129 | 			orderBy: { recordedAt: "desc" }
 130 | 		});
 131 | 
 132 | 		const chartData = await db.query.vitalSign.findMany({
 133 | 			where: { patientId, clinicId },
 134 | 			orderBy: { recordedAt: "asc" },
 135 | 			limit: 50
 136 | 		});
 137 | 
 138 | 		return { history, chartData };
 139 | 	});
 140 | 
 141 | export const updateVitalSigns = protectedProcedure.input(VitalSignUpdateSchema).handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 142 | 	const { clinicId } = context;
 143 | 	const { id, ...updateData } = input;
 144 | 
 145 | 	if (!clinicId) {
 146 | 		throw new Error("Clinic context missing");
 147 | 	}
 148 | 
 149 | 	console.info("Updating vital signs", { vitalSignsId: id });
 150 | 
 151 | 	// Verify existence using queries
 152 | 	const existing = await medicalRepo.getVitalSignById(id as string, clinicId);
 153 | 
 154 | 	if (!existing) {
 155 | 		throw new Error("Vital signs not found");
 156 | 	}
 157 | 
 158 | 	// Use mutation to update
 159 | 	const updated = await medicalRepo.updateVitalSign(id as string, updateData);
 160 | 
 161 | 	console.info("Vital signs updated", { vitalSignsId: id });
 162 | 	return updated;
 163 | });
 164 | 
 165 | export const getVitalSignsById = protectedProcedure
 166 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
 167 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 168 | 		const { clinicId } = context;
 169 | 		const { id } = input;
 170 | 
 171 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 172 | 			throw new Error("Clinic context missing");
 173 | 		}
 174 | 
 175 | 		const vitalSignsRecord = await medicalRepo.getVitalSignById(id, clinicId);
 176 | 
 177 | 		if (!vitalSignsRecord) {
 178 | 			throw new Error("Vital signs not found");
 179 | 		}
 180 | 
 181 | 		console.debug("Retrieved vital signs", { vitalSignsId: id });
 182 | 		return vitalSignsRecord;
 183 | 	});
 184 | 
 185 | export const listVitalSignsByPatient = protectedProcedure
 186 | 	.input(ListVitalSignsSchema)
 187 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 188 | 		const { clinicId, user } = context;
 189 | 		const { patientId, page, pageSize, fromDate, toDate } = input;
 190 | 
 191 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 192 | 			throw new Error("Clinic context missing");
 193 | 		}
 194 | 
 195 | 		console.debug("Listing vital signs", { patientId, page, pageSize });
 196 | 
 197 | 		// Use the checkVitalSignsAccess from queries
 198 | 		const hasAccess = await medicalRepo.checkVitalSignsAccess(user?.id ?? "", patientId);
 199 | 		if (!hasAccess && user?.role !== "admin" && user?.role !== "staff") {
 200 | 			throw new Error("You don't have access to this patient's vital signs");
 201 | 		}
 202 | 
 203 | 		const vitalSignsList = await medicalRepo.listVitalSignsByPatient(
 204 | 			patientId,
 205 | 			context.clinicId ?? "",
 206 | 			fromDate ?? subDays(new Date(), 30),
 207 | 			toDate ?? new Date(),
 208 | 			pageSize,
 209 | 			page
 210 | 		);
 211 | 
 212 | 		const total = vitalSignsList.length;
 213 | 
 214 | 		return {
 215 | 			vitalSigns: vitalSignsList,
 216 | 			pagination: {
 217 | 				page,
 218 | 				pageSize,
 219 | 				total,
 220 | 				totalPages: Math.ceil(total / pageSize)
 221 | 			}
 222 | 		};
 223 | 	});
 224 | 
 225 | export const getLatestVitalSigns = protectedProcedure
 226 | 	.input(z.object({ patientId: z.string(), limit: z.number().default(1) }))
 227 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 228 | 		const { clinicId } = context;
 229 | 		const { patientId } = input;
 230 | 
 231 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 232 | 			throw new Error("Clinic context missing");
 233 | 		}
 234 | 
 235 | 		const latestVitalSigns = await medicalRepo.getLatestVitalSigns(patientId, clinicId);
 236 | 
 237 | 		return latestVitalSigns ?? null;
 238 | 	});
 239 | 
 240 | export const getVitalSignsTrend = protectedProcedure
 241 | 	.input(VitalSignsTrendSchema)
 242 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 243 | 		const { clinicId } = context;
 244 | 		const { patientId, days, metrics } = input;
 245 | 
 246 | 		const startDate = startOfDay(subDays(new Date(), days));
 247 | 
 248 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 249 | 			throw new Error("Clinic context missing");
 250 | 		}
 251 | 
 252 | 		console.debug("Getting vital signs trend", { patientId, days, metrics });
 253 | 
 254 | 		const vitalSignsList = await medicalRepo.listVitalSignsByPatient(
 255 | 			patientId,
 256 | 			context.clinicId ?? "",
 257 | 			startDate,
 258 | 			new Date(),
 259 | 			10,
 260 | 			1
 261 | 		);
 262 | 
 263 | 		const trend: {
 264 | 			dates: string[];
 265 | 			temperature: Array<{ value: number; date: string }>;
 266 | 			bloodPressure: Array<{
 267 | 				systolic: number;
 268 | 				diastolic: number;
 269 | 				date: string;
 270 | 			}>;
 271 | 			heartRate: Array<{ value: number; date: string }>;
 272 | 			oxygen: Array<{ value: number; date: string }>;
 273 | 		} = {
 274 | 			dates: [],
 275 | 			temperature: [],
 276 | 			bloodPressure: [],
 277 | 			heartRate: [],
 278 | 			oxygen: []
 279 | 		};
 280 | 
 281 | 		for (const vs of vitalSignsList) {
 282 | 			const date = vs.recordedAt.toISOString();
 283 | 			trend.dates.push(date);
 284 | 
 285 | 			if (metrics.includes("temperature") && vs.bodyTemperature) {
 286 | 				trend.temperature.push({ value: vs.bodyTemperature, date });
 287 | 			}
 288 | 
 289 | 			if (metrics.includes("bloodPressure") && vs.systolic && vs.diastolic) {
 290 | 				trend.bloodPressure.push({
 291 | 					systolic: vs.systolic,
 292 | 					diastolic: vs.diastolic,
 293 | 					date
 294 | 				});
 295 | 			}
 296 | 
 297 | 			if (metrics.includes("heartRate") && vs.heartRate) {
 298 | 				trend.heartRate.push({ value: vs.heartRate, date });
 299 | 			}
 300 | 
 301 | 			if (metrics.includes("oxygen") && vs.oxygenSaturation) {
 302 | 				trend.oxygen.push({ value: vs.oxygenSaturation, date });
 303 | 			}
 304 | 		}
 305 | 
 306 | 		// Calculate summary statistics
 307 | 		const summary = {
 308 | 			temperature: calculateSummary(trend.temperature.map(t => t.value)),
 309 | 			heartRate: calculateSummary(trend.heartRate.map(h => h.value)),
 310 | 			oxygenSaturation: calculateSummary(trend.oxygen.map(o => o.value))
 311 | 		};
 312 | 
 313 | 		return {
 314 | 			patientId,
 315 | 			period: { days, startDate, endDate: new Date() },
 316 | 			trend,
 317 | 			summary,
 318 | 			totalReadings: vitalSignsList.length
 319 | 		};
 320 | 	});
 321 | 
 322 | export const deleteVitalSigns = protectedProcedure
 323 | 	.input(z.object({ id: z.string(), reason: z.string().optional() }))
 324 | 	.handler(async ({ context, input }) => {
 325 | 		const { clinicId } = context;
 326 | 		const { id, reason } = input;
 327 | 
 328 | 		if (!clinicId) {
 329 | 			throw new Error("Clinic context missing");
 330 | 		}
 331 | 
 332 | 		console.warn("Deleting vital signs", { vitalSignsId: id, reason });
 333 | 
 334 | 		// Verify existence using queries
 335 | 		const existing = await medicalRepo.getVitalSignById(id, clinicId);
 336 | 
 337 | 		if (!existing) {
 338 | 			throw new Error("Vital signs not found");
 339 | 		}
 340 | 
 341 | 		// Use mutation to delete
 342 | 		const result = await medicalRepo.deleteVitalSign(id);
 343 | 
 344 | 		return {
 345 | 			success: true,
 346 | 			message: "Vital signs deleted successfully",
 347 | 			result
 348 | 		};
 349 | 	});
 350 | 
 351 | // ============================================
 352 | // Helper Functions
 353 | // ============================================
 354 | 
 355 | function calculateSummary(values: number[]): {
 356 | 	min: number | null;
 357 | 	max: number | null;
 358 | 	avg: number | null;
 359 | 	latest: number | null;
 360 | } {
 361 | 	if (values.length === 0) {
 362 | 		return { min: null, max: null, avg: null, latest: null };
 363 | 	}
 364 | 	return {
 365 | 		min: Math.min(...values),
 366 | 		max: Math.max(...values),
 367 | 		avg: values.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / values.length,
 368 | 		latest: values.at(-1) ?? 0
 369 | 	};
 370 | }

```
